[\[1a\]]
[\[1a.1\]{D4020}]@#/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa bzhugs so/_/
[\[1b\]]
[\[1b.1\]]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_ma hA yA na sU tra a laM ka ra nA ma kA ri kA/_bod skad du/_theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa/_sangs rgyas dang
[\[1b.2\]]byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/_/don shes don ston rab tu byed pa ngag dang tshig rnams dri med pas/_/sdug bsngal bsgral phyir de yi bdag nyid sdug bsngal
[\[1b.3\]]'gro la snying rje las/_/theg mchog bstan pa'i rnam pa chos kyi de yis 'gro ba'i sems can la/_/'byor pa'i don tshul bla med gyur pa rnam lnga'i bdag nyid ston par byed/_/
[\[1b.4\]]gser las brdungs byas 'dra zhing pad+ma rgyas pa bzhin/_/bkres pas nyen pa g.yos legs kha zas za ba 'dra/_/'phrin yig legs pa thos 'dra rin chen sgrom phye lta'i/_/
[\[1b.5\]]chos de 'dir bshad pa yang dga' ba'i mchog skyed do/_/gzugs rgyan rang bzhin yon tan ldan pa me long nang song na/_/mthong ba'i dbang gis mi rnams rab tu dga' ba'i
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]mchog skyed pa/_/de bzhin legs gsungs rtag tu rang bzhin yon tan ldan pa yi/_/chos kyang don rnams phye bas mkhas rnams 'di na dga' mchog skyed/_/ji ltar mnams na rab dku
[\[2a.2\]]la/_/myangs na zhim pa'i sman bzhin du/_/chos kyang de bzhin gnyis su gnas/_/don dang yi ger shes par bya/_/chos dka' rgya chen zab mo 'di/_/rgyal po bzhin du mnyes par dka'/_/mnyes par byas
[\[2a.3\]]na de bzhin du/_/yon tan mchog gi nor sbyin byed/_/rin chen rigs ldan rin thang med/_/lta mi shes pa'i mig mi mgu/_/de bzhin mi mkhas chos 'di la/_/bzlog na de bzhin mgu bar 'gyur/_/theg pa
[\[2a.4\]]chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las le'u dang po'o//_//sngar lung ma bstan lhan cig byung /_/spyod yul ma yin grub pa dang /_/yod dang med na yod med dang /_/gnyen po dang ni sgra gzhan phyir/_/sangs rgyas
[\[2a.5\]]rnams ni mngon sum spyan/_/bstan pa dag kyang srung bar mdzad/_/dus la'ang ye shes ma bsgribs pas/_/de phyir btang snyoms mi rung ngo /_/ma tshang ba dang 'gal ba dang /_/thabs min de ltar ma bstan phyir/_/
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]nyan thos kyi ni theg pa 'di/_/theg chen chos shes bya ba min/_/bsam pa dang ni bstan pa dang /_/sbyor ba dang ni rton pa dang /_/dus 'gal phyir na dman pa gang /_/de ni dman pa kho na yin/_/rang gi nyid la 'jug pa dang /_/rang gi 'dul la'ang snang phyir dang /_/
[\[2b.2\]]zab pa'i phyir dang rgya che'i phyir/_/chos nyid dang ni 'gal ba med/_/rtog ge rten cing ma nges la/_/ma khyab kun rdzob skyo ba can/_/byis pa la ni rten par 'dod/_/de phyir de ni de yul min/_/rgya che'i phyir dang zab pa'i phyir/_/yongs su smin dang rnam mi rtog_/_
[\[2b.3\]]de phyir 'di las gnyis bstan te/_/de ni bla na med pa'i thabs/_/'gro ba de'i gnas min la skrag pa gdung byed 'gyur/_/bsod nams ma yin phung chen bsags byas yun ring du/_/rigs med grogs ngan sngon dge ma bsags blo ma sbyangs/_/chos
[\[2b.4\]]'dis skrag 'gyur 'di na don chen 'di las ltung /_/de las gzhan dang gzhan med shin tu zab cing rjes song phyir/_/sna tshogs ston cing mang po'i sgo nas rtag tu ston dang ldan/_/ji skad bshad bzhin don min bcom ldan dgongs pa shin tu zab/_/mkhas
[\[2b.5\]]pa rnams kyis tshul bzhin brtags na chos 'dis skrag mi 'gyur/_/'di na dang por thos la brtan nas yid la byed pa 'byung /_/tshul bzhin yid la byed las yang dag don yul ye shes 'byung /_/de las chos thob de yod de las blo gros rab tu
[\[2b.6\]]skye/_/gang tshe de ni so so rang rig med na ji ltar nges/_/bdag gis mi shes sangs rgyas zab mo mkhyen ma yin/_/zab mo ci yi phyir na rtog ge'i yul ma yin/_/ci phyir zab mo'i don rig pa dag thar 'gyur zhes/_/bya ba de ni skrag pa'i gnas su rigs
[\[2b.7\]]ma yin/_/dman par mos shing khams kyang shin tu dman/_/grogs po dman pa dag gis yongs bskor ba/_/zab cing rgya che legs par bshad pa'i chos/_/'di la gal te mos med grub pa yin/_/thos rjes 'brangs te blo ldan thob nas ni/_/
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]gang zhig thos la rab tu gnas byed pa/_/rnam pa sna tshogs dpag tu med lus la/_/rmongs pa gang gi phyir na nges par byed/_/don sgra ji bzhin yongs rtog na/_/bdag nyid snyems shing blo nyams 'gyur/_/legs par gsungs
[\[3a.2\]]pa'ang spangs pas na/_/brlag 'gyur chos la khong khro sgrib/_/yid kyi nyes pa rang bzhin gdug pa ste/_/mi rigs pa yi gzugs la'ang mi rigs na/_/the tshom za ba'i chos la smos ci dgos/_/de phyir btang snyoms gzhag legs nyes pa med/_/theg pa
[\[3a.3\]]chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las theg pa chen po sgrub pa'i skabs kyi le'u ste gnyis pa'o//_//kun du 'gro dang khas len rtogs dang zil gnon par/_/dbye ba'i rang bzhin don rnam bzhi yi khyad par gyis/_/theg pa mchog phyir dkon mchog skyabs rab
[\[3a.4\]]song ba gang /_/de ni skyabs su song ba rnams kyi mchog ces bya/_/gang phyir dang por nges par bya ba 'di dka' ste/_/de ni bskal pa stong phrag du mar bsgrub par dka'/_/gang phyir grub na sems can phan byed don che ste/_/de phyir theg chen 'di la skyabs don
[\[3a.5\]]mchog yin no/_/gang zhig sems can thams cad bsgral bar zhugs pa dang /_/theg pa ye shes kun tu 'gro la mkhas par ldan/_/gang zhig mya ngan 'das la 'khor zhi ro gcig pa/_/de 'dra'i blo ldan de 'dir kun 'gror shes par bya/_/gang zhig
[\[3a.6\]]dga' ba mang pos byang chub mchog don gnyer/_/gang zhig skyo ba med par dka' ba yang dag spyod/_/gang zhig rnam sangs rgyas nas sangs rgyas kun mnyam 'gyur/_/blo ldan de ni khas len mchog tu shes par bya/_/sangs rgyas sras kyi mchog tu legs
[\[3a.7\]]par gang skyes pa/_/sems dang shes rab dang ni tshogs ldan snying rje ni/_/sa bon ma dang mngal gnas ma ma mtshungs pa med/_/blo ldan de ni khas len mchog tu shes par bya/_/sna tshogs mtshan rnams kun gyis de'i lus brgyan/_/sems can thams
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]cad smin par byed stobs thob/_/sangs rgyas bde chen mtha' yas zhi ba rnyed/_/sems can kun skyabs thabs chen bsham pa shes/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis 'od zer chen pos dbang bskur byin/_/de ni chos la dbang ba kun dang yang dag ldan/_/sangs
[\[3b.2\]]rgyas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor ston pa'i rnam pa shes/_/bslab pa bca' bas tshar gcod phan 'dogs byed la brtson/_/blon po chen po lta bur pha rol phyin la 'jug pa'i phyir/_/byang chub chen po'i phyogs mthun bdal la rtag tu spyan byed phyir/_/gsang
[\[3b.3\]]ba'i gnas ni rnam gsum rtag tu yang dag 'dzin pa'i phyir/_/sems can mang don rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par rab byed phyir/_/bsod nams phung chen srid gsum bla ma srid pa'i bde ba dang /_/sdug bsngal phung po chen po rab zhi blo mchog bde ba dang /_/
[\[3b.4\]]chos mang phung po mchog rab rtag pa'i sku ste dge ba'i tshogs/_/bag chags bzlog cing srid dang zhi las rnam par grol ba 'thob/_/blo ldan nyan thos tshogs bcas dge ba rgya chen don chen dang /_/mtha' yas rtag rgyun mi 'chad zad mi shes pas zil gyis gnon/_/
[\[3b.5\]]dge ba de yang 'jig rten 'jig rten ma yin yongs smin byed/_/dbang 'byor rnyed pa de ni phung po zhi bas zad mi shes/_/'di ni de dngos 'dod pas khas len de yang snying brtse las rig bya/_/de las rnam pa kun mkhyen phan dang bde byed dka' la skyo ba med/_/
[\[3b.6\]]nges par 'byung la theg pa kun gyis rton pa'i yon tan rtag tu ldan/_/brda dang chos nyid thob pa blo ldan rnams kyi skyabs 'gro 'di mchog yin/_/skyabs su 'gro ba 'dir song don chen te/_/de ni dpag med yon tan tshogs 'phel 'gyur/_/'gro ba 'di
[\[3b.7\]]la snying rje'i bsam pas khyab/_/mtshungs med 'phags chen chos kyang rgyas par byed/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las skyabs su 'gro ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o//_//yod dang mchog dang mtshan nyid dang /_/rtags dang rigs rab dbye ba
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]dang /_/nyes dmigs dang ni phan yon dang /_/dpe rnam gnyis te rnam pa bzhi/_/khams rnams dang ni mos pa dang /_/sgrub pa tha dad dbye ba dang /_/'bras bu tha dad dmigs pa'i phyir/_/rigs yod nyid du nges par brjod/_/de dge
[\[4a.2\]]khyad par 'phags pa dang /_/thams cad dang ni don chen dang /_/mi zad pa yi rgyu mtshan phyir/_/rigs mchog nyid ces brjod pa yin/_/rang bzhin dang ni rgyas pa dang /_/de ni rten dang brten pa dang /_/yod med nyid dang yon tan ni/_/sgrol ba'i don du shes
[\[4a.3\]]par bya/_/sbyor ba'i sngon du snying rje dang /_/mos pa dang ni bzod pa dang /_/dge ba yang dag spyod pa ni/_/rigs kyi rtags su nges par bshad/_/rigs ni nges dang ma nges dang /_/rkyen rnams kyis ni mi 'phrogs dang /_/'phrogs pa nyid de mdor na rigs/_/
[\[4a.4\]]dbye ba 'di ni rnam pa bzhi/_/nyon mongs goms dang grogs ngan dang /_/'phongs dang gzhan gyi dbang nyid dang /_/mdor na rigs kyi nyes dmigs ni/_/rnam pa bzhi ru shes par bya/_/ring mo zhig na ngan song du/_/'gro zhing myur du thar pa dang /_/de na'ang
[\[4a.5\]]sdug bsngal chung ngu myong /_/skyo bcas sems can smin par byed/_/gser gyi rigs bzhin shes par bya/_/dge ba dpag tu med pa'i gnas/_/ye shes dang ni dri med ldan/_/mthu rnams kyi yang gnas yin no/_/rin chen mchog rigs bzhin shes bya/_/
[\[4a.6\]]byang chub chen po'i rgyu mtshan phyir/_/ye shes che dang ting 'dzin 'phags/_/sems can mang po'i don gnas phyir/_/la la gcig tu nyes par spyod nges yod/_/la la dkar po'i chos rnams kun du bcom/_/la la thar pa'i cha mthun dge ba med/_/dkar po
[\[4a.7\]]dman pa yod pa rgyu dang bral/_/zab cing rgya che bshad pa gzhan la phan phyir bstan pa'i chos chen la/_/mi shes bzhin du mos pa shin tu rgya chen 'byung zhing sgrub la bzod/_/de dag tha mar rnam pa gnyis mchog phun sum tshogs 'gyur gang yin de/_/byang chub
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]sems dpa' rang bzhin yon tan ldan de rgyas pa'i rigs las shes/_/yon tan shin tu rgya che byang chub shing skyed phyir/_/bde dang sdug bsngal chen po zhi ba thob bya'i phyir/_/bdag dang gzhan la phan bde byed pa 'bras bu'i phyir/_/rigs mchog de ni rtsa ba bzang po
[\[4b.2\]]lta bu yin/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_rigs kyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o//_//spro ba che dang rtsom pa che/_/don che ba dang 'byung ba che/_/byang chub sems dpa'i sems dpa' ste/_/don gnyis ldan pa'i sems 'byung ba/_/sems bskyed de ni
[\[4b.3\]]sa rnams la/_/mos dang lhag bsam dag pa dang /_/rnam par smin pa gzhan du 'dod/_/de bzhin sgrib pa spangs pa'o/_/de yi rtsa ba snying rjer 'dod/_/rtag tu sems can phan par sems/_/chos la mos dang de bzhin de'i/_/ye shes tshol ba dmigs
[\[4b.4\]]pa'o/_/gong du 'dun pa 'gro ba ste/_/sdom pa rgya chen de yi rten/_/lam 'gog pa ni mi mthun phyogs/_/slong zhing dang du len pa'o/_/bsod nams ye shes rang bzhin gyi/_/dge ba 'phel ba de'i phan yon/_/pha rol phyin la rtag sbyor ba/_/de ni nges par
[\[4b.5\]]'byung bar 'dod/_/'di yi mthar thug sa yin te/_/so so rang gi der sbyor bas/_/byang chub sems dpa'i sems bskyed pa/_/rnam par nges par shes par bya/_/grogs stobs rgyu stobs rtsa ba'i stobs/_/thos stobs dge ba goms pa las/_/
[\[4b.6\]]mi brtan pa dang brtan 'byung ba/_/gzhan gyis bstan pa'i sems bskyed bshad/_/rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rab bsnyen byas/_/bsod nams ye shes tshogs rab bsags/_/chos la mi rtog ye shes ni/_/skyes phyir de ni dam par 'dod/_/chos
[\[4b.7\]]dang sems can rnams dang ni/_/de yi bya ba sangs rgyas nyid/_/mchog la sems mnyam rnyed pa'i phyir/_/de yi rab dga' khyad par 'phags/_/skye ba rgya chen de la spro/_/bsam pa yang ni dag pa dang /_/lhag ma dag la mkhas pa dang /_/nges par 'byung
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]bar shes par bya/_/chos la mos pa sa bon dang /_/pha rol phyin mchog ma las skyes/_/bsam gtan las byung bde ba mngal/_/snying rje skyed pa'i ma ma 'o/_/smon lam chen po bcu sgrub phyir/_/rgya che bar ni shes par bya/_/dka' ba yun
[\[5a.2\]]ring mi skyo'i phyir/_/spro bar khong du chud par bya/_/byang chub nye bar rtogs pa dang /_/de yi thabs shes rnyed pa'i phyir/_/bsam pa dag par shes par bya/_/sa gzhan tshul la mkhas pa nyid/_/ji ltar rnam gzhag yid byed pas/_/de rtog nyid du shes phyir dang /_/
[\[5a.3\]]de nyid la yang mi rtog phyir/_/nges par 'byung bar shes par bya/_/skyed pa sa dang mtshungs pa ste/_/gzhan ni bzang po'i gser dang 'dra/_/zla ba yar gyi tshes pa bzhin/_/gzhan ni me dang 'drar shes bya/_/gzhan ni gter chen bzhin shes bya/_/gzhan ni rin
[\[5a.4\]]chen 'byung gnas bzhin/_/rgya mtsho 'dra bar shes bya gzhan/_/rdo rje dang 'dra ri rab 'dra/_/sman gyi rgyal po 'dra ba ste/_/gzhan ni mdza' chen 'drar shes bya/_/yid bzhin nor bu 'dra ba dang /_/gzhan ni nyi ma 'drar shes bya/_/gzhan ni dri za'i dbyangs snyan
[\[5a.5\]]bzhin/_/gzhan ni rgyal po 'drar shes bya/_/de bzhin gzhan ni mdzod lta bu/_/lam po che dang 'drar shes bya/_/theg pa 'dra bar shes bya ste/_/sems bskyed bkod ma 'dra ba yin/_/kun dga'i sgra dang 'dra ba ste/_/klung chen rgyun dang 'dra ba'o/_/rgyal sras
[\[5a.6\]]rnams kyi sems bskyed pa/_/sprin dang 'dra bar bstan pa ste/_/de phyir de ltar yon tan phyug_/sems ni dga' bas yang dag bskyed/_/cher 'os sems bskyed spangs pa'i skye bo dag_/gzhan don sems dang de yi thabs rnyed dang /_/dgongs chen don dang
[\[5a.7\]]de nyid mchog mthong bas/_/bde ba de spangs zhi bar 'gro bar 'gyur/_/blo ldan sems mchog skyes ma thag tu yang /_/mtha' yas nyes pa byed las sems rab bsdams/_/gnyis 'phel byed pas rtag tu dge ba dang /_/brtse ldan bde dang sdug bsngal
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]dag gis dga'/_/gang tshe gzhan gyi don phyir lus dang ni/_/srog la mi lta rab dal khas len pa/_/de lta bu de gzhan gyi gnod pa yis/_/ji ltar ngan par byed pa'i las la 'jug_/de yis chos kun sgyu ma lta bu dang /_/skye ba skyed mos tshal 'gro
[\[5b.2\]]ltar rtogs nas/_/'byor ba'i dus dang rgud pa'i dus na'ang 'di/_/nyon mongs sdug bsngal dag gis 'jigs pa med/_/rang gi yon tan sems can phan 'dogs dga'/_/bsams bzhin skye ba rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul/_/rgyan dang ston mo sa mchog
[\[5b.3\]]brtse dga' ba/_/snying rje'i bdag nyid min pa rnams la med/_/gzhan don brtson ldan snying rje'i bdag nyid 'di/_/gang tshe mnar med pa la'ang dgar 'dzin pa/_/de 'dra ba dag srid na gzhan rten phyir/_/sdug bsngal 'byung ba rnams kyis ga la 'jigs/_
[\[5b.4\]]slob dpon brtse chen rtag tu brten pa'i bdag_/pha rol sdug bsngal dag gis sems gdungs pa/_/gzhan gyi bya ba nye bar gnas pa la/_/gzhan gyis bskul ba shin tu ngo yang tsha/_/mgo la sems can khur chen khyer ba yi/_/sems can mchog ni dal
[\[5b.5\]]gyis 'gro mi mdzes/_/bdag gzhan sna tshogs 'ching bas rab bcings pas/_/brtson pa brgya 'gyur du ni bya ba'i rigs/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las sems bskyed pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o//_//gnas rtsom 'bras bu 'byung ba che bdag nyid/_/
[\[5b.6\]]rgyal sras rnams kyi sgrub pa yin par 'dod/_/rtag tu len pa che dang bzod pa che/_/don chen yang dag sgrub pa'i bya ba byed/_/gzhan dang bdag tu mnyam pa'i sems nyid dam/_/bdag pas gzhan ches sdug pa rnyed nas ni/_/de ltar bdag pas gzhan
[\[5b.7\]]don mchog 'du shes/_/rang gi don gang gzhan gyi don gang yin/_/ji ltar snying rje'i bdag nyid gzhan gyi don gyi phyir/_/bdag la sdug bsngal mi bzad gdung ba rab byed pa/_/de ltar 'jig rten gdung ba'i las kyis gzhan dgra la'ang /_/shin tu
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]brtse ba med par rab tu 'jug ma yin/_/tha chad 'bring dang mchog chos nyid gnas la/_/legs par ston dang mgu byed 'jug pa dang /_/don la rnam nges dge ba yongs smin byed/_/de bzhin gdams ngag gnas dang blo rnam
[\[6a.2\]]grol/_/yon tan khyad par can 'grub de bzhin du/_/rigs su skye dang lung bstan dbang bskur dang /_/de bzhin gshegs mkhyen bla med go 'phang ste/_/bcu gsum bdag nyid 'di ni gzhan gyi don/_/skye bo dang mthun phyin ci ma log 'chad/_/mi
[\[6a.3\]]'gying ba dang bdag gi med la mkhas/_/bzod dul shin tu ring song mi zad pa/_/rgyal sras rnams kyi sgrub pa mchog yin no/_/'dod ldan skye bo 'jigs pa che la 'jug_/srid dga' phyin ci log bde g.yo ba la/_/zhi dga' rang gi len pa rab zhi la/_/
[\[6a.4\]]snying rje'i bdag nyid len kun zhi la rtag_/skye bo rmongs pa rang gi bde don brtson/_/rtag tu de ma thob par sdug bsngal 'gyur/_/brtan pa rtag tu gzhan don brtson ldan pa/_/gnyi ka'i don byas mya ngan 'da' bar 'gyur/_/rgyal sras spyod tshe ji lta ji lta bur/_/
[\[6a.5\]]dbang po'i spyod yul sna tshogs 'jug 'gyur ba/_/de lta de ltar rigs shing mthun tshig gis/_/sems can phan phyir de mngon 'du byed do/_/rtag tu nyes pas rang dbang med par byas sems kyi/_/skye bo la ni blo ldan nyes par mi 'dzin te/_/mi 'dod bzhin
[\[6a.6\]]du log par sgrub par 'gyur ro zhes/_/skye bo dag la snying rje rnam par 'phel phyir ro/_/sgrub pa 'dis ni srid dang 'gro ba kun/_/zil gyis mnan 'gro zhi ba mchog dang ldan/_/yon tan sna tshogs tshogs kyis rnam par 'phel/_/byams pa'i bsam pas
[\[6a.7\]]rtag tu 'gro ba sdud/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las sgrub pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o//_//yod min med min de bzhin min gzhan min/_/skye dang 'jig med 'bri bar mi 'gyur te/_/'phel ba med cing rnam par dag pa'ang med/_/rnam par dag
[\[6b\]]
[\[6b.1\]]'gyur de ni don dam mtshan/_/bdag tu lta ba bdag nyid bdag mtshan min/_/ngan par gnas min mtshan nyid mi 'dra phyir/_/gnyis las gzhan med de ni nor pa skyes/_/de phyir thar pa nor tsam zad pa yin/_/ji ltar 'khrul pa tsam brten skye bo yis/_/sdug
[\[6b.2\]]bsngal rang bzhin rgyun chags rtogs mi 'gyur/_/rig min rig nyid sdug bsngal sdug bsngal med/_/chos kyi rang bzhin de yi rang bzhin min/_/brten nas dngos rab skye ba mngon 'jug na/_/skye bo ji ltar gzhan gyis byas la rten/_/gang phyir yod pa
[\[6b.3\]]mi mthong med mthong ba/_/'di 'dra'i mun nag rnam pa de gang zhig_/'di la don dam tshul gyis zhi ba dang /_/skye ba de gnyis khyad par ci yang med/_/'on kyang dge ba'i las rnams byed pa dag_/skye ba zad pas zhi ba 'thob par bshad/_/byang chub sems dpas
[\[6b.4\]]bsod nams ye shes kyi/_/mtha' yas pha rol tshogs rnams legs bsags nas/_/chos la sems pa shin tu rnam nges phyir/_/don gyi rnam pa brjod pa'i rgyu can rtogs/_/de yis brjod pa tsam du don rig nas/_/der snang sems tsam la ni yang
[\[6b.5\]]dag gnas/_/de nas chos dbyings gnyis kyi mtshan nyid dang /_/bral ba mngon sum nyid du rtogs par 'gyur/_/sems las gzhan med par ni blos rig nas/_/de nas sems kyang med pa nyid du rtogs/_/blo dang ldan pas gnyis po med rig nas/_/de mi
[\[6b.6\]]ldan pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas/_/blo dang ldan pas mi rtog ye shes stobs/_/rtag tu kun nas mnyam par song ba yis/_/de la rten pa'i nyes tshogs tshang tshing dag_/dug sman chen pos dug bzhin sel bar byed/_/thub pas gsungs pa'i dam chos legs
[\[6b.7\]]bzhag pa/_/rtsa ba chos kyi dbyings la blo gros bzhag_/dran rgyu rtog pa tsam rig brtan pa dag_/myur du yon tan rgya mtsho'i pha rol 'gro/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_de kho na nyid kyi le'u ste bdun pa'o//_//skye dang ngag sems dge dang mi dge
[\[7a\]]
[\[7a.1\]]bskyed/_/de yi gnas dang 'byung ba mngon sum gang /_/shes pa kun 'gro rab tu dbye bcas la/_/thogs med brtan pa thob pa'i mthu yin no/_/bsam gtan bzhi pa shin tu dag thob nas/_/mi rtog ye shes yongs su bzung ba dang /_/
[\[7a.2\]]ji ltar rnam gnas yid la byed pa las/_/mthu grub pa yi dam pa thob par 'gyur/_/gang gis 'phags dang lha dang tshangs pa yi/_/gnas pa dpe med rgya ches rtag tu gnas/_/phyogs su de song sangs rgyas sems can rnams/_/yang dag mchod byed rnam par
[\[7a.3\]]dag pa skyed/_/chags dang 'jig bcas sems can bcas pa yi/_/'jig rten khams kun sgyu ma lta bur mthong /_/dbang ldan ji ltar 'dod bzhin de dag dang /_/rnam bcas sna tshogs dag kyang yang dag ston/_/'od zer btang bas shin tu sdug bsngal ba'i/_/ngan
[\[7a.4\]]song ba dag mtho ris 'gro bar byed/_/'dud gnas gzhal med khang mtho mdzes pa dag_/bdud bcas kun du bskyod cing skrag par byed/_/de ni mchog tshogs nang du ting nge 'dzin/_/dpag med rnam par rol pa kun ston cing /_/bzo dang skye dang mchog gi
[\[7a.5\]]sprul pa yis/_/sems can rnams kyi don du dus kun gnas/_/ye shes dag la dbang phyir zhing rnams ni/_/ji ltar 'dod bzhin bstan phyir dag la 'thob/_/sangs rgyas mtshan mi grags par sangs rgyas mtshan/_/yang dag bsgrags pas de dag khams
[\[7a.6\]]gzhan 'gyed/_/'dab gshog kun du rgyas pa'i bya bzhin du/_/sems can smin par byed par nus pa nyid/_/sangs rgyas las ni shin tu bsngags pa 'thob/_/skye dgu rnams la tshig gzung 'os par 'gyur/_/mngon par shes pa drug dang rig pa gsum/_/
[\[7a.7\]]rnam thar brgyad dang de bzhin zil gnon brgyad/_/zad par skye mched bcu dang ting nge 'dzin/_/dpag tu med pa brtan pa thob pa'i mthu/_/de ni dbang mchog thob pa'i blo dang ldan/_/'gro ba dbang med rang dbang bkod rtag tu/_/gzhan la phan bya gcig tu mngon dga'
[\[7b\]]
[\[7b.1\]]ste/_/seng ge bzhin du rab brtan srid na spyod/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_mthu'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o//_//dga' dang dad dang rab zhi snying brtse dang /_/bzod dang yid gzhungs mthu can nyid dang ni/_/mi 'phrogs pa dang yan lag ldan pa rab/_/de ni
[\[7b.2\]]rgyal sras yongs su smin pa'i mtshan/_/grogs mchog la sogs gsum dang brtson rab dang /_/mthar phyin dam pa dang ni chos mchog sdud/_/dam chos cher gzung phyir ni snying rje can/_/yang dag yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/_/yon tan shes dang sems
[\[7b.3\]]kyang mi phyed dang /_/ting 'dzin myur du thob dang 'bras bu myong /_/ston la yid ches bya phyir rgyal sras kyi/_/yang dag yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/_/shin tu sdom zhing nyon mongs rtog pa spong /_/bar chad med cing dge la mngon par dga'/_/rgyal ba'i sras
[\[7b.4\]]kyi nyon mongs bsal ba'i phyir/_/yang dag yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/_/rang bzhin snying brtse gzhan gyi sdug bsngal mthong /_/dman pa'i sems kyang yang dag rab tu spong /_/khyad par 'gro dang 'gro ba'i mchog gyur lus/_/gzhan la snying brtse yongs su
[\[7b.5\]]smin pa'i mtshan/_/rang bzhin brtan pa so sor brtags bsgom pa/_/grang sogs shin tu sdug bsngal rtag mi mjed/_/khyad par 'gro dang dge la mngon par dga'/_/bzod pa yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/_/rnam smin dag cing thos sogs dran mi brjed/_/
[\[7b.6\]]de bzhin legs bshad nyes par smras pa dag_/rab shes blo chen skye bar rung ba nyid/_/shin tu yid gzhungs yongs su smin pa'i mtshan/_/dge ba gnyis kyis khams gnyis brtas pa dang /_/rten ni 'bras bu skye bar rung ba'i mchog_/yid la bsam grub
[\[7b.7\]]'gro ba'i mchog gyur pa/_/mthu thob yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid do/_/chos bzang rigs pas rnam dpyad bsam pa can/_/rtag tu bdud kyi bar chad byed pa med/_/khyad par rnyed dang gzhan gyi phyogs sun 'byin/_/mi 'phrogs yongs su smin pa'i mtshan
[\[8a\]]
[\[8a.1\]]nyid do/_/dge ba bsags dang rten kyang brtson par rung /_/dben dang dge ba mchog la mngon par dga'/_/rgyal ba'i sras kyi yan lag ldan pa yi/_/yang dag yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid do/_/de ltar dngos po rnam dgus smin pa'i
[\[8a.2\]]bdag_/pha rol yongs su smin byed rung dang ldan/_/chos kyi rang bzhin rgyun 'phel bdag nyid can/_/rtag tu 'gro ba'i gnyen mchog gyur pa yin/_/ji ltar rma dang zas la de dag gi_/gzag dang spyad du rung ba smin 'dod ltar/_/de bzhin rten 'dir phyogs gnyis
[\[8a.3\]]zhi ba dang /_/de bzhin spyad pa nyid du smin pa bstan/_/lus can bral bar smin byed de bzhin du/_/yongs smin rab smin mthun par smin byed gzhan/_/legs par smin byed rtogs pas smin byed dang /_/rtag smin gong du smin byed bshad par 'dod/_/ji ltar rgyal sras
[\[8a.4\]]phan pa'i bsam pas 'dir/_/'gro kun rnam par smin byed gnas pa ltar/_/de bzhin pha dang ma dang gnyen bshes rnams/_/bu dang gnyen pa rnams la legs mi gnas/_/ji ltar brtse bdag bde dang phan phyir sbyor/_/sems can gzhan la byams 'dod de ltar ni/_/
[\[8a.5\]]skye bo bdag la'ang byams par mi 'dod na/_/rab sdug skye bo gzhan brten smos ci dgos/_/byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang longs spyod dag_/gzhan la mi sbyin pa ni yod med de/_/phan 'dogs rnam pa gnyis kyis gzhan smin byed/_/mnyam par sbyin pa'i yon
[\[8a.6\]]tan ngoms mi 'gyur/_/brtan pa rang bzhin lhag par 'tshe ba med/_/bdag dga' bag yod 'di la gzhan 'god cing /_/phan rnam gnyis 'dogs rnam par smin pa dang /_/rgyu mthun yon tan brgyud pas gzhan smin byed/_/gzhan gnod byed la phan byed blo ldan
[\[8a.7\]]pa/_/gnod byed drag po dag kyang rab tu bzod/_/thabs rig gnod byed bzod pa de dag gis/_/gnod byed dge ba yang dag len du 'jug_/rgyal sras brtson 'grus mchog la brten pa de/_/sems can tshogs rab smin par byed pa na/_/pha rol sems dge
[\[8b\]]
[\[8b.1\]]gcig gi phyir yang ni/_/bskal pa bye ba stong du'ang skyo mi 'gyur/_/yid kyi dbang ni bla na med thob nas/_/gzhan gyi mchod 'dod thams cad nges bcom ste/_/mchog gi bstan la gzhan dag 'dun byed cing /_/de dag dge ba yang dag 'phel bar byed/_/de
[\[8b.2\]]nyid dgongs don tshul la rab nges te/_/sems can the tshom shin tu sel bar byed/_/de phyir rgyal ba'i bstan la de gus pas/_/rang gzhan dge ba'i yon tan rnam 'phel byed/_/de ltar byang chub sems dpa' snying rje yis/_/'gro kun bde 'gro'i 'gro ba'ang dge
[\[8b.3\]]gsum la/_/rnam pa chung dang mchog dang 'bring dag gis/_/'jig rten yod dang mnyam par 'jug pas 'dul/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las yongs su smin pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o//_//dka' spyod dpag med brgya phrag dang /_/dpag med dge ba
[\[8b.4\]]bsags pa dang /_/dpag tu med pa'i dus dang ni/_/dpag med sgrib pa zad pa'i phyir/_/sgrib pa kun gyi dri med pa/_/rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid 'thob/_/rin chen snod ni phye ba ltar/_/sangs rgyas nyid ni yang dag bstan/_/ngal brgyas rmad byung dka'
[\[8b.5\]]spyad dge kun bsags/_/bskal mchog dus ring 'gro ba'i sgrib kun zad/_/sar gtogs sgrib pa phra bcom sangs rgyas te/_/de ni mthu chen rin chen snod phye bzhin/_/chos rnams thams cad sangs rgyas nyid/_/chos ni gang yang yod ma yin/_/de ni chos dkar rang
[\[8b.6\]]bzhin yang /_/de yis de ni brjod ma yin/_/rin chen chos kyi rgyu mtshan phyir/_/de ni rin chen 'byung gnas bzhin/_/dge ba'i lo tog rgyu mtshan phyir/_/de ni sprin dang 'dra bar 'dod/_/sangs rgyas nyid ni chos kun ldan pa'am yang na chos kun bral ba ste/_/
[\[8b.7\]]rin chen chos rab che yangs 'byung phyir rin chen chos kyi 'byung gnas bzhin/_/skye dgu rnams la legs bshad mi zad chos kyi char chen 'bebs pas na/_/'byung po'i lo tog dkar po shin tu che 'phel rgyu phyir sprin dang 'dra/_/rtag tu nyon mongs tshogs kun dang /_/
[\[9a\]]
[\[9a.1\]]nyes par spyod pa thams cad dang /_/rga dang 'chi ba dag las kyang /_/sangs rgyas nyid ni yongs su skyob/_/'tshe ba dag ni thams cad dang /_/ngan song dang ni thabs min dang /_/'jig tshogs theg pa dman dag las/_/de phyir skyabs kyi
[\[9a.2\]]dam pa 'o/_/sangs rgyas nyid de skyabs ni dpe med mchog tu 'dod/_/sna tshogs 'jigs gyur 'jig tshogs kun dang theg pa dang /_/ngan song rnam mang sdug bsngal thabs min song ba rnams/_/skye dang 'chi dang nyon mongs ngan song kun las srung /_/sangs rgyas
[\[9a.3\]]chos kyi shin tu rdzogs pa'i sku gang yin/_/dam pa'i chos la sems can rab 'dul mkhyen pa gang /_/'gro ba kun la thugs brtse'i pha rol phyin pa gang /_/sangs rgyas nyid de 'dir ni skyabs kyi mchog tu 'dod/_/'jig rten ji srid sems can gyi/_/gnod dang
[\[9a.4\]]phun sum tshogs pa kun/_/bzlog cing 'byor par bya ba'i phyir/_/sangs rgyas skyabs chen nyid du 'dod/_/gang la nyon mongs shes bya'i sgrib pa'i sa bon dus ring rtag ldan pa/_/spong ba shin tu rgya chen rnam pa kun gyi rab tu bcom gyur cing /_/gnas gyur chos dkar yon
[\[9a.5\]]tan mchog rab ldan pa thob pa sangs rgyas nyid/_/de ni mi rtog rab dag shin tu yul chen ye shes lam gyis 'thob/_/de bzhin gshegs pa de ni der bzhugs nas/_/ri dbang mtho steng bzhugs bzhin 'gro la gzigs/_/zhi bar mngon dga'i 'gro la'ang
[\[9a.6\]]thugs rje na/_/srid la mngon dga'i skye bo gzhan ci smos/_/gnas la 'jug dang rab 'jug mi 'jug dang /_/ldog dang kun 'jug gnyis dang mi gnyis dang /_/mnyam dang khyad 'phags kun 'gro'i bdag nyid ni/_/de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi yongs gyur
[\[9a.7\]]'dod/_/ji ltar nam mkha' rtag tu kun song 'dod/_/de bzhin de yang rtag tu kun song 'dod/_/ji ltar nam mkha' gzugs gyur kun du song /_/de bzhin de yang sems can tshogs kun song /_/ji ltar chu yi snod chag na/_/zla ba'i gzugs brnyan mi
[\[9b\]]
[\[9b.1\]]snang ba/_/de bzhin sems can ngan pa la/_/sangs rgyas gzugs kyang mi snang ngo /_/ji ltar me ni gzhan du 'bar/_/gzhan du zhi bar 'gyur ba ltar/_/de bzhin sangs rgyas rnams la yang /_/snang dang mi snang shes par bya/_/ji ltar rnga dag ma brdungs par/_/sgra ni kun du
[\[9b.2\]]'byung ba ltar/_/de bzhin rgyal ba gzo med par/_/bshad pa dag ni kun du 'byung /_/ji ltar nor bu 'bad med par/_/rang gi 'od ni ston pa ltar/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyang gzo med par/_/de bzhin mdzad pa nges pa ston/_/ji ltar mkha' la 'jig rten gyi/_/bya ba
[\[9b.3\]]rgyun mi 'chad par snang /_/de bzhin zag med dbyings na yang /_/rgyal ba'i mdzad pa rgyun mi 'chad/_/ji ltar mkha' la rtag tu ni/_/bya ba nyams shing 'byung ba ltar/_/de bzhin zag med dbyings na yang /_/sangs rgyas 'phrin las skye zhing 'bri/_/snga ma phyi mar khyad med
[\[9b.4\]]kyang /_/sgrib pa kun gyi dri med pa/_/de bzhin nyid ni sangs rgyas 'dod/_/dag pa ma yin ma dag min/_/stong pa nyid ni rnam dag na/_/bdag med mchog gi bdag thob pas/_/sangs rgyas dag pa'i bdag thob phyir/_/bdag nyid chen po'i bdag tu 'gyur/_/de phyir
[\[9b.5\]]sangs rgyas yod min zhing /_/med par yang ni mi brjod do/_/de ltar sangs rgyas de skad 'dri/_/lung ma bstan pa'i tshul du 'dod/_/ji ltar lcags la tsha ba dang /_/mig la rab rib zhi ba ltar/_/sangs rgyas sems dang ye shes la/_/yod dang med par mi brjod
[\[9b.6\]]do/_/zag med dbyings na sangs rgyas rnams/_/mkha' ltar lus ni med phyir dang /_/sngon gyi lus rjes 'brang ba'i phyir/_/gcig min mang po nyid ma yin/_/stobs sogs sangs rgyas chos rnams la/_/byang chub rin chen 'byung gnas 'dra/_/'gro ba'i dge
[\[9b.7\]]ba'i lo tog la/_/sprin chen dang yang 'dra bar 'dod/_/bsod nams ye shes rab rdzogs phyir/_/zla ba nya ba lta bur 'dod/_/ye shes snang ba byed pa'i phyir/_/nyi ma chen po 'dra bar 'dod/_/ji ltar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi/_/'od zer dpag tu med 'dres
[\[10a\]]
[\[10a.1\]]shing /_/rtag tu bya ba gcig la 'jug_/'jig rten la yang snang ba byed/_/de bzhin zag med dbyings na yang /_/sangs rgyas dpag tu med 'dres shing /_/mdzad pa gcig ni mdzad pa la/_/ye shes snang bar mdzad par 'dod/_/dper na
[\[10a.2\]]nyi ma'i 'od zer gcig_/byung na 'od zer kun 'byung ba/_/de bzhin sangs rgyas rnams kyi yang /_/ye shes 'byung bar shes par bya/_/ji ltar nyi ma'i 'od zer dag_/'jug la bdag gir bya ba med/_/de bzhin sangs rgyas ye shes kyang /_/'jug la bdag gir
[\[10a.3\]]mdzad mi mnga'/_/nyi ma'i 'od zer gcig btang bas/_/'gro ba snang ba byed pa ltar/_/de bzhin shes bya thams cad la/_/sangs rgyas ye shes cig car snang /_/ji ltar nyi ma'i 'od zer rnams/_/sprin la sogs pas bsgribs par 'dod/_/de bzhin sangs rgyas
[\[10a.4\]]ye shes rnams/_/sems can gyi ni nyes pas bsgribs/_/ji ltar mdud pa'i dbang gis na/_/gos la tshon bkra mi bkra ba/_/de bzhin 'phen pa'i dbang gis na/_/grol ba'i ye shes bkra mi bkra/_/dri med dbyings la sangs rgyas kyi/_/mtshan nyid dang ni
[\[10a.5\]]gnas pa dang /_/'phrin las zab pa 'di bshad pa/_/mkha' la tshon gyis ri mo 'dri/_/de bzhin nyid ni thams cad la/_/khyad par med kyang dag gyur pa/_/de bzhin gshegs nyid de yi phyir/_/'gro kun de yi snying po can/_/nyan thos rnams kyi 'byor pas
[\[10a.6\]]ni/_/'jig rten pa yi zil gyis gnon/_/rang sangs rgyas kyis pa yis/_/nyan thos kyi yang zil gyis gnon/_/de yis byang chub sems dpa' yi/_/'byor pa'i char yang mi phod do/_/de yis de bzhin gshegs pa yi/_/'byor pa'i char yang mi
[\[10a.7\]]phod do/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyi 'byor pa ni/_/gang gi gang du ji ltar dang /_/ji tsam dus gang 'jug pa ni/_/bsam yas dpag tu med par 'dod/_/dbang po lnga rnams gzhan gyur na/_/don kun 'jug dang thams cad kyi/_/yon tan brgya phrag bcu
[\[10b\]]
[\[10b.1\]]gnyis 'byung /_/'byor pa dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/yid ni gzhan du gyur pa na/_/'byor dang mthun spyod mi rtog pa'i/_/ye shes shin tu dri med la/_/'byor pa dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/don bcas 'dzin pa gzhan gyur na/_/ji ltar 'dod bzhin longs spyod
[\[10b.2\]]dag_/bstan phyir zhing ni dag pa la/_/'byor pa dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/rnam rtog gzhan du gyur na ni/_/dus rnams rtag tu ye shes dang /_/las rnams kun la thogs med la/_/'byor pa dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/rten ni gzhan du gyur pa na/_/sangs
[\[10b.3\]]rgyas dri med gnas la ni/_/mi gnas mya ngan 'das pa yi/_/'byor pa dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/'khrig pa gzhan du gyur na ni/_/sangs rgyas bde bar gnas pa dang /_/mo mthong nyon mongs med pa la/_/'byor pa dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/nam mkha'i 'du
[\[10b.4\]]shes gzhan gyur na/_/bsam pa'i don ni 'byor pa dang /_/'gro gzugs rnam par 'byed pa la/_/'byor pa dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/de ltar sangs rgyas dri med pa'i/_/gnas na gzhan gyur dpag med la/_/bsam yas bya ba sgrub pa yi/_/'byor pa dpag
[\[10b.5\]]tu med par 'dod/_/'di na 'jig rten phyogs phyogs rgyal ba'i legs bshad pa'i/_/dge ba 'phel ba'i 'jig rten rnam dag mchog tu 'gro/_/dge ba ma bsags dge ba 'phel ba'i mchog tu 'gro/_/de ltar ma smin smin pa rtag 'gro'ang ma lus min/_/de ltar
[\[10b.6\]]'jig rten phyogs phyogs brten rnams rtag par dus kun du/_/byang chub chen po 'thob dka' yon tan mchog ldan rmad byung can/_/rtag brtan skyabs med rnams kyi skyabs gang yin pa thob pa de/_/ya mtshan che la tshul bzang spyad phyir ya mtshan che ba'ang med/_/
[\[10b.7\]]de ni cig car la lar sgo mang brgya nas chos kyi 'khor lo dang /_/la lar skye ba mi snang la lar skye ba'i spyod pa sna tshogs dang /_/la lar byang chub thams cad la lar de ni mya ngan 'das ston kyang /_/de ni gnas de las kyang rnam par g.yo mi mnga' la thams cad mdzad/_/
[\[11a\]]
[\[11a.1\]]sangs rgyas rnams ni 'di snyam lus can 'di ni bdag gis smin byas she'am/_/'di ni rab tu smin bya gzhan yang da ltar smin par byed snyam du/_/'du mdzad mi mnga' bar yang phyogs phyogs kun du rtag par sgo gsum nas/_/dge ba'i chos rnams
[\[11a.2\]]kyis ni skye bo rab tu smin par 'gyur ba nyid/_/ji ltar nyi ma 'bad med phyogs phyogs kun du 'od zer dag_/rab 'byams gsal ba mang pos lo tog rnam smin byed pa ltar/_/de bzhin chos ldan nyi ma'ang rab zhi byed pa chos kyi 'od/_/rab 'byams dag gis phyogs
[\[11a.3\]]phyogs kun du sems can rnam smin mdzad/_/ji ltar mar me gcig las mar me'i tshogs rab mang /_/dpag med grangs med 'byung yang de la zad pa med/_/de bzhin smin pa gcig las smin pa'i tshogs rab mang /_/grangs med dpag med 'byung yang de la zad
[\[11a.4\]]pa med/_/ji ltar rgya mtsho chen po 'di ni chu yis ngoms par mi 'gyur zhing /_/chu chen mang po rab tu 'bab pas 'phel bar yang ni mi 'gyur ba/_/de bzhin sangs rgyas khams kyang dag pa 'jug pa rtag rgyun mi 'chad pas/_/ngoms pa mi mnga' 'phel bar mi 'gyur
[\[11a.5\]]de 'dir rmad du byung ba'i mchog_/chos rnams kun gyi de bzhin nyid/_/sgrib gnyis dag pa'i mtshan nyid de/_/dngos dang nges dmigs shes pa la/_/dbang zad mi shes mtshan nyid do/_/de bzhin nyid shes thams cad nas/_/bsgoms pa las ni yang dag 'byung /_/
[\[11a.6\]]sems can kun la rnam kun du/_/gnyis skyed mi zad 'bras bu can/_/sku dang gsung dang thugs sprul pa'i/_/sbyor ba'i thabs kyi las can te/_/ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs sgo dang /_/dpag tu med pa gnyis dang ldan/_/rang bzhin chos rdzogs longs spyod dag_/_
[\[11a.7\]]sprul pa dag gis tha dad du/_/'jug pa 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi/_/chos dbyings rnam par dag par bshad/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku dbye ba/_/rang bzhin longs spyod rdzogs pa dang /_/gzhan ni sprul pa'i sku yin te/_/dang po gnyis po'i rten yin no/_/longs
[\[11b\]]
[\[11b.1\]]spyod rdzogs pa khams kun du/_/'khor yongs sdud dang zhing dang mtshan/_/sku dang chos rdzogs longs spyod dang /_/mdzad pa dag gis tha dad do/_/rang bzhin sku ni mnyam pa dang /_/phra zhing de dang 'brel pa dang /_/dgyes dgur longs spyod bstan pa la/_/longs spyod
[\[11b.2\]]rdzogs 'byor rgyur 'dod do/_/sangs rgyas sprul pa dpag med pa/_/sprul pa'i skur ni 'dod pa ste/_/don gnyis phun sum tshogs pa ni/_/rnam pa thams cad gnyis la gnas/_/bzo dang skye dang byang chub che/_/mya ngan 'das pa rtag ston pas/_/sangs rgyas sprul
[\[11b.3\]]pa'i sku 'di ni/_/rnam par grol ba'i thabs chen no/_/sku gsum dag gis sangs rgyas kyi/_/sku bsdus par ni shes bya ste/_/sku gsum dag gis rang bzhin gyi/_/don 'di rten dang bcas par bstan/_/de dag rten dang dgongs pa dang /_/'phrin las kyis ni
[\[11b.4\]]mnyam pa nyid/_/rang bzhin dang ni rgyun mi 'chad/_/rgyun gyis de dag rtag pa nyid/_/me long ye shes mi g.yo ba/_/ye shes gsum ni de la brten/_/mnyam pa nyid dang so sor rtog_/bya ba sgrub pa kho na'o/_/me long ye shes nga yi med/_/yongs su
[\[11b.5\]]ma chad rtag tu ldan/_/shes bya kun la ma rmongs la/_/rtag tu de la mngon phyogs min/_/ye shes kun gyi rgyu mtshan phyir/_/ye shes 'byung gnas chen po 'dra/_/longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyid/_/ye shes gzugs brnyan 'byung ba'i phyir/_/mnyam
[\[11b.6\]]nyid ye shes sems can la/_/bsgom pa dag pa la 'dod do/_/mi gnas zhi bar zhugs pa ni/_/mnyam nyid ye shes yin par 'dod/_/dus rnams kun du byams pa dang /_/thugs rje chen po dag dang ldan/_/sems can rnams la mos pa bzhin/_/sangs rgyas
[\[11b.7\]]sku ni nges par ston/_/so sor rtog pa'i ye shes ni/_/shes bya kun la rtag mi thogs/_/ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs rnams kyi/_/gter dang 'dra ba kho na yin/_/'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnams su ni/_/'byor pa thams cad ston mdzad pa/_/the tshom thams cad gcod
[\[12a\]]
[\[12a.1\]]pa yi/_/chos chen char ni rab tu 'bebs/_/bya ba sgrub pa'i ye shes ni/_/khams rnams kun du sna tshogs shing /_/dpag med bsam yas sprul pa yis/_/sems can kun gyi don sgrub pa'o/_/sangs rgyas sprul pa de rtag tu/_/mdzad pa grub
[\[12a.2\]]pa'i bye brag dang /_/grangs dang zhing gis rnam kun du/_/bsam mi khyab par shes par bya/_/'dzin pa'i phyir dang sems mnyam phyir/_/yang dag chos rab ston phyir dang /_/bya ba sgrub pa nyid kyi phyir/_/ye shes bzhi po yang dag 'byung /_/rigs tha dad phyir don yod
[\[12a.3\]]phyir/_/rdzogs phyir thog ma med pa'i phyir/_/sangs rgyas gcig min dri med gnas/_/tha dad med phyir mang po'ang min/_/med pa gang yin de nyid ni/_/yod pa yi ni dam par 'dod/_/rnam pa kun du mi dmigs pa/_/dmigs pa yi ni mchog tu 'dod/_/bsgom pa
[\[12a.4\]]rnam par mi lta ba'i/_/bsgom pa dam par 'dod pa ste/_/thob par lta ba med rnams kyi/_/thob pa yang ni dam par 'dod/_/bla ma ring dang mtshan ma dang /_/bdag gi brtson 'grus lhag lta ba'i/_/byang chub sems dpa' nga rgyal can/_/byang chub las ni ring zhes
[\[12a.5\]]bya/_/ji skad bshad pa de dag kun/_/rtog pa tsam du lta ba yi/_/byang chub sems dpa' rtog med rnams/_/byang chub thob ces nges par brjod/_/klung dag sa yi 'og tu ma song ba/_/gnas rnams tha dad chu yang tha dad la/_/chu yang chung zhing bya ba tha dad byed/_/
[\[12a.6\]]chu gnas srog chags phra mo'i nyer spyad 'gyur/_/rgya mtshor song bar gyur na thams cad kyang /_/gnas rnams gcig cing chu yang che la gcig_/bya ba gcig cing chu la gnas pa yi/_/srog chags mang po'i rtag tu nyer spyad che/_/sangs rgyas nyid du ma zhugs
[\[12a.7\]]brtan pa rnams/_/rten kyang tha dad blo gros tha dad cing /_/rtogs chung rang gi bya ba tha dad la/_/sems can nyung don rtag tu nyer spyad 'gyur/_/sangs rgyas nyid du zhugs na de dag kun/_/rten kyang gcig cing rtogs pa che la gcig_/mdzad pa gcig tu 'dres
[\[12b\]]
[\[12b.1\]]shing rtag par yang /_/sems can tshogs che'i nye bar spyad pa che/_/de ltar sangs rgyas nyid ni dkar po'i chos/_/dpe med ldan phyir phan bde'i rgyu yi phyir/_/bde dge dam pa mi zad 'byung gnas phyir/_/blo ldan byang chub sems dge blang ba'i rigs/_/theg pa chen po
[\[12b.2\]]mdo sde'i rgyan las/_byang chub kyi le'u ste bcu pa'o//_//sdom ni/_dang po sgrub skyabs rigs dang ni/_/de bzhin du ni sems bskyed dang /_/rang gzhan don dang de nyid don/_/mthu dang yongs smin byang chub po/_/skyes dang ma skyes 'dzin dang gzung gyur dang /_/
[\[12b.3\]]grogs blangs bdag nyid dang ni nor pa dang /_/ma nor mngon sum mngon sum ma yin gzhan/_/sgras byung tshol ba dang ni lta ba po/_/'phrogs dang 'dres dang mi mthun phyogs ma 'dres/_/dman dang rgya che bsgribs dang ma bsgribs dang /_/brtson dang mi brtson bsags dang
[\[12b.4\]]ma bsags dang /_/brtan zhugs ring du song ba'i mos pa'o/_/yid la mi byed mang ba dang /_/le lo rnal 'byor 'khrugs pa dang /_/grogs ngan dge ba zhan pa dang /_/tshul bzhin ma yin yid la byed/_/bag med pa dang thos pa nyung /_/thos dang bsam pa nyung
[\[12b.5\]]ngus chog_/zhi ba tsam gyis nga rgyal dang /_/de bzhin ma 'dris yin par 'dod/_/mi skyo ba dang de bzhin skyo/_/bsgribs pa dang ni mi brtson pa/_/tshogs ma bsags pa mos pa yis/_/bar du gcod par shes par bya/_/bsod nams che dang 'gyod pa med/_/yid
[\[12b.6\]]bde ba dang bde ba che/_/chud mi za dang brtan pa dang /_/de bzhin khyad par 'gro ba dang /_/chos ni mngon par rtogs pa dang /_/bdag dang gzhan don thob pa'i mchog_/mngon shes myur ba de dag ni/_/mos pa yi ni phan yon yin/_/'dod pa can gyi de khyi 'dra/_/ting
[\[12b.7\]]nge 'dzin pa'i rus sbal bzhin/_/rang don byed pa'i de dran 'dra/_/gzhan don byed pa'i rgyal po bzhin/_/ji ltar khyi ni rtag tu ltogs shing sdug bsngal gyis nyen chog mi shes/_/ji ltar rus sbal de ni chu yi nang na kun nas bskums shing 'dug_/ji ltar bran ni rtag
[\[13a\]]
[\[13a.1\]]tu 'jigs shing skrag pa'i lus kyis rnam par rgyu/_/ji ltar rgyal po yang ni bka' yis yul la dbang sgyur gnas pa ltar/_/de bzhin g.yem dang gnas dang rang gzhan phan bya don byed pa'i/_/mos pa sna tshogs dag gi rtag tu khyad par shes
[\[13a.2\]]par bya/_/theg pa chen po de la de mchog tshul bzhin rig nas ni/_/'di na brtan pas de la de nyid rtag par rab tu tshol/_/gang phyir sems can mir gyur pas/_/tshad med skad cig re re la/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob de'i phyir/_/zhum pa dang du blang mi bya/_/gzhan
[\[13a.3\]]dag la ni zas sbyin pa'i/_/bsod nams 'phel ba ji lta bar/_/bdag nyid za ba'i ma yin pa/_/de bzhin gzhan don rten gyi chos/_/bstan las mdo las gsungs pa yi/_/bsod nams cher 'byung thob pa ltar/_/rang gi don gyi rten gyi chos/_/bstan las thob
[\[13a.4\]]pa ma yin no/_/de ltar 'phags pa chen po'i chos ni yangs gyur pa/_/blo dang ldan pas rtag tu mos pa cher bskyed na/_/bsod nams rgya chen rgyun mi 'chad dang de 'phel dang /_/yon tan dpag tu med pas bdag nyid chen por 'gyur/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_mos
[\[13a.5\]]pa'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o//_//sde snod dag ni gsum mam gnyis kyang rung /_/bsdus pa'i phyir te rgyu ni dgur 'dod do/_/des ni bag chags rtogs dang zhi ba dang /_/rab tu rtogs pas rnam par grol bar byed/_/mdo dang chos mngon 'dul ba dag_/mdor na don
[\[13a.6\]]ni rnam bzhir 'dod/_/blo dang ldan pas de shes nas/_/rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa 'thob/_/gnas rnams dang ni mtshan nyid dang /_/chos don smos phyir mdo yin no/_/mngon du'i phyir dang yang yang dang /_/zil gnon rtogs phyir mngon pa'i chos/_/ltung dang 'byung dang ldang
[\[13a.7\]]ba dang /_/nges par 'byung dang gang zag dang /_/bcas pa dang ni rab dbye dang /_/rnam par nges phyir 'dul ba nyid/_/dmigs pa chos dang nang dang ni/_/phyi dang gnyis ni yin par 'dod/_/don gnyis kyis ni gnyis po rnyed/_/gnyis po dag ni mi dmigs pas/_/yid
[\[13b\]]
[\[13b.1\]]kyi brjod pas bshad bzhin don/_/rab dang don du snang ba ni/_/brjod las yin par rab 'dzin phyir/_/sems ni ming la gnas pa'i phyir/_/thos la sogs pa'i shes gsum gyis/_/chos kyi dmigs pa rnyed par 'gyur/_/dmigs pa rnam pa gsum rnyed pa/_/
[\[13b.2\]]sngar bshad de la yang dag rten/_/rigs gsum pa dang bya ba byed/_/gnod bcas gnod med rten can te/_/mos pa 'jog par byed dang gzhan/_/'dun pa drag por byed pa dang /_/dman nad rdzogs rten rnam pa gnyis/_/rjod dang bcas dang rjod med nyid/_/shes pa
[\[13b.3\]]dang ni mtshungs ldan pa/_/rnal 'byor rgyu dang bdag bcas dang /_/de ni 'dres la dmigs pa dang /_/ma 'dres pa la dmigs pa ste/_/rnam pa lnga dang rnam bdun nyid/_/'di yi yongs su shes pa lnga/_/rnam pa sgom dang ldan pa ni/_/bzhi dang sum cu rtsa bdun no/_/
[\[13b.4\]]de ni lam gnyis rang bzhin te/_/phan yon gnyis dang nod pa dang /_/sbyor ba pa dang dbang sgyur dang /_/chung dang rgya che'i bdag nyid de/_/rnal 'byor rnams kyi yid byed 'di/_/thams cad bdag nyid yin par 'dod/_/rtag tu gnyis bral 'khrul pa'i rten gang yin
[\[13b.5\]]dang gang zhig rnam kun du/_/brjod par nus ma yin zhing spros pa med pa'i bdag nyid de kho na/_/shes bya spang bya rang bzhin dri med 'dod gang rnam par sbyang bya ste/_/de ni nam mkha' gser dang chu ltar nyon mongs pa las rnam dag 'dod/_/'gro ba dag na de las
[\[13b.6\]]gzhan yang cung zad yod min la/_/'gro ba ma lus pa yang de la kun du rmongs pa'i blo/_/yod pa kun nas spangs te med la mngon zhe na gang yin pa/_/'jig rten rmongs pa'i rnam pa tshabs chen 'di ko ji lta bu/_/ji ltar sgyu ma de bzhin du/_/yang dag ma yin kun
[\[13b.7\]]rtog brjod/_/sgyu ma'i rnam pa ji lta bar/_/de bzhin gnyis su 'khrul par brjod/_/ji ltar de la de med pa/_/de bzhin du ni don dam 'dod/_/ji ltar de ni dmigs gyur pa/_/de bzhin du ni kun rdzob 'dod/_/de med na ni de yi rgyu/_/gsal bar dmigs pa ji lta ba/_/
[\[14a\]]
[\[14a.1\]]de bzhin gnas ni gzhan gyur na/_/yang dag ma yin rtog pa dmigs/_/ji ltar 'jig rten ma 'khrul pa/_/de yi rgyu la 'dod dgur spyod/_/de bzhin sdom brtson ma 'khrul ba/_/gnas gzhan gyur la dgyes dgur spyod/_/de yi rnam pa de la yod/_/
[\[14a.2\]]de yi dngos po yod ma yin/_/de ltar sgyu ma la sogs la/_/yod dang med pa nyid du brjod/_/de la yod pa med ma yin/_/med pa yod pa nyid ma yin/_/sgyu ma dag la sogs pa la/_/yod med khyad par med pa'ang brjod/_/de bzhin gnyis snang de la yod/_/de yi
[\[14a.3\]]dngos po yod ma yin/_/de ltar gzugs la sogs pa la/_/yod dang med pa nyid du brjod/_/de la yod pa med ma yin/_/med pa yod pa nyid ma yin/_/gzugs la sogs pa dag la ni/_/yod med khyad par med pa'ang brjod/_/sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa yi/_
[\[14a.4\]]mtha' rnams dgag par bya phyir dang /_/theg pa dman pas 'gro ba dag_/dgag par bya phyir 'dod pa yin/_/'khrul pa'i rgyu dang 'khrul pa ni/_/gzugs kyi rnam par rig pa dang /_/gzugs can min rnam rig par 'dod/_/med phyir cig shos kyang med 'gyur/_/
[\[14a.5\]]sgyu ma'i glang po'i gzugs 'dzin pa/_/'khrul phyir gnyis su brjod pa ste/_/de la ji bzhin gnyis med kyang /_/gnyis po dag tu nye bar dmigs/_/keng rus kyi ni gzugs 'dzin pa/_/'khrul phyir gnyis su brjod pa ste/_/de la ji bzhin gnyis med kyang /_/
[\[14a.6\]]gnyis po dag tu nye bar dmigs/_/'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid chos gang yin/_/de bzhin yod dang de bzhin med/_/yod med khyad par med pa'i phyir/_/yod dang med dang sgyu ma 'dra/_/gnyen po'i chos ni gang yin pa/_/de bzhin med dang de bzhin yod/_/de bzhin
[\[14a.7\]]med phyir mtshan nyid med/_/sgyu ma dang yang 'dra bar bstan/_/sgyu ma'i rgyal po sgyu ma yi/_/rgyal po gzhan gyis pham pa ltar/_/gang dag gis ni chos mthong ba'i/_/rgyal sras de dag nga rgyal med/_/sangs rgyas rnams sangs rgyas mchog rnams kyis de
[\[14b\]]
[\[14b.1\]]dang de las 'dus byas dag_/gsungs pa sgyu ma rmi lam smig rgyu gzugs brnyan dang 'dra mig yor dang /_/brag ca lta bu dang ni chu zla'i gzugs 'dra sprul dang 'drar shes bya/_/drug dang drug dang gnyis dang drug tshan gnyis dang gsum po re rer 'dod/_/yang dag min rtog
[\[14b.2\]]yang dag min/_/yang dag ma yin min mi rtog_/rtog min mi rtog ma yin pa/_/shes bya thams cad yin par brjod/_/rang gi khams las gnyis snang zhing /_/ma rig nyon mongs lhan cig tu/_/'jug pa'i rnam rtog rab 'byung ste/_/rdzas gnyis rnam par spangs
[\[14b.3\]]pa yin/_/dmigs pa'i khyad par thob pa yi/_/rang gi dbyings la gnas ldan phyir/_/de nyid gnyis su snang med par/_/'jug ste lpags dang mda' bzhin no/_/sems ni gnyis su snang ba ste/_/de bzhin chags sogs snang ba'am/_/dad la sogs par snang
[\[14b.4\]]bar 'dod/_/nyon mongs dge chos yod ma yin/_/sems ni sna tshogs snang ba dang /_/rnam pa sna tshogs can du 'jug_/de la snang de yod dang med/_/de phyir chos kyi ma yin no/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyis sems can la/_/phan gdags phyir ni mtshan gzhi
[\[14b.5\]]dang /_/mtshan nyid dang ni mtshon pa dag_/rab tu dbye bas yang dag bshad/_/sems ni lta bcas gang yin dang /_/de yi gnas skabs mi 'gyur ba/_/'di ni mdor na mtshan gzhi ste/_/rab tu dbye na tshad med do/_/ji ltar brjod don 'du shes kyi/_/rgyu mtshan
[\[14b.6\]]dang de'i bag chags dang /_/de las kyang don snang ba ni/_/kun brtags pa yi mtshan nyid do/_/ming dang don ni ji lta bar/_/don dang ming du snang ba gang /_/yang dag min rtog rgyu mtshan ni/_/kun brtags pa yi mtshan nyid do/_/rnam gsum rnam gsum snang ba can/_/
[\[14b.7\]]'dzin dang gzung ba'i mtshan nyid de/_/yang dag ma yin kun rtog ni/_/gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid de/_/med dang yod nyid gang yin dang /_/yod dang med pa mnyam nyid dang /_/ma zhi zhi dang rnam mi rtog_/yongs su grub pa'i mtshan nyid do/_/rgyu mthun chos la dmigs
[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]nas ni/_/tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang /_/sems kyi dbyings la gnas pa dang /_/don yod pa dang med par mthong /_/de na mnyam pa nyid du 'gyur/_/'phags rigs shin tu dri med pa/_/mnyam dang khyad 'phags 'bri med cing /_/
[\[15a.2\]]'phel ba med pa'i mtshan nyid do/_/sa bon gzhan du gyur pa'i phyir/_/gnas don lus su snang ba dag_/gzhan du gyur pas zag med dbyings/_/de ni rten kun 'gro ba can/_/yid dang 'dzin dang rnam par rtog_/gyur phyir rnam par mi rtog dang /_/zhing dang ye shes
[\[15a.3\]]las dag la/_/dbang ni rnam pa bzhi yin no/_/dbang de mi g.yo la sogs pa'i/_/sa gsum la ni rnam bzhi ste/_/gcig la rnam gnyis de las gzhan/_/dbang re rer ni 'dod pa yin/_/blo dang ldan pas srid rtogs bdag med rnam pa gnyi ka'ang rig 'gyur la/_/de
[\[15a.4\]]yang mnyam par shes nas de ni 'dzin pa'i sgo nas de nyid 'jug_/de nas de la yid gnas phyir na de la de yang mi snang ngo /_/de ni snang ba grol ba yin te mchog tu dmigs dang bral ba'o/_/tshogs kyi gzhi dang bskyed yod na/_/ming tsam du ni mthong bar 'gyur/_/ming tsam
[\[15a.5\]]mthong ste der mthong nas/_/de yang phyi nas mi mthong ngo /_/sems ni gnas ngan len dang bcas/_/bdag lta'i zhags pas zin par ni/_/rab tu 'jug par 'gyur te de/_/nang du gnas phyir ldog par 'dod/_/rang dang rang gi bdag nyid du/_/med phyir rang gi ngo bo la/_/mi
[\[15a.6\]]gnas phyir dang bzung bzhin de/_/med phyir ngo bo nyid med 'dod/_/snga ma phyi ma'i rten yin pas/_/ngo bo nyid ni med pa yis/_/skye med 'gag med gzod nas zhi/_/rang bzhin mya ngan 'das pa 'grub/_/thog ma dang ni de nyid gzhan nyid dang /_/rang gi mtshan nyid rang dang
[\[15a.7\]]gzhan du 'gyur/_/kun nas nyon mongs pa dang khyad par la/_/skye ba med pa'i chos la bzod par bshad/_/chos dang bdag med grol ba rnams/_/mtshungs phyir rigs ni tha dad phyir/_/bsam gnyis thob phyir sprul pa'i phyir/_/mthar thug phyir ni theg
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]gcig nyid/_/kha cig dag ni drang phyir dang /_/gzhan dag yang dag gzung ba'i phyir/_/rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis ni/_/ma nges rnams la theg gcig bshad/_/nyan thos ma nges rnam gnyis te/_/theg don mthong dang ma mthong ba'o/_/don mthong 'dod
[\[15b.2\]]chags bral ba dang /_/'dod chags bral min 'di dman pa'o/_/de gnyis 'phags pa'i lam thob pa/_/srid pa dag tu sgyur ba'i phyir/_/bsam gyis mi khyab sgyur ba yi/_/skye ba dang ni yang dag ldan/_/gcig ni smon lam dbang gis na/_/skye ba rab tu sgrub
[\[15b.3\]]par byed/_/cig shos phyir mi 'ong ba dang /_/ldan phyir sprul pas rab tu sgrub/_/de gnyis yang dang yang du ni/_/rang sems kun du 'byung ldan pas/_/mya ngan 'das la mngon dga'i phyir/_/rtogs pa bul ba yin par 'dod/_/don byas ma yin de sangs
[\[15b.4\]]rgyas/_/med par skyes nas sprul don gnyer/_/bsam gtan don brtson der brten nas/_/byang chub dam pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/rig pa'i gnas lnga dag la brtson par ma byas na/_/'phags mchog gis kyang thams cad mkhyen nyid mi 'gyur te/_/de lta
[\[15b.5\]]bas na gzhan dag tshar bcad rjes gzung dang /_/bdag nyid kun shes bya phyir de la de brtson byed/_/rgyu dmigs nas ni dga' ba dang /_/rten la de rjes dran pa dang /_/'bras bu thun mong 'dod pa dang /_/ji ltar byang chub bzhin mos pa'o/_/mthu ni rnam pa bzhi dag gis/_/
[\[15b.6\]]dka' dang nges par mi skyo dang /_/mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po la/_/sgrub pa rnam pa bzhi yin no/_/rab dang yang dag nod pa dang /_/gzhan la sbyin par 'dun pa dang /_/go cha dang ni smon lam dang /_/mngon par dga' dang bya ba'i yid/_/sbyin sogs rnam pa drug la
[\[15b.7\]]ni/_/mthu thob pa dang yongs smin dang /_/mchod pa dang ni sten pa la/_/yang dag spro ba mchog dang brtse/_/ma byas ngan par byas pa la/_/ngo tsha 'gyod dang yul la dga'/_/skyo la dgra bo'i 'du shes dang /_/'gong dang brjod pa'i blo gros so/_/sbyin sogs
[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi/_/rten yin dbang phyug la sogs min/_/gnyis po dag la skyon dang ni/_/yon tan so so yang dag rig_/bsags pa rjes su dran pa yis/_/dga' dang don chen mthong ba dang /_/rnal 'byor rnam par mi rtog dang /_/
[\[16a.2\]]de 'dzin byed dang phrad 'dod pa/_/log par 'dzin pa rnam pa bdun/_/spong ba'i mthu ni thob pa dang /_/ngo mtshar ngo mtshar med pa la/_/'du shes rnam pa bzhi nyid do/_/sems can rnams la snyoms pa dang /_/bdag nyid chen po mthong ba dang /_/gzhan gyi yon tan
[\[16a.3\]]lan re dang /_/gsum du smon dang rgyun du'o/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa bsgrub pa'i phyir/_/tshu rol mi gnas sems pa dang /_/des sman dar ba'i sems can la/_/mi dga' ba dang rab dga' ba'o/_/bsgom pa bcos dang yang dag la/_/ma dad pa dang dad pa dang /_/
[\[16a.4\]]dang du mi len yid byed dang /_/lung bstan nges par dga' ba'o/_/phyi ma'i tshe la mthong ba'i phyir/_/'jug sems mnyam par blta ba'i phyir/_/mchog chos rnams la zhugs pa yis/_/bdag nyid mchog tu nges 'dzin phyir/_/pha rol phyin bcu'i rgyus byung
[\[16a.5\]]ba/_/dge ba yid la byed 'di dag_/rtag tu byang chub sems dpa' yi/_/khams ni rtas par byed pa yin/_/rgyas dang lhag pa'i bsam dang chen po ni/_/brten pa'i yongs su tshol ba yin par 'dod/_/de dag gi ni spang dang bcas pa dang /_/spang bya med dang de
[\[16a.6\]]bzhin dbang 'byor pa'o/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshol ba ni/_/sku med pa dang sku bcas sku thob dang /_/sku yongs rdzogs dang nga rgyal mang ba dang /_/nga rgyal phra dang nga rgyal med par 'dod/_/brtan chos gzugs dang gzugs min la/_/mtshan dang de
[\[16a.7\]]bzhin nad med dang /_/mngon shes rnams kyi dbang phyug dang /_/de zad mi shes nyid kyi rgyu/_/rgyal ba'i sras rnams kyis ni yod dang med pa dang /_/sgro 'dogs skur ba'i rtog dang gcig dang du ma nyid/_/rang dang khyad par rtog dang ming don ji bzhin du/_/mngon par
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]zhen pa'i rtog pa yang dag spang bar bya/_/de ltar blo gros dge ba brtson 'grus drag rten nas/_/de bzhin nyid bcas gnyis kyi chos nyid yongs btsal ba/_/de phyir rtag tu skye dgu rnams kyi ston par 'gyur/_/de ni rgya mtsho bzhin du yon tan rnams kyis gang /_/theg
[\[16b.2\]]pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_yongs su tshol ba'i le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o//_//brtan pa rnams ni srog dang longs spyod tshegs ches rnyed cing snying po med pa dag_/rab dga'i yid kyis sems can sdug bsngal rnams la sbyin rnams rgya chen rtag
[\[16b.3\]]gtong na/_/chos yangs skye dgu rnams la rnam pa kun du phan byed tshegs ches rnyed min zhing /_/shin tu btang yang zad med 'phel 'gyur ba lta lan cig ma yin smos ci dgos/_/gang phyir so so rang rig bya phyir bcom ldan 'das kyis chos ma bstan/_/thugs
[\[16b.4\]]rje'i bdag nyid sprul chen lta bus rigs bshad dbugs 'dra'i chos rnams kyis/_/skye bo nyid kyi chos la kun nas drangs te nyer zhi zhal gyi sgo/_/rnam par dag pa rgya chen thun mong zad mi shes la yang dag bkod/_/de ltas rnal 'byor can gyi sgom pa
[\[16b.5\]]gang yin de ni don med min/_/de ltar bde bar gshegs kyi bstan pa gang yin de yang don med min/_/gal te thos pa tsam gyis don mthong 'gyur na sgom pa don med 'gyur/_/gal te ma thos par yang bsgom 'jug 'gyur na bstan pa don med 'gyur/_/sems
[\[16b.6\]]dpa' mchog gi ston pa ni/_/lung dang rtogs dang dbang 'byor las/_/kha dang gzugs ni thams cad dang /_/nam mkha' las kyang 'byung ba yin/_/rgya che the tshom spong ba dang /_/gzung 'os de nyid gnyis ston pa/_/'di ni byang chub sems dpa' yi/_/
[\[16b.7\]]ston pa phun tshogs yin zhes bya/_/sems dpa' mchog gi ston pa ni/_/'jam zhing rgyags bral mi skyo dang /_/gsal zhing sna tshogs rigs pa dang /_/go zhing zang zing med kun 'gro/_/rgyal sras tshig ni mi zhen pa/_/snyan cing legs bshad grags pa dang /_/
[\[17a\]]
[\[17a.1\]]ci rigs pa dang zang zing med/_/ran cing de bzhin yangs pa yin/_/bstan dang de bzhin bshad pa dang /_/theg dang mthun dang bde ba dang /_/grags pa dang ni ci rigs dang /_/nges par 'byung dang mthun pa'i phyir/_/de mdor sems dpa' mchog
[\[17a.2\]]rnams kyi/_/yi ge phun tshogs yin zhes bya/_/bde gshegs gsungs ni mtha' yas te/_/yan lag drug cu bsam mi khyab/_/ngag tshig shin tu rigs pa dang /_/brten dang rnam 'byed the tshom gcod/_/lan mang byed dang ldan pa ni/_/mgo smos rnam spros go
[\[17a.3\]]rnams la/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyi ston pa 'di/_/'khor gsum gyis ni dag pa ste/_/'di ni nyes pa brgyad dag dang /_/bral ba nyid du shes par bya/_/le lo dang ni mi go ba/_/skabs mi 'byed dang ma nges dang /_/the tshom dag ni mi gcod dang /_/de dang bral bar brten
[\[17a.4\]]mi byed/_/skyo ba dang ni ser sna nyid/_/'di dag gtam gyis nyes par 'dod/_/de dag med phyir sangs rgyas kyi/_/bshad pa bla na med par 'gyur/_/dad dang dga' dang blo rnams kyi/_/rgyu phyir chos 'di dge ba yin/_/don rnam gnyis ldan gzung bla dang /_/yon
[\[17a.5\]]tan gzhi can tshangs spyod ston/_/gzhan dag thun mong ma yin ldan pa dang /_/khams gsum nyon mongs rnam spong rdzogs byed dang /_/ngo bo nyid dag dri mas dag pa ste/_/tshangs spyod yon tan bzhi ldan yin par 'dod/_/gzhug pa ldem por dgongs pa dang /_/mtshan
[\[17a.6\]]nyid ldem por dgongs pa dang /_/gnyen po ldem por dgongs pa dang /_/bsgyur ba ldem por dgongs pa ste/_/nyan thos dang ni ngo bo nyid/_/de bzhin nyes pa 'dul ba dang /_/brjod pa zab pa nyid la ni/_/ldem por dgongs pa 'di rnam bzhi/_/mnyam pa nyid
[\[17a.7\]]dang don gzhan dang /_/de bzhin du ni dus gzhan dang /_/gang zag gi ni bsam pa la/_/dgongs pa rnam pa bzhir shes bya/_/sangs rgyas chos la brnyas pa dang /_/le lo cung zad chog 'dzin dang /_/nga rgyal 'dod chags spyod pa dang /_/'gyod dang ma nges ldog pa
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]ni/_/sems can rnams kyi sgrib pa ste/_/de yi gnyen por theg mchog gsungs/_/des de'i bar du gcod pa yi/_/nyes pa thams cad spong bar 'gyur/_/gang zhig tshig gam don sgo nas/_/tshigs bcad gnyis 'dzin rab sbyor ba/_/sems can blo ldan mchog de yis/_/
[\[17b.2\]]yon tan rnam bcu thob 'gyur te/_/khams ni zad par rtas pa dang /_/'chi ba'i tshe na rab dga' mchog_/ji ltar 'dod par skye ba dang /_/kun du tshe rabs dran pa dang /_/sangs rgyas rnams dang 'phrad pa dang /_/de las theg mchog thos pa dang /_/mos pa blo dang bcas
[\[17b.3\]]pa dang /_/sgo gnyis byang chub myur thob pa'o/_/de ltar blo bzang skyo ba med ldan brtse ba can/_/snyan pa rab grags cho ga bzang shes ldan pa yi/_/byang chub sems dpa' legs par smra ba yin pa ste/_/bshad pas skye bo'i nang na nyi ma bzhin du lham/_/theg pa
[\[17b.4\]]chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_bshad pa'i le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o//_//blo ldan gnyis la log nyid dang /_/yang dag nyid rnam spangs gsum gyis/_/gang zag dang ni chos dag la/_/bdag med rnam gnyis kun shes nas/_/don shes pa ni chos
[\[17b.5\]]rnams kun/_/gzings dang 'dra ba nyid du rig_/thos pas chog par 'dzin spong ba/_/des na chos shes pa zhes brjod/_/so so skye bo'i shes pa yis/_/de bzhin du ni gnyis rtogs nas/_/shes pa de yongs rdzogs bya'i phyir/_/mthun pa'i chos ni rab tu sgrub/_/
[\[17b.6\]]de nas des ni sa dang por/_/byang chub sems dpa' de bdag nyid/_/kun dang mnyam par 'jig rten las/_/'das pa'i ye shes bla med 'thob/_/mthong bas spang bya'i nyon mongs rnams/_/thams cad yang dag zad byas nas/_/shes bya'i sgrib pa spang ba'i phyir/_/
[\[17b.7\]]bsgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor/_/rnam 'jog rnam par mi rtog pa'i/_/ye shes lhan cig spyod pa yis/_/de bzhin sa ni lhag ma la/_/mthun pa yi ni chos spyod do/_/blo ldan gang du sgrub pa'i yul/_/legs par rnyed dang gnas bzang dang /_/sa bzang ba dang grogs
[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]bzang dang /_/rnal 'byor bde ba'i yon tan ldan/_/byang chub sems dpa' thos mang dang /_/bden mthong smra mkhas brtse ba can/_/skyo med skyes bu dam pa ni/_/chen po yin par shes par bya/_/dmigs pa bzang dang ston pa bzang /_/thabs bzang ba
[\[18a.2\]]dang nges 'byung dang /_/sbyor ba bzang po'i bdag nyid kyi/_/yang dag gtod pa yin par bshad/_/dga' dang dal bar skye ba dang /_/nad med pa dang ting nge 'dzin/_/rnam par 'byed pa'i byed rgyu ni/_/sngon chad bsod nams byas pa nyid/_/chos kyi dbyings ni ma gtogs
[\[18a.3\]]pa/_/gang phyir chos med de yi phyir/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyis de dag las/_/nges 'byung chags sogs yin par dgongs/_/chos kyi dbyings ni ma gtogs par/_/gang phyir chos med de yi phyir/_/kun nas nyon mongs bstan pa la/_/blo ldan dgongs pa de yin 'dod/_/
[\[18a.4\]]gang phyir chags sogs de nyid la/_/tshul bzhin 'jug pa de yi phyir/_/de las rnam grol 'gyur des na/_/de yis de dag las nges 'byung /_/sems can ched du dmyal ba'i srid par gnas pa yi/_/sdug bsngal mi bzad cis kyang rgyal sras gnod byed min/_/zhi srid
[\[18a.5\]]yon tan skyon gyis theg pa dman zhugs pa'i/_/rnam rtog dge ba sna tshogs blo ldan gnod byed yin/_/blo dang ldan pa dmyal bar gnas pa dus kun du/_/byang chub dri med yangs pa'i bar du gcod byed min/_/theg pa gzhan la rab bsil rnam rtog bdag phan pa/_/
[\[18a.6\]]rab tu bde bar gnas kyang bar du gcod par byed/_/chos med pa dang dmigs pa dang /_/kun nas nyon mongs med rnam dag_/sgyu ma la sogs 'dra ba dang /_/de bzhin nam mkha' 'drar shes bya/_/ji ltar tshul bzhin bris pa'i ri mo la/_/mtho dman med kyang
[\[18a.7\]]snang ba de bzhin du/_/yang dag ma yin rtog la rnam kun du/_/gnyis po rtag tu med kyang snang bar 'gyur/_/ji ltar chu rnyog pa las dang ba ni/_/dang ba nyid de de las skyes min gyi/_/de ni de la dri ma bral bar zad/_/de bzhin rang sems dag la tshul de nyid/_/sems
[\[18b\]]
[\[18b.1\]]ni rtag tu rang bzhin 'od gsal 'dod/_/de ni glo bur nyes pas ma rungs byas/_/chos nyid sems las gzhan pa'i sems gzhan ni/_/'od gsal ma yin rang bzhin la brjod do/_/byang chub sems dpa' sems can la/_/bu gcig pa la bya ba bzhin/_/rkang gi khong nas byams pa che/_/de
[\[18b.2\]]ltas rtag phan byed par 'dod/_/sems can rnams la phan byed phyir/_/de la chags skyes ltung mi 'gyur/_/'di yi zhe sdang rnam kun du/_/sems can kun dang 'gal bar 'gyur/_/ji ltar phug ron rang gi bu mchog byams/_/rang gi bu de nye bar 'khyud nas 'dug_/de 'dra ba la khong khro
[\[18b.3\]]'gal ba ltar/_/brtser bcas lus can bu la'ang de dang 'dra/_/gang phyir byams pa de phyir khong khro 'gal/_/gang phyir zhi ba de phyir gnod sems 'gal/_/gang phyir don byed de phyir sgyu sems 'gal/_/gang phyir sim byed de phyir 'jigs byed 'gal/_/sman bzang po la nad pa
[\[18b.4\]]bzhin/_/'khor ba la ni 'jug par byed/_/nad pa la ni sman pa bzhin/_/sems can rnams la sgrub par byed/_/bran ma grub pa ji bzhin du/_/bdag nyid la ni sgrub par byed/_/zong la tshong ba ji bzhin du/_/'dod pa dag la sgrub par byed/_/gos la btso blag mkhan bzhin
[\[18b.5\]]du/_/las la rab tu sgrub par byed/_/bu gzhon pa la pha bzhin du/_/sems can mi 'tsho sgrub par byed/_/me don gnyer la gtsub shing ltar/_/rtag par rab tu sgrub par byed/_/yid brtan bzhin du lhag pa'i sems/_/ma rdzogs pa la sgrub par byed/_/sgyu ma
[\[18b.6\]]mkhan ltar shes bya la/_/shes rab kyis ni sgrub par byed/_/de ni byang chub sems dpa' yi/_/ji ltar gong du sgrub par 'dod/_/de ltar rtag tu brtson 'grus rgya chen ldan/_/gnyis yongs smin par bya la rab brtson de/_/rim gyis dri med mi rtog blo mchog
[\[18b.7\]]gis/_/sgrub pa bla na med par rab tu 'gro/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_sgrub pa'i le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o//_//bskal pa grangs med nges 'byung zhing /_/mos pa rnam par 'phel byed pa/_/ji ltar chu yis rgya mtsho bzhin/_/dge chos rnams kyis yang
[\[19a\]]
[\[19a.1\]]dag rdzogs/_/de bzhin du ni tshogs bsags pa'i/_/rgyal sras gzod nas dag pa po/_/legs par shes shing sems dge ba/_/bsgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor/_/de tshe chos kyi rgyun la ni/_/sangs rgyas rnams las zhi gnas dang /_/ye shes yangs pa thob bya'i phyir/_/gdams ngag rgya chen rnyed par
[\[19a.2\]]'gyur/_/de nas dang por sdom brtson de/_/mdo yi sde la sogs pa'i chos/_/mi gnyis don ni rnam 'byed pa/_/mdo sogs ming la sems 'jog go/_/de nas de ni rim bzhin du/_/tshig rab dbye la dpyod byed cing /_/so so'i nang la tshul bzhin du/_/de yi don yang rnam par dpyod/_/don de dag
[\[19a.3\]]ni nges bzung nas/_/chos la kun nas sdom par byed/_/de yi don ni thob bya'i phyir/_/de nas de ni smon par byed/_/yid kyi brjod pas rgyun chags su/_/btsal bya so sor brtag par bya/_/yid la byed pa brjod med par/_/ro gcig pas kyang dpyad par bya/_/chos kyi ming ni bsdoms pa'ang 'di/_/
[\[19a.4\]]zhi gnas lam du shes par bya/_/lhag mthong lam ni de'i don rnams/_/rnam par dpyod par shes par bya/_/zung du 'brel ba'i lam ni de/_/bsdoms pa yin par shes par bya/_/zhum pa'i sems ni rab gzung ste/_/rgod pa yang ni zhi bar bya/_/de nas dmigs pa de la ni/_/mnyam par gyur na btang
[\[19a.5\]]snyoms gzhag_/de la rtag tu bya ba dang /_/gus par bya ste sbyar bar bya/_/dmigs pa la ni sems gtad nas/_/de'i rgyun rnam par g.yeng mi bya/_/rnam g.yeng myur du rtogs byas nas/_/de la slar ni blan par bya/_/blo ldan gong nas gong du yang /_/sems ni nang du bsdu bar bya/_/de nas yon tan
[\[19a.6\]]mthong ba'i phyir/_/ting nge 'dzin la sems gdul lo/_/rnam g.yeng nyes pa mthong ba'i phyir/_/de la mi dga' zhi bar bya/_/brnab sems yid mi bde la sogs/_/langs pa de bzhin zhi bar bya/_/de nas sdom brtson can gyis ni/_/sems la mngon par 'du byed bcas/_/rang gi ngang gis 'byung ba
[\[19a.7\]]'thob/_/de goms pa las 'du mi byed/_/de nas de yis lus dang sems/_/shin tu sbyangs pa che thob nas/_/yid la byed dang bcas shes bya/_/de yis de ni 'phel byas nas/_/'phel ba ring du 'gro ba yis/_/dngos gzhi'i gnas pa des 'thob bo/_/mngon shes don du gnyer bas de/_/sbyangs nas
[\[19b\]]
[\[19b.1\]]las su rung ba'i mchog_/bsam gtan las 'thob mngon par shes/_/mngon par bsgrubs pa'i sgo nas de/_/sangs rgyas dpag tu med pa la/_/mchod pa'i phyir dang mnyan pa'i phyir/_/'jig rten khams ni rnams su 'gro/_/'dis ni sangs rgyas dpag med la/_/bskal dpag med par bsnyen bkur byas/_/de
[\[19b.2\]]la bsnyen bkur byas pa'i phyir/_/sems ni las rung mchog tu 'gyur/_/des na de dag sngon rol du/_/phan yon lnga ni 'thob 'gyur te/_/des ni rnam par dag pa'i snod/_/bla na med pa nyid 'gyur 'di'i/_/lus la gnas ngan len pa kun/_/skad cig re re la zad 'gyur/_/lus dang sems ni kun du yang /_/shin tu
[\[19b.3\]]sbyangs pas gang bar 'gyur/_/chos rnams snang ba thams cad du/_/yongs su chad pa med rtogs 'gyur/_/yang dag pa yi rgyu mtshan ni/_/ma brtags pa dag rab tu mthong /_/de bzhin chos sku rab rdzogs dang /_/rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir/_/blo dang ldan pa rnam kun du/_/rtag tu rgyu yongs 'dzin par byed/_/
[\[19b.4\]]de nas de 'drar gyur pa yi/_/byang chub sems dpa' mnyam gzhag pas/_/yid kyi brjod pa ma gtogs par/_/don kun rab tu mi mthong ngo /_/chos kyi snang ba 'phel bya'i phyir/_/brtson 'grus brtan pa kun du brtsam/_/chos kyi snang ba 'phel nas ni/_/sems tsam la ni gnas par 'gyur/_/de nas don
[\[19b.5\]]du snang ba kun/_/sems su rab tu snang bar 'gyur/_/de tshe de yi gzung ba yi/_/rnam par g.yeng ba de spangs 'gyur/_/de nas de la 'dzin pa yi/_/rnam par g.yeng ba 'ba' zhig lus/_/de tshe bar chad med pa yi/_/ting nge 'dzin la myur du reg_/'di ltar de yi mjug thogs su/_/
[\[19b.6\]]'dzin pa'i rnam par g.yeng ba spong /_/'di dag go rims bzhin du ni/_/dro bar 'gyur sogs yin shes bya/_/de nas des ni 'jig rten las/_/'das pa'i ye shes bla med pa/_/rnam par mi rtog dri ma med/_/'dzin pa gnyis dang bral ba 'thob/_/de 'di'i gnas yongs gyur pa ste/_/
[\[19b.7\]]sa ni dang po yin par 'dod/_/de 'di bskal pa dpag med kyis/_/shin tu rnam par dag par 'gyur/_/chos kyi dbyings ni mnyam pa nyid/_/rab tu rtogs nas de yi tshe/_/rtag tu sems can thams cad la/_/bdag dang mtshungs pa'i sems 'thob ste/_/sems can rnams la bdag med dang /_/sdug bsngal dang ni don
[\[20a\]]
[\[20a.1\]]bya dang /_/lan la mi re 'di sems snyoms/_/rgyal sras gzhan dang 'dra ba yin/_/des ni khams gsum 'dus byas rnams/_/yang dag ma yin kun rtog par/_/ye shes shin tu rnam dag pa/_/gnyis su med pa'i don gyis mthong /_/
[\[20a.2\]]de dag med pa'i ngo bo nyid/_/mthong bas spang bya rnams las grol/_/des na de tshe mthong ba'i lam/_/thob pa zhes ni nges par brjod/_/med pa'i stong pa nyid shes shing /_/de bzhin yod pa'i stong nyid dang /_/rang bzhin stong pa nyid shes pas/_/stong pa shes
[\[20a.3\]]pa zhes brjod do/_/mtshan med bzhi ni rnam rtog rnams/_/yang dag zad pa yin zhes bya/_/smon pa med par gyur pa'i de/_/yang dag ma yin kun rtog go/_/rgyal sras byang chub phyogs mthun pa/_/rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad ni/_/rtag tu mthong ba'i lam
[\[20a.4\]]de dang /_/lhan cig tu ni thob par 'dod/_/gang zhig blo yis 'gro ba 'dus byas tsam/_/bdag med sdug bsngal rgyas pa tsam shes te/_/don med rang bzhin bdag lta rnam spangs nas/_/bdag nyid che lta don chen rnyed pa gang /_/'di ni bdag lta med par
[\[20a.5\]]bdag tu lta/_/sdug bsngal med par shin tu sdug bsngal 'gyur/_/rang la phan byas bdag la ji lta bar/_/don kun byed la lan kyang re ba med/_/gang zhig grol ba mchog gis sems grol la/_/'ching ba mi zad yun yang ring por bcings/_/sdug bsngal
[\[20a.6\]]mthar thug pa ni ma mthong yang /_/rab tu sbyor ba nyid dang byed pa nyid/_/'jig rten tshe gcig rang sdug bkur mi nus/_/'jig rten gnas pa srid du gzhan sdug bsngal/_/bsdoms pa smos ci dgos te bsam du med/_/byang chub sems dpa' de las bzlog pa
[\[20a.7\]]yin/_/rgyal sras sems can rnams la dga' ba dang /_/byams pa gang yin sbyor dang mi skyo gang /_/de ni srid pa dag na ngo mtshar che/_/sems can bdag dang mtshungs phyir de lta'ang min/_/de nas de ni lhag ma yi/_/sa rnams bsgom pa'i lam 'di la/_
[\[20b\]]
[\[20b.1\]]ye shes rnam pa gnyis po dag_/bsgom phyir rab tu sbyong bar byed/_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes de/_/sangs rgyas chos ni sbyong bar byed/_/gzhan ni ji bzhin rnam 'jog pa/_/sems can rnams ni yongs smin byed/_/grangs med gnyis ni rdzogs pa yis/_/
[\[20b.2\]]bsgom pa yi ni tshar phyin te/_/bsgom pa tha ma thob nas ni/_/byang chub sems dpa' dbang bskur ba/_/rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin/_/rtog pas mi shigs thob nas ni/_/gnas gzhan gyur pas mthar thug pa/_/sgrib pa kun gyi dri med pa/_/gang la gnas nas
[\[20b.3\]]sems can kun/_/phan phyir rab tu sgrub byed pa/_/rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa yi/_/go 'phang bla na med pa 'thob/_/de ltar mthong dka'i thub pa rtag mthong ba/_/thos pa mnyam med las byung rab dang ba'i/_/shugs kyis rtag par shin tu sems tshim
[\[20b.4\]]la/_/ji lta bur na don chen 'gyur ma yin/_/chos kyi sgo la rnam par gnas pa la/_/de bzhin gshegs rtag mngon sum 'doms mdzad cing /_/co nas 'dren bzhin nyes pa'i tshang tshing nas/_/mtshan gyis drangs te byang chub la dgod do/_/sangs rgyas
[\[20b.5\]]rnams ni rtag tu rang don yang dag sbyor la legs par bsngags pa dang /_/log par sbyor la smod mdzad gnas dang rnam 'byed lhur len mchog gi sems can la/_/gang zhig spangs dang bsten pas bde gshegs bstan pa 'di la rnal 'byor yangs 'gyur ba/_/
[\[20b.6\]]bar chad mthun pa'i chos ni rnam pa thams cad rgyal rnams tshul bzhin 'di na ston/_/de ni mthong ba rab dag mi rtog byang chub kyis/_/'jig rten thams cad zil mnan mun pa chen po yang /_/rnam pa kun tu bsal nas nyi ma chen po dag_/shar ba bzhin du 'gro ba rnams
[\[20b.7\]]la lam me'o/_/de ltar rtag tu dge ba bsags pas rab gang zhing /_/thub pa las ni rtag tu gdams ngag che thob pa'i/_/sems dpa' mchog ni sems kyi ting 'dzin rab yangs pa/_/thob nas yon tan rgya mtsho'i pha rol 'gro bar 'gyur/_/theg pa chen po
[\[21a\]]
[\[21a.1\]]mdo sde'i rgyan las/_gdams ngag rjes su bstan pa'i le'u ste bco lnga pa'o//_//sdom ni/_mos pa mang ba nyid dang ni/_/chos tshol ba dang bshad pa dang /_/de bzhin sgrub dang yang dag pa'i/_/gdams ngag rjes su bstan pa
[\[21a.2\]]yin/_/ji ltar nags tshal dang ni lus can ri bo dang /_/chu bo rnams kyi rten ni kun nas sa yin pa/_/de bzhin mkhas pa rnams kyi las rnam gsum po yang /_/kun nas sbyin pa la sogs dge ba'i yin par brjod/_/shin tu dka' ba'i las ni ngo bo sna tshogs
[\[21a.3\]]pa/_/bskal ba mang pos tshar phyin mngon brtson bdag nyid can/_/rgyal sras rnams ni lus dang ngag sems rang bzhin gyi/_/las rnams dag gis 'di na yid 'byung 'gyur ba med/_/ji ltar bdag la phan 'dod dug dang mtshon dang ni/_/gnam lcags lce dang dgra
[\[21a.4\]]las rang gi lus zlog pa/_/de bzhin rgyal sras theg pa dman pa rnam gnyis las/_/las rnam gsum gyi bdag nyid zlog par byed pa yin/_/rtag tu rnam par mi rtog las can las min zhing /_/las kyi bya ba dang rnam gsum la mi lta ste/_/des na 'di ni de'i thabs yang
[\[21a.5\]]dag gzung ba'i phyir/_/las rnams dag pa mtha' yas de yi pha rol 'gro/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_thabs dang ldan pa'i las kyi le'u ste bcu drug pa'o//_//grangs dang de yi mtshan nyid go rims dang /_/nges pa'i tshig dang yon tan goms bya dang /_/de dag
[\[21a.6\]]rab dbye bsdu dang mi mthun phyogs/_/yon tan phan tshun rnam nges yin zhes bya/_/longs spyod dang lus phun sum tshogs pa dang /_/'khor rtsom phun sum tshogs pa mngon mtho dang /_/rtag tu nyon mongs dbang nyid mi 'gro dang /_/bya ba rnams la phyin ci ma
[\[21a.7\]]log pa'o/_/sems can don la rab brtson pa/_/gtong dang mi gnod bzod pas byed/_/gnas dang grol ba bzhir bcas pa/_/rang don rnam pa thams cad spyod/_/mi 'phongs pa dang rnam par mi 'tshe dang /_/rnam 'tshe bzod dang bya bas mi skyo dang /_/dga' byed
[\[21b\]]
[\[21b.1\]]legs par brjod pa de yi phyir/_/gzhan gyi don ni rang gi don yin no/_/longs spyod mngon par mi dga' dang /_/rab gus gnyis la mi skya dang /_/rnal 'byor rnam par mi rtog pa/_/theg chen mtha' dag 'dir zad do/_/yul rnams la ni ma chags lam/_
[\[21b.2\]]de thob rnam g.yeng sdom pa'i gzhan/_/sems can mi gtong 'phel ba dang /_/sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i gzhan/_/bslab gsum dbang du mdzad nas ni/_/rgyal bas pha rol phyin pa drug_/yang dag bshad de dang po gsum/_/tha ma gnyis kyis rnam pa gnyis/_/
[\[21b.3\]]gcig ni gsum char la yang gtogs/_/sbyin pa mi mthun phyogs nyams dang /_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/_/sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/_/tshul khrims mi mthun phyogs nyams dang /_/
[\[21b.4\]]rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/_/sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/_/bzod pa mi mthun phyogs nyams dang /_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/_/sems can
[\[21b.5\]]rnam smin byed rnam gsum/_/brtson 'grus mi mthun phyogs nyams dang /_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/_/sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/_/bsam gtan mi mthun phyogs nyams dang /_/rnam par mi rtog
[\[21b.6\]]ye shes ldan/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/_/sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/_/shes rab mi mthun phyogs nyams dang /_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/_/sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/_/
[\[21b.7\]]snga ma la brten phyi ma skye/_/dman dang mchog tu gnas phyir dang /_/rags pa dang ni phra ba'i phyir/_/de dag rim par bstan pa yin/_/dbul ba 'dor bar byed pa dang /_/bsil ba 'thob dang khro bzod dang /_/mchog sbyor ba dang yid 'dzin dang /_/don dam
[\[22a\]]
[\[22a.1\]]shes pa'i phyir bshad do/_/thams cad bsgom pa dngos po dang /_/de bzhin yid la byed pa dang /_/bsam pa dang ni thabs dag dang /_/dbang sbyor nyid la rten par brjod/_/don rnams gtong bar byed pa dang /_/rtsa ba sems pa la
[\[22a.2\]]brten dang /_/lus dang longs spyod phun tshogs dang /_/gnyis rjes 'dzin dang rdzogs byed dang /_/de yang ser sna med ldan par/_/chos dang zang zing mi 'jigs gtong /_/sbyin pa de 'drar yongs shes nas/_/mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/_/yan
[\[22a.3\]]lag drug zhi bsam pas zin/_/bde 'gro gnas pa sbyin byed dang /_/rten dang zhi dang 'jigs pa med/_/bsod nams tshogs dang ldan pa dang /_/brdar brtags chos nyid thob pa ste/_/sdom la gnas pa rnams la yod/_/tshul khrims de 'drar yongs
[\[22a.4\]]shes nas/_/mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/_/mi mjed ji mi snyam shes dang /_/snying rjes chos la rten pa'i phyir/_/phan yon lngar ni yang dag bshad/_/de ni gnyis kyi don byed de/_/dka' thub gtso dang kun tu ldan/_/de la de ni rnam gsum 'dod/_/
[\[22a.5\]]bzod pa de 'drar yongs shes nas/_/mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/_/dge la yang dag spro ba dang /_/dad dang 'dun la rten pa dang /_/dran sogs yon tan 'phel byed dang /_/kun nas nyon mongs gnyen po dang /_/ma chags la sogs yon tan
[\[22a.6\]]ldan/_/de dag la ni de rnam bdun/_/brtson 'grus de 'drar yongs shes nas/_/mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/_/sems ni nang du gnas pa dang /_/dran dang brtson 'grus la brten pa/_/bde bskyed par byed pa dang /_/mngon shes gnas la dbang
[\[22a.7\]]bsgyur ba/_/chos rnams kyi ni gtso bo ste/_/de dag la yod de rnam gsum/_/bsam gtan de 'drar yongs shes nas/_/mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/_/shes bya yang dag rab rnam 'byed/_/ting nge 'dzin la rten pa dang /_/kun nas nyon mongs
[\[22b\]]
[\[22b.1\]]shin tu grol/_/shes rab 'tshe ba legs bshad dang /_/chos rnams kyi ni mchog yin te/_/de dag la yod de rnam gsum/_/shes rab de 'drar yongs shes nas/_/mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/_/dkar po'i chos kun rnam par g.yengs pa dang /_/
[\[22b.2\]]mnyam par gzhag dang gnyis kar shes par bya/_/pha rol phyin pa gnyis dang ni/_/gnyis dang gnyis kyis yongs su bsdus/_/byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa ni/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/_/ma chags mi
[\[22b.3\]]chags chags pa med/_/byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims ni/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/byang chub sems dpa'i bzod pa ni/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/
[\[22b.4\]]chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/byang chub sems dpa'i brtson 'grus ni/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/byang chub sems dpa'i bsam gtan
[\[22b.5\]]ni/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab ni/_/ma chags mi chags chags pa med/_/chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/_/ma chags mi
[\[22b.6\]]chags chags pa med/_/sangs rgyas sras rnams slong dang phrad na rang gi srog kyang rtag tu gtong /_/snying rjes gzhan las lan kyang mi re 'dod pa'i 'bras bu don mi gnyer/_/sbyin pa de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/_/sbyin pa ye shes
[\[22b.7\]]kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag_/sangs rgyas sras rnams sdom dang brtson pa'i rang bzhin tshul khrims gsum rtag blangs/_/mtho ris mngon par mi 'dod yang dag thob kyang de la chags mi skyed/_/tshul khrims de nyid kyis kyang skye bo
[\[23a\]]
[\[23a.1\]]thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/_/tshul khrims ye shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag_/sangs rgyas sras rnams shin tu bya dka' de bzhin mi yi gnod kun bzod/_/mtho ris gnyer dang mi nus pas min
[\[23a.2\]]'jigs pas ma yin phan ltas min/_/bzod pa bla na med pas skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/_/bzod pa ye shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag_/rgyal ba'i sras rnams go cha sbyor ba'i bdag nyid brtson 'grus dpe med
[\[23a.3\]]byas/_/rang dang gzhan gyi nyon mongs tshogs gzhom byang chub dam pa 'thob par byed/_/brtson 'grus de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/_/brtson 'grus ye shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag_/rgyal
[\[23a.4\]]ba'i sras rnams ting 'dzin mang ldan bsam gtan rnam pa thams cad bsgrubs/_/bsam gtan bde ba phul gyis gnas shing snying rjes skye ba dman la rten/_/bsam gtan de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/_/bsam gtan ye
[\[23a.5\]]shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag_/rgyal ba'i sras rnams de nyid shes bya gang yin mtha' dag rnam kun shes/_/mya ngan 'das la'ang blo yis chags rab mi skyed 'khor bar smos ci dgos/_/ye shes de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad
[\[23a.6\]]byang chub gsum la bkod/_/ye shes sems can yongs su gsung bas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag_/rgya che ba dang zang zing med/_/don che ba dang mi zad pa/_/sbyin la sogs pa thams cad kyi/_/yon tan bzhir ni shes par bya/_/slong ba mthong rdzogs
[\[23a.7\]]dga' ba dang /_/mi dga' ba dang smon pa dang /_/sbyin pa po ni brtser ldan pas/_/lhag par ldan pas rtag zil gnon/_/brtse bas sems can rnams la ni/_/srog dang longs spyod chung ma dag_/rtag gtong shin tu dga' byed pa/_/de spong ji ltar srung mi
[\[23b\]]
[\[23b.1\]]'gyur/_/'phags pa mi lta sems snyoms shing /_/mi 'jigs brtse phyir kun ster ba/_/gzhan la gnod par byed pa yis/_/log pa'i tshig ni ji ltar smra/_/snyoms par phan par 'dod pas brtse ba can/_/gzhan gyi sdug bsngal skye bas shin tu 'jigs/_/
[\[23b.2\]]sems can 'dul ba la ni sems brtson pa/_/ngag gi nyes rnam gsum las shin tu ring /_/thams cad gtong ba snying rje can/_/rten 'byung chos la rab mkhas pa/_/de ni yid kyi nyon mongs kun/_/ji lta bur na dang du len/_/brtser ldan gang tshe gnod pa
[\[23b.3\]]byed pa dang /_/gzhan la phan pa'i sdug bsngal la [(]rteg [,]rtag [)]tu/_/phan pa'i 'du shes dga' ba rnyed gyur pa/_/de yis gang la ci zhig bzod par bya/_/gzhan la gzhan gyi 'du shes bral ba dang /_/bdag pas ches lhag gzhan la rtag byams dang /_/dka' ba
[\[23b.4\]]spyod phyir brtse ba dang bcas la/_/brtson 'grus dka' ba min la shin tu dka'/_/gsum gyi bsam gtan bde ba chung /_/bdag bde gzhan pa yongs nyams 'gyur/_/zad 'gyur rmongs dang bcas par 'dod/_/byang chub sems dpa'i bzlog pa'o/_/
[\[23b.5\]]ji ltar mtshan mo lag nom dang /_/khebs sgron de bzhin shes pa gsum/_/snying rje can gyi shes pa ni/_/nyi ma'i zer bzhin mtshungs pa med/_/sbyin pa rten dang gzhi dang ni/_/rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang /_/gnas
[\[23b.6\]]kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/_/tshul khrims rten dang gzhi dang ni/_/rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang /_/gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/_/bzod pa rten dang gzhi dang ni/_/rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rgyu dang ye shes
