[\[23b.7\]]zhing dag dang /_/gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/_/brtson 'grus rten dang gzhi dang ni/_/rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang /_/gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/_/bsam gtan rten dang gzhi dang ni/_/rgyu mtshan dang
[\[24a\]]
[\[24a.1\]]ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang /_/gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/_/shes rab rten dang gzhi dang ni/_/rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang /_/gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/_/
[\[24a.2\]]byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa ni/_/sems can gcig bde bskal mang du/_/gnod pa byed kyang dga' 'gyur na/_/de las bzlog pa smos ci dgos/_/lus can rnams ni gang phyir nor 'dod pa/_/brtan rnams de nyid lus can rnams la gtong /_/skye bo
[\[24a.3\]]rnams ni lus phyir nor 'dod de/_/de nyid brtan rnams brgya phrag rnams su gtong /_/gang tshe lus nyid gtong yang yid sdug mi bsngal ba/_/de tshe rdzas ngan lta la smos kyang ci zhig dgos/_/de 'di'i 'jig rten 'das pa de des dga' 'gyur ba/_/gang yin de
[\[24a.4\]]ni de yi yang ni bla ma yin/_/ji ltar blo ldan 'di ni kun gtong bas/_/don gnyer skye bo dga' bas dga' ba ltar/_/de ltar slong mo ba dag blang bya ba/_/'dod dgu thob pa dag gis dgar mi 'gyur/_/blo can bdog dgu btang bas nor med pa/_/bdag nyid
[\[24a.5\]]nor ldan sems pa ji lta bar/_/slong ba longs spyod kun rdzogs bdag nyid ni/_/de ltar nor dang ldan par mi sems so/_/ji ltar blo ldan 'di ni sbyin pa bzang pos tshul bzhin du/_/don gnyer tshim byas de la phan chen 'dogs par sems pa ltar/_/de bzhin
[\[24a.6\]]slong mo ba dag shin du nor mang thob nas ni/_/sbyin pa po la rnyed pa'i rgyu yis drin du mi brtsi'o/_/lam ka'i 'bras mchog ldan pa'i shing las longs spyod ji lta bar/_/lus can rnams kyis gang gi nor rdzas rgya cher blangs nas ni/_/bdag nyid dogs dang bral
[\[24a.7\]]bar rang nyams spyod par byed pa la/_/btang dga' longs spyod can de byang chub sems dpa' las gzhan min/_/gtso dang de'i rgyu las kyi dbye ba dang /_rnam pa'i dbye brten gyi dbye ba dang /_/bar chad rnam bzhi'i gnyen po'i dbye ba yis/_/brtson 'grus
[\[24b\]]
[\[24b.1\]]yongs shes bya zhes rab tu bstan/_/dge ba'i tshogs kyi nang na brtson 'grus mchog_/'di ltar de la brten nas de rjes 'thob/_/brtson 'grus kyis ni mod la bde gnas mchog_/'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten gtogs pa 'grub/_/brtson 'grus
[\[24b.2\]]kyis ni srid spyod 'dod pa 'thob/_/brtson 'grus kyis ni dag pa rab 'gyur ldan/_/brtson 'grus kyis ni 'jig tshogs 'das nas grol/_/brtson 'grus kyis ni byang chub mchog sangs rgyas/_/gzhan yang nyams dang 'phel ba'i brtson 'grus dang /_/
[\[24b.3\]]thar pa'i dbang dang mi mthun phyogs spangs gzhan/_/de nyid rab zhugs yongs su sgyur byed dang /_/brtson 'grus don chen nges tshig gzhan du 'dod/_/thog mar dge ba'i brtson 'grus de nas ni/_/tshul bzhin rab zhugs sbyor ba'i brtson 'grus te/_/
[\[24b.4\]]ma zhum mi 'gong chog mi shes brtson 'grus/_/rnam pa thams cad sangs rgyas rnams rab gsungs/_/theg pa gsum brtson skye bo la brten nas/_/bsam blo zhan dang rgya rab che ldan phyir/_/brtson 'grus tha ma 'bring dang mchog gzhan te/_/de ni don
[\[24b.5\]]chung ba dang don chen 'dod/_/brtson 'grus ldan pa longs spyod kyis pham med/_/brtson 'grus ldan pa nyon mongs kyis pham med/_/brtson 'grus ldan pa skyo bas pham pa med/_/brtson 'grus ldan pa thob pas pham pa med/_/phan tshun bsdus phyir rab
[\[24b.6\]]dbye'i phyir/_/chos nyid phyir dang rgyu mtshan phyir/_/pha rol phyin drug rnam kun du/_/rnam par nges par shes par bya/_/sbyin mtshungs de ston len 'jug dang /_/bdag nyid rjes su 'jug rnams kyis/_/snyan par smra dang don spyod dang /_/don mthun nyid
[\[24b.7\]]du 'dod pa yin/_/phan par byed pa'i thabs dang ni/_/'dzin par byed dang 'jug byed dang /_/de bzhin rjes su 'jug byed pas/_/bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhir shes bya/_/dang pos snod 'gyur dngos po ste/_/gnyis pa yis ni mos pa yin/_/gsum pa yis
[\[25a\]]
[\[25a.1\]]ni sgrub pa ste/_/bzhi pas rnam par sbyong ba'o/_/zang zing dang ni chos kyi ste/_/dmigs pa'i chos la sogs pa yis/_/bsdu ba gnyis kyi sgo nas ni/_/bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhir 'dod do/_/rnam pa'i dbye ba'i sgo nas ni/_/bsdu ba
[\[25a.2\]]dman dang 'bring dang mchog_/phal cher don med don yod dang /_/rnam kun don yod shes par bya/_/'khor sdud pa dang ldan pa rnams/_/tshul 'di la ni yang dag rten/_/kun gyi don kun sgrub byed cing /_/thabs bzang yin par rab tu bsngags/_/bsdus
[\[25a.3\]]dang sdud par 'gyur ba dang /_/gang dag da ltar sdud byed pa/_/de kun de 'drar de lta bas/_/'di ni sems can smin byed lam/_/de ltar rtag tu longs spyod ma chags blo/_/zhi sdom brtson pa'i pha rol phyin gnas bdag_/srid yul mtshan ma rnam par mi rtog
[\[25a.4\]]pa/_/de ni sems can tshogs sdud byed pa yin/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_pha rol tu phyin pa dang bsdu ba'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o//_//rab dang sems dang ldan pa yis/_/tshogs gnyis rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/_/sangs
[\[25a.5\]]rgyas rnams la gos sogs kyis/_/mngon sum mngon sum min par mchod/_/sangs rgyas 'byung ba don yod par/_/smon lam dang ni ldan pa yi/_/gsum po dmigs par mi byed pa/_/sangs rgyas mchod pa rdzogs pa yin/_/sems can dag ni tshad
[\[25a.6\]]med pa/_/yongs su smin par byed pa gzhan/_/rdzas dang sems kyi sgo nas gzhan/_/mos pa dang ni smon pa dang /_/brtse dang bzod pa dag dang ni/_/yang dag spyod pa'i sgo dang ni/_/gzhi la gtod dang rtogs pa dang /_/grol dang de bzhin nyid kyis gzhan/_/
[\[25a.7\]]rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rten dang dngos dang rgyu dang ni/_/ye shes dang ni zhing dag dang /_/gnas kyi mchod pa rab bstan pa/_/rgyu dang 'bras bu nyid dang ni/_/bdag nyid dang ni gzhan dag dang /_/rnyed dang bkur sti nyid dang ni/_/sgrub pa'i sgo
[\[25b\]]
[\[25b.1\]]nas de rnam gnyis/_/mchod pa chung dang chen po de/_/nga rgyal bcas dang nga rgyal med/_/sbyor dang 'gro ba nyid dang ni/_/smon pa'i sgo nas der 'dod do/_/rang gi sems kyis sangs rgyas rnams mchod pa/_/chos la mos dang bsam dang dbang 'byor dang /_/rnam
[\[25b.2\]]par mi rtog thabs yongs bzung ba dang /_/kun dang don gcig nyid la 'jug pas mchog_/bsten pa rten dang gzhi dang ni/_/rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang /_/rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang /_/gnas kyi sgo nas rab tu bstan/_/bshes gnyen dul
[\[25b.3\]]ba zhi zhing nyer zhi ba/_/yon tan lhag pa brtson bcas lung gis phyug_/de nyid rab tu rtogs pa smra mkhas ldan/_/brtse ba'i bdag nyid skyo ba spangs la sten/_/bkur sti rnyed pa dag dang rim gro dang /_/sgrub pa'i sgo nas bshes gnyen bsten par bya/_/bsten
[\[25b.4\]]gzhi de bzhin blo ldan chos la ni/_/shes bsam dus su 'dud pas bshes gnyen bgrod/_/de ni bsnyen bkur rnyed la 'dod pa med/_/bsgrub par bya phyir de yongs sngo bar byed/_/brtan pa ji skad bstan pa sgrub pa des/_/de yi sems ni yang dag mgu
[\[25b.5\]]bar byed/_/theg pa gsum la mkhas pa blos rtogs nas/_/rang gi theg pa bsgrub par bya phyir 'bad/_/sems can tshad med yongs smin bya phyir dang /_/zhing dag pa yang sbyang bar bya ba'i phyir/_/de chos bgo skal la spyod yon tan ldan/_/bshes gnyen rab
[\[25b.6\]]tu bsten bya zang zing min/_/blo dang ldan pa rgyu dang 'bras bu dang /_/chos sgo rjes 'gro phyi dang thos mnyan dang /_/sems kyi rnal 'byor nga rgyal bcas pa dang /_/nga rgyal med yid ldan pas bshes gnyen bsten/_/blo ldan 'gro dang sbyor ba dang /_/smon pa'i sgo
[\[25b.7\]]nas bshes gnyen bsten/_/rang gi sems kyis bshes gnyen mchog bsten pa/_/chos la mos dang bsam dang dbang 'byor dang /_/rnam par mi rtog thabs yongs bzung ba dang /_/kun dang don gcig nyid la 'jug pas mchog_/brtan pa'i tshangs pa
[\[26a\]]
[\[26a.1\]]mi mthun spangs/_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/dmigs pa rnam pa gsum la 'jug_/sems can rnams ni yongs smin byed/_/brtan pa rnams kyi de dag bde 'dod dang /_/sdug bsngal gyis nyam thag dang bde ba dang /_/
[\[26a.2\]]nyon mongs can dang de dag bstan bcos dang /_/de yi de bzhin nyid la rab tu 'jug_/de don de bzhin nyid phyir dang /_/zhi ba thob pas dag phyir dang /_/las gnyis nyon mongs zad pa'i phyir/_/byams pa dmigs pa med pa yin/_/de dag g.yo dang mi
[\[26a.3\]]g.yo dang /_/chags pas ro myang min zhes bya/_/byang chub sems dpa' mi g.yo ba/_/chags dang bral bar rab tu gnas/_/mnyam gzhag ngo bo nyid min chung /_/'bring dang dman pa'i sa pa dang /_/bsam pa dman dang nga rgyal bcas/_/gang yin de
[\[26a.4\]]dman gzhan nyid lhag_/tshangs pa'i gnas pas gnas pa yi/_/blo ldan rtag tu 'dod par skye/_/des ni tshogs rnams rdzogs byed cing /_/sems can dag kyang rnam smin byed/_/kun du tshangs dang mi 'bral ba/_/de yi mi mthun phyogs dang bral/_/bag
[\[26a.5\]]med gyur kyang de yi rkyen/_/mi bzad pas kyang mi 'gyur ro/_/byang chub sems dpa' gnod sems dang /_/rnam 'tshe mi dga' gnod sems dang /_/'dod pa'i 'dod chags dang ldan pa/_/nyes dmigs rnam pa mang la reg_/nyon mongs kyis ni bdag
[\[26a.6\]]'joms sems can 'joms shing tshul khrims 'joms/_/nyams bcas snyed pas dman zhing srung dang de bzhin ston pas smad/_/rtsod bcas mi snyan de ni gzhan du mi khom rnams su skye/_/thob dang ma thob nyams pas yid la sdug bsngal chen po 'thob/_/
[\[26a.7\]]nyes pa 'di kun byams sogs la/_/legs par gnas la mi 'byung ste/_/nyon mongs can min sems can gyi/_/don du 'khor ba yongs mi gtong /_/ji ltar rgyal ba'i sras rnams sems can la/_/byams pa la sogs sems pa 'di 'byung ba/_/sems
[\[26b\]]
[\[26b.1\]]can thams cad yon tan ldan pa yi/_/bu gcig pa la'ang de lta ma yin no/_/rab 'bar dgra yi dbang du song /_/sdug bsngal gyis non mun pas bsgribs/_/bgrod dka'i lam la kun du zhugs/_/'ching ba che dang yang dag ldan/_/zas chen dug dang
[\[26b.2\]]'dres la zhen/_/lam ni rab tu stor gyur pa/_/lam gol rab zhugs stobs chung ba'i/_/sems can rnams la snying rje'o/_/'tshe spangs byang chub mchog gi sa bon dang /_/bde ba bskyed dang gdung byed 'dod pa'i rgyu/_/ngo bo nyid sbyin chos la rten pa yi/_/
[\[26b.3\]]rgyal ba'i sras la byang chub thag mi ring /_/snying rje blo mchog 'khor bar gtogs pa yi/_/sdug bsngal bdag nyid kun dang bdag med par/_/rnam par shes nas skyo bar mi 'gyur zhing /_/nyes pas rab gnod par yang mi 'gyur ro/_/'jig rten sdug bsngal
[\[26b.4\]]bdag nyid lta ba yi/_/brtse dang ldan pas sdug bsngal de dang ni/_/de yongs spong ba'i thabs kyang ji bzhin rig_/nyam nga bar byed skyo bar yang mi 'gyur/_/snying rje'i bdag nyid can gyi brtse ba 'di/_/rang bzhin dang ni so sor brtags pa dang /_/de sngon
[\[26b.5\]]goms par byas dang ldan pa dang /_/mi mthun phyogs nyams rnam dag thob pa bzhi/_/mnyam dang rtag min lhag pa'i bsam pas min/_/sgrub pa'i sgo dang 'dod chags bral ba dang /_/mi dmigs pas min gang de brtse min te/_/de bzhin brtse med gang de byang chub
[\[26b.6\]]min/_/snying rje dang ni bzod dang sems pa dang /_/smon lam skye ba sems can yongs smin byed/_/dang po rtsa ba tha ma 'bras mchog ldan/_/'di ni snying rje'i ljon shing chen po yin/_/rtsa ba snying rje med gyur na/_/dka' spyod bzod pa nyid mi 'gyur/_/blo ldan
[\[26b.7\]]sdug bsngal mi bzod na/_/sems can don sems nyid mi 'gyur/_/sems pa dang ni bral ba'i blo/_/skye ba dkar po rnam dag tu/_/smon lam 'debs par mi 'gyur ro/_/skye ba bzang po ma thob na/_/sems can yongs smin byed mi 'gyur/_/snying rje'i 'chu
[\[27a\]]
[\[27a.1\]]ba byams pa ste/_/de sdug bsngal na bde ba yis/_/sangs rgyas tshul bzhin yid byed pas/_/yal ga rgya chen 'phel ba dang /_/smon lam rgyun ni ma bcad pas/_/lo ma 'dor len rkyen rnam gnyis/_/grub pa de phyir me tog dang /_/'bras
[\[27a.2\]]bu don yod shes par bya/_/snying rje chen po yon tan 'byung gnas kyi/_/sems can rnams la snying rje su mi byed/_/'di ltar 'di dag la ni sdug bsngal yang /_/brtses bskyed bde ba gzhal du med pa 'byung /_/snying rjes zin pa'i brtser ldan rnams/_/zhi la'ang
[\[27a.3\]]yid ni mi gnas na/_/'jig rten bde dang rang srog la/_/chags par 'gyur ba smos ci dgos/_/byams pa gang de kha na ma tho ba/_/med dang 'jig rten 'das pa yod ma yin/_/blo ldan rnams kyi brtse bas byams pa ni/_/kha na ma tho med cing 'jig rten 'das/_/
[\[27a.4\]]sdug bsngal rba rgal che dang mi shes pa'i/_/mun pa che la rten par gyur pa yi/_/'jig rten 'dren pa'i thabs gang yin pa de/_/ji ltar kha na ma tho med mi 'gyur/_/'jig rten byang chub rang sangs rgyas pa yi/_/dgra bcom rnams la byams pa de med na/_/de las
[\[27a.5\]]gzhan la smos kyang ci dgos pa/_/ji ltar 'jig rten 'das pa ma yin 'gyur/_/byang chub sems dpa' sdug bsngal med/_/brtse bas sdug bsngal gyur pa gang /_/de la dang por kun tu skrag_/reg nas shin tu mngon par dga'/_/brtse bas bskyed pa'i
[\[27a.6\]]sdug bsngal 'jig rten gyi/_/bde ba thams cad zil gyis gnon 'gyur zhing /_/don byas rnams kyang de dang mi ldan gang /_/de las ngo mtshar che ba ci zhig yod/_/brtan pa'i brtse dang ldan pa'i sbyin pa yis/_/sbyin pa'i bde ba byed pa gang yin pa/_/de la
[\[27a.7\]]khams gsum nye bar spyad rnams kyi/_/bde ba de yis char yang mi phod do/_/sems can don phyir brtse bas sdug bsngal gyi/_/rang bzhin 'khor ba gang yin mi gtong na/_/snying rje can rnams gzhan la phan pa'i phyir/_/sdug bsngal ci ste khas len byed mi
[\[27b\]]
[\[27b.1\]]'gyur/_/brtse dang ldan pa'i snying rje'i sbyin pa gang /_/longs spyod dang ni de las byams pa dang /_/rjes su gzung bas bskyed dang de yi mthus/_/byas pa'i bde ba rtag tu 'phel bar 'gyur/_/snying rjes rgyas par bya zhing 'phel bar bya/_/sbyin pas yongs
[\[27b.2\]]smin bya zhing bde bar bya/_/kun du drang bar bya zhing bkri bya zhes/_/zhen pa rnams la rab tu smra dang 'dra/_/snying rjes sdug bsngal dag gis sdug bsngal ba/_/bde ma bskyed par gang gis bde bar 'gyur/_/de phyir brtse dang ldan pas gzhan bde ba/_/bskyed
[\[27b.3\]]nas bdag nyid bde bar byed pa yin/_/snying rje can ni rtag tu rang sbyin la/_/ston dang 'dra ste rang bde mi 'dod pa/_/longs spyod rnams kyis gzhan dag bde bar gyis/_/yang na tha dad min bde bdag la'ang min/_/de bdes bde ba bdag gis sbyin pa ni/_/'bras
[\[27b.4\]]dang bcas te sems can rnams la byin/_/gal te khyod kyis bdag la bya ba yod/_/de dag nyid la shin tu 'bras bur byos/_/sbyin pa po ni longs spyod mi 'dod kyang /_/longs spyod shin tu mang la bzang dang phrad/_/bdag ni bde ba de 'dod ma yin te/_/'di
[\[27b.5\]]ltar bdag ni sbyin la brgyud dang ldan/_/bdag ni rtag tu brtse bas bdog pa kun/_/yongs su gtong ba gang yin de ltos la/_/des na khyod kyis bdag ni de'i 'bras la/_/don gnyer med pa nyid du shes par bya/_/gal te khyod 'bras thob pa mi gtong na/_/
[\[27b.6\]]sbyin la mngon dga' yin par mi 'gyur te/_/'di ltar skad cig tsam yang sbyin med na/_/sbyin la mngon par dga' ba nyid ma yin/_/ma byas pa la 'bras bu mi 'byin te/_/'di ltar lan bltas bdag gi cha ma yin/_/khyod kyi lan la lta dang bral bas na/_/
[\[27b.7\]]'bras bu shin tu gzhan la gtong ba yin/_/rgyal sras rnams kyi brtse bas sbyin pa ni/_/kha na ma tho med cing dag pa'i gzhi/_/bde ba 'dren par byed pa nyid dang ni/_/rjes su srung bcas tshol med gos pa med/_/rgyal sras rnams kyi brtse bas sbyin pa ni/_/
[\[28a\]]
[\[28a.1\]]mtha' dag rgya che gtso dang rtag pa dang /_/dga' dang zang zing med dang dag pa dang /_/byang chub la gzhol dge la gzhol ba yin/_/ji ltar bde ba gsum gyis tshim pa'i yid/_/brtse ldan yongs su gtong bas dga' 'gyur ba/_/longs
[\[28a.2\]]spyod can dag nye bar spyad pa yis/_/de ltar dga' bar 'gyur ba ma yin no/_/bkren la brtse dang ma rungs pa la brtse/_/kun 'khrugs la brtse bag med rnams la brtse/_/yul gyi gzhan dbang can la snying rje dang /_/log par mngon par zhen la snying rje'o/_/
[\[28a.3\]]bde dang sdug bsngal bde rgyu las/_/byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje ste/_/rgyu dang bshes gnyen rang bzhin las/_/byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje'o/_/byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje ni/_/mnyam par shes bya de bsam phyir/_/sgrub phyir 'dod chags bral
[\[28a.4\]]phyir dang /_/mi dmigs phyir dang dag phyir ro/_/rang gi sems kyis byams la sogs/_/sgom pa chos la mos pa dang /_/bsam dang dbang 'byor nyid dang ni/_/rnam par mi rtog gcig phyir mchog_/de ltar bcom ldan 'das la dang ba rab skyes shing /_/
[\[28a.5\]]rdzas dang bkur sti chen pos shin tu rgyun mchod ldan/_/yon tan mang ldan phan byed shes la rtag sten pa/_/'gro la rjes su brtse ba grub pa kun thob 'gyur/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_mchod pa dang bsten pa dang tshad med pa'i le'u ste bco brgyad
[\[28a.6\]]pa'o//_//ngo tsha mi mthun phyogs spangs dang /_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/kha na ma tho med dman yul/_/sems can smin byed brtan pa'i yin/_/pha rol phyin pa drug po yi/_/mi mthun phyogs ni 'phel ba dang /_/gnyen po 'grib
[\[28a.7\]]pas byang chub sems/_/mi zad ngo tsha skye bar 'gyur/_/brtan rnams pha rol phyin pa drug_/brtan pa la ni le lo dang /_/nyon mongs rjes su mthun chos la/_/sbyor ba las kyang ngo mtshar 'gyur/_/mnyam gzhag ngo bo nyid min chung /_/'bring dang dman pa'i
[\[28b\]]
[\[28b.1\]]sa pa dang /_/bsam pa dman dang ngar bcas pa'i/_/ngo tsha dman de las gzhan lhag_/blo ldan khrel med tshul min las/_/nyon mongs dang len khro ba dang /_/yal bar 'dor dang nga rgyal gyis/_/sems can rnams dang tshul khrims 'joms/_/'gyod
[\[28b.2\]]pas nyams dang bcas 'gyur zhing /_/bkur sti dman pa thob 'gyur des/_/dad ldan mi min tshogs dang ni/_/ston pas kyang ni btang snyoms mdzad/_/rgyal sras chos dang mthun rnams kyis/_/rnam par smod cing 'jig rten las/_/mthong ba'i chos la
[\[28b.3\]]mi snyan 'thob/_/gzhan du phyir zhing mi khom skye/_/des na chos dkar thob pa dang /_/ma thob pa las rnam nyams 'gyur/_/de phyir sdug bsngal gnas pa dang /_/yid kyang rnal du mi gnas 'gyur/_/rgyal sras ngo tsha ldan rnams la/_/nyes pa 'di dag
[\[28b.4\]]kun mi 'byung /_/mkhas pa rtag tu lha dag dang /_/mi rnams su ni yang dag skye/_/blo ldan ngo tshas myur du ni/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub tshogs rdzogs byed/_/rgyal ba'i sras ni sems can rnams/_/smin byed skyo bar mi 'gyur nyid/_/de rtag mi mthun
[\[28b.5\]]phyogs dang ni/_/gnyen po bral dang mi 'bral 'gyur/_/de ltar rgyal sras ngo tsha ldan/_/phan yon de dag 'thob par 'gyur/_/byis pa shin tu gos bzang gyon yang ni/_/khrel dang bral phyir nyes pas dri ma can/_/rgyal sras ngo tsha shes pa'i gos can
[\[28b.6\]]ni/_/dgab pa med kyang nyes pa'i dri ma bral/_/rgyal ba'i sras ni khrel dang ldan gyur pa/_/nam mkha' bzhin du chos kyis gos mi 'gyur/_/rgyal sras rnams kyi nang du 'dus gyur pa/_/ngo tsha shes pas brgyan pa mdzes pa yin/_/byang chub sems
[\[28b.7\]]dpa' rnams ni ngo tsha bas/_/gdul bya rnams la ma bzhin byams pa nyid/_/ngo tsha ba ni nyes pa thams cad las/_/'khor ba kun tu srung bar byed pa'ang yin/_/kun la dang du len pa dang /_/kun la dang du mi len cing /_/kun la mi 'jug 'jug pa ni/_/
[\[29a\]]
[\[29a.1\]]khrel ldan khrel bas byas pa'i rtags/_/rang gi sems kyis khrel sgom pa/_/chos la mos dang bsam pa dang /_/dbang 'byor pa dang mi rtog dang /_/gcig pa nyid kyis gtso bo yin/_/byang chub sems dpa'i brtan pa ni/_/de las
[\[29a.2\]]gzhan pa thams cad las/_/mtshan nyid dang ni rab dbye dang /_/mi 'gyur bas ni khyad par 'phags/_/brtson 'grus ting 'dzin shes rab ni/_/snying stobs sran thub brtan par 'dod/_/gang phyir gsum gyis byang chub sems/_/'jigs pa med par
[\[29a.3\]]rab tu 'jug_/zhum dang g.yo dang rmongs pa yis/_/bya ba rnams la 'jigs pa skye/_/de phyir gnyug ma gsum la ni/_/brtan pa'i ming du shes par bya/_/rang bzhin dang ni smon lam dang /_/lta ba med pa nyid dang ni/_/sems can log par sgrub pa dang /_/
[\[29a.4\]]zab cing rgya che thos pa dang /_/gdul bya gdul bar dka' ba dang /_/rgyal sku bsam gyis mi khyab dang /_/dka' ba dag ni sna tshogs dang /_/'khor ba gtong ba med nyid dang /_/de nyid nyon mongs med pa la/_/brtan pa'i brtan pa skye ba ni/_/de las gzhan dang mi
[\[29a.5\]]mtshungs te/_/brtan ldan rnams kyi mchog tu 'dod/_/phye ma leb dang 'dab chags dang /_/rgya mtsho dag gis ri rab ltar/_/brtan pa grogs ngan sdug bsngal dang /_/zab mo thos pas mi g.yos so/_/byang chub mi skyo mnyam med pa/_/gzhi gsum thos pas
[\[29a.6\]]mi ngoms dang /_/brtson 'grus che dang sdug bsngal la'o/_/ngo tsha brtan la brten pa ste/_/byang chub che la 'dun pa dag_/blo ldan rnams kyi mi skyo ba/_/sa rnams la ni ma rdzogs dang /_/rdzogs dang shin tu rdzogs par 'dod/_/brtan pa'i bstan bcos
[\[29a.7\]]shes pa nyid/_/gzhi dang ched du bya ba dang /_/las dang mtshan nyid dag dang ni/_/mi zad nyid dang 'bras bu ni/_/yang dag 'grub pas khyad par 'phags/_/ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs sgos bsdus/_/sems can smin par byed pa dang /_/dam chos
[\[29b\]]
[\[29b.1\]]'dzin par byed pa'ang yin/_/brtan rnams 'jig rten shes pa nyid/_/lus dang ngag dang yid dag gis/_/bden pa shes pas mnyam pa med/_/de las gzhan pa dag las 'phags/_/brtan rnams rtag tu 'dzum par byed/_/gsong po dag tu smra ba yin/_/
[\[29b.2\]]sems can snod du bya ba'i phyir/_/dam chos bsgrub par bya ba'i phyir/_/gang phyir bden pa gnyis kyis ni/_/'jig rten rnams rtag 'byung bar 'dod/_/gnyis kyis nub 'gyur de yi phyir/_/de shes 'jig rten shes zhes bya/_/de dag zhi ba thob bya'i phyir/_/
[\[29b.3\]]blo ldan bden pa rnams la sbyor/_/gang gis blo ldan bden shes phyir/_/'jig rten shes zhes nges par brjod/_/gtsug lag brtan pa'i chos dang ni/_/de don dgongs pa can dang ni/_/nges don tshad mar ldan pa dang /_/de yi brjod med thob pa'o/_/spong dang
[\[29b.4\]]ji skad bshad pa dang /_/'gog par yang dag shes pa dang /_/brjod dang bcas par 'thob pa dag_/'dir ni dgag par bstan pa yin/_/mos dang rnam par dpyod pa dang /_/gzhan las ji bzhin thos pa dang /_/rjod pa med pa'i ye shes las/_/brtan
[\[29b.5\]]rnams nyams par mi 'gyur ro/_/rnam grangs dang ni mtshan nyid dang /_/tshig dang ye shes shes pa'i phyir/_/byang chub sems dpa'i yang dag rig_/bzhi po mtshungs pa med par 'dod/_/bstan pa la ni rab brtson pa'i/_/gang zhig gang gis ston pa ni/_/
[\[29b.6\]]chos dang don ni gnyis po dag_/tshig dang shes pa kho nas ston/_/chos ni bstan dang bshad phyir dang /_/rnam pa kun du gnyis thob phyir/_/rgol ba rnams kyi lan 'debs phyir/_/so so yang dag rig pa bzhi/_/mnyam nyid so so rang rig nas/_/
[\[29b.7\]]phyis ni rab tu shes pa yin/_/the tshom thams cad gcod byed pa/_/so so yang dag rig par brjod/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshogs/_/bsod nams ye shes mtshungs pa med/_/gcig gis 'khor bar mngon mtho byed/_/gzhan gyis nyon
[\[30a\]]
[\[30a.1\]]mongs med par 'khor/_/sbyin dang tshul khrims bsod nams kyi/_/tshogs yin shes rab ye shes kyi/_/gsum po gzhan ni gnyis ka'i ste/_/lnga car yang ni ye shes tshogs/_/rgyun du sgom pa thob nas ni/_/dge la yang dang yang du
[\[30a.2\]]sgrub/_/brtan pa'i tshogs gang yin pa de/_/don kun sgrub par byed pa yin/_/'jug dang mtshan ma med pa dang /_/lhun gyis grub par bya ba dang /_/dbang bskur mthar thug bya ba'i phyir/_/brtan rnams tshogs ni sgrub par byed/_/blo ldan dran pa nyer gzhag
[\[30a.3\]]pa/_/bsgom pa rnam pa bcu bzhi yis/_/mtshungs pa med pa'i phyir na de/_/de las gzhan las khyad par 'phags/_/rten dang gnyen po dag dang ni/_/de bzhin rjes su 'jug pa dang /_/dmigs pa dang ni yid byed dang /_/thob pas bsgom pa khyad par
[\[30a.4\]]'phags/_/mthun dang rjes su 'jug pa dang /_/yongs su shes dang skye ba dang /_/chen po dang ni mchog nyid dang /_/bsgom dang yang dag 'grub pas gzhan/_/brtan pa rnams kyi yang dag spong /_/lus can rnams dang mtshungs pa med/_/dran pa nye
[\[30a.5\]]bar gzhag pa yi/_/nyes pa rnams kyi gnyen por bsgom/_/'khor ba nye bar spyad pa dang /_/sgrib pa dag ni dor ba dang /_/yid la byed pa dor ba dang /_/sa rnams la ni 'jug pa dang /_/mtshan ma med par gnas pa dang /_/lung bstan pa ni thob pa dang /_/
[\[30a.6\]]sems can rnams yongs smin bya dang /_/dbang ni bskur bar bya ba dang /_/zhing rnams dag par bya phyir dang /_/mthar thug nyid du bya ba'i phyir/_/byang chub sems dpa' blo ldan rnams/_/mi mthun phyogs kyi gnyen por bsgom/_/'dun pa la ni brten nas
[\[30a.7\]]su/_/rnal 'byor rgyu mtshan bcas bsgom pa/_/yang dag spong ba thams cad la/_/gnyen po zhes ni nges par brjod/_/brtan pa rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi/_/rkang pa mtshan nyid mchog ldan bzhi/_/bdag nyid dang ni gzhan dag gi/_/don kun 'grub pa'i
[\[30b\]]
[\[30b.1\]]phyir skye'o/_/rten dang rab tu dbye ba dang /_/thabs dang mngon par sgrub pa yis/_/blo ldan rdzu 'phrul rkang pa rnams/_/rnam pa kun tu rnam gzhag 'dod/_/bsam gtan pha rol phyin brten nas/_/rab tu dbye ba dag dang thabs/_/rnam bzhi mngon par sgrub pa
[\[30b.2\]]ni/_/rnam pa drug tu brjod pa yin/_/gcig ni 'bad par byed pa ste/_/gnyis pa phan 'dogs bdag nyid yin/_/gsum pa gtod par byed pa ste/_/bzhi pa gnyen po pa yin no/_/mthong ba dang ni gdams ngag dang /_/gnas pas rnam par rtse ba dang /_/
[\[30b.3\]]smon lam dang ni dbang dag dang /_/chos thob pa ni sgrub pa'i phyir/_/byang chub spyod dang thos mchog dang /_/zhi gnas lhag mthong dad sogs kyi/_/gzhi yin par ni shes bya ste/_/don sgrub byed pa'i skabs kyis so/_/dad sogs sa la 'jug pa ste/_/
[\[30b.4\]]kun nas nyon mongs can du 'dod/_/mi mthun phyogs nyam chung bas yang /_/de dag nyid la stobs zhes bya/_/sar zhugs rnams la byang chub kyi/_/yan lag rnam par gzhag par 'dod/_/chos rnams dang ni sems can kun/_/mnyam pa nyid du rtogs
[\[30b.5\]]phyir ro/_/shes byas rgyal rgyal bya yi phyir/_/dran pa dag ni kun tu spyod/_/'di yi rnam 'byed rtog pa yi/_/mchan ma thams cad 'joms par byed/_/'di yi brtson 'grus ma lus pa/_/myur du rtogs par bya phyir 'jug_/chos kyi snang ba rnam 'phel
[\[30b.6\]]ba'i/_/dga' bas rtag tu rgyas par 'gyur/_/sgrib pa kun las thar ba'i phyir/_/shin tu sbyangs pas bde ba 'thob/_/ting nge 'dzin las bsams pa'i don/_/'byor ba nye bar skye bar 'gyur/_/btang snyoms kyis ni thams cad du/_/'di ni ji ltar
[\[30b.7\]]'dod bzhin gnas/_/rjes la thob dang mi rtog pa'i/_/gnas pas mchog ni rtag tu gnas/_/yon tan de lta'i sems dpa' ni/_/'khor los sgyur ba 'dra bar 'jog_/rtag tu rin chen bdun lta bu'i/_/byang chub yan lag rnams kyis bskor/_/
[\[31a\]]
[\[31a.1\]]rang bzhin yan lag gnas yan lag_/gsum pa nges 'byung yan lag ste/_/bzhi pa phan yon yan lag yin/_/rnam gsum nyon mongs med yan lag_/de yi 'og tu ji lta ba/_/rtogs pa'i rjes su 'jug pa ste/_/rnam gzhag
[\[31a.2\]]ji bzhin rtogs pa dang /_/rnam par gzhag la 'jug pa dang /_/las gsum rnam par dag pa dang /_/shes bya dag dang lam dang ni/_/yon tan khyad par can gyi ni/_/sgrib pa'i gnyen por sgom pa'o/_/yang dag gnas pa la brten nas/_/sems la
[\[31a.3\]]sems ni 'jog phyir dang /_/chos rab rnam par 'byed pa'i phyir/_/zhi gnas dang ni lhag mthong yin/_/de ni kun 'gro cha gcig dang /_/cha gcig ma yin rgyur 'dod do/_/rtogs dang nges par 'byung ba dang /_/mtshan med 'du mi byed pa dang /_/yongs dag
[\[31a.4\]]rnam par dag pa la/_/brten pa'i zhi gnas lhag mthong gi_/rnal 'byor de sa kun 'gro ste/_/thams cad sgrub par byed pa yin/_/sangs rgyas chos rnams rdzogs bya dang /_/sems can rnams yongs smin bya dang /_/myur thob bya ba 'grub pa dang /_/lam
[\[31a.5\]]rgyun mi gcod la mkhas pa/_/byang chub sems dpa'i sa kun la/_/thabs ni mtshungs pa med pa ste/_/thabs mkhas de la brten nas ni/_/de dag don kun sgrub par byed/_/rnam smin thos la goms pa dang /_/ting nge 'dzin gyi gzungs dag ni/_/chung
[\[31a.6\]]ngu dang ni chen po ste/_/chen po de yang rnam pa gsum/_/blo ldan ma zhugs zhugs pa yang /_/ma dag sa pa rnams kyi ni/_/chung ngu dang ni 'bring po ste/_/dag pa'i sa pa'i gzungs chen yin/_/byang chub sems dpa' yang dang yang /_/de la yang dag brten
[\[31a.7\]]nas ni/_/rtag tu dam pa'i chos dag kyang /_/rab tu ston cing 'dzin par byed/_/brtan pa rnams kyi smon lam ni/_/sems pa 'dun dang bcas pa ste/_/de ni ye shes kyis bskul ba/_/sa rnams kun la mnyam pa med/_/de ni rgyu gyur shes bya ste/_/
[\[31b\]]
[\[31b.1\]]sems tsam las ni 'grub pa'i phyir/_/sems las mod la 'bras bu can/_/de ni ma 'ongs don 'grub byed/_/sna tshogs che dang byang chub par/_/sa rnams gong nas gong du ni/_/rnam dag byang chub sems dpa' yi/_/rang bzhin don rab sgrub byed yin/_/
[\[31b.2\]]ting 'dzin gsum gyi spyod yul ni/_/bdag med rnam pa gnyis po dang /_/bdag tu 'dzin pa'i rten dang ni/_/de rtag nyer zhi yin zhes bya/_/de ni gzung 'dzin ngo bo'i phyir/_/rnam pa gsum du shes par bya/_/rnam par mi rtog rgyab kyis phyogs/_/rab tu
[\[31b.3\]]dga' dang ldan pa'o/_/yongs su shes dang spang ba dang /_/mngon sum du ni bya ba'i phyir/_/stong nyid la sogs ting 'dzin rnams/_/don rnam gsum du yongs su bsgrags/_/sems can rnams la phan bzhed pas/_/ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyu nyid du/_/chos
[\[31b.4\]]kyi sdom ni rnam pa bzhi/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams la bshad/_/brtan pa rnams kyi bzhi po de/_/med pa'i don dang rnam rtog don/_/kun du rtog don kho na dang /_/rnam rtog nye bar zhi ba'i don/_/mi rung rgyu las skye phyir dang /_/'gal phyir rang nyid mi
[\[31b.5\]]gnas phyir/_/med phyir mtshan nyid nges phyir dang /_/rjes su 'jug phyir 'gag pa'i phyir/_/yongs su 'gyur ba dmigs phyir dang /_/de rgyu nyid dang 'bras bu'i phyir/_/zin pa'i phyir dang bdag po'i phyir/_/dge dang sems can rjes 'jug phyir/_/dang po je
[\[31b.6\]]bas je che dang /_/rgyas dang rten gyi dngos po dang /_/'gyur dang yongs su smin pa dang /_/de bzhin dman dang khyad par 'phags/_/'od gsal ba dang 'od mi gsal/_/yul gzhan 'gro dang sa bon bcas/_/sa bon med pa'i ngo bo dang /_/gzugs brnyan du ni
[\[31b.7\]]skye ba ste/_/skye ba rnam pa bcu bzhi la/_/rgyu dang tshad kyi khyad par dang /_/rgyas pa don med mi rung dang /_/rten nyid du ni mi srid dang /_/gnas pa la ni mi srid dang /_/dang po mi 'jig mthar mi 'gyur/_/de bzhin dman dang khyad par 'phags/_/'od gsal ba
[\[32a\]]
[\[32a.1\]]dang 'od mi gsal/_/'gro med gnas pa mi rung dang /_/tha ma nyid ni mi srid phyir/_/sems kyi rjes su 'jug pa'i phyir/_/'dus byas thams cad skad cig ma/_/'byung ba rnams dang don rnam drug_/skad cig nyid du brjod pa ni/_
[\[32a.2\]]skam dang 'phel dang rang bzhin gyis/_/g.yo dang 'phel dang 'grib pa'i phyir/_/'byung ba de dang 'phel phyir dang /_/yongs su 'gyur ba bzhi yi phyir/_/kha dog dri dang ro dang reg_/'dra phyir de ni de dang 'dra/_/bud shing rag las 'jug pa'i phyir/_
[\[32a.3\]]je bas je cher dmigs pa'i phyir/_/sems rjes 'jug phyir dri ba'i phyir/_/des na phyi yang skad cig ma/_/gang zag btags par yod nyid du/_/brjod bya rdzas su ma yin no/_/mi dmigs phyin ci log pa dang /_/kun nas nyon mongs nyon mongs rgyu/_/
[\[32a.4\]]nyes pa gnyis phyir de las 'di/_/gcig dang gzhan du brjod bya min/_/phung po bdag tu thal ba dang /_/de rdzas nyid du thal 'gyur phyir/_/gal te rdzas yod brjod min pa'i/_/dgos pa yang ni brjod dgos so/_/gcig dang gzhan du brjod min pa/_/
[\[32a.5\]]dgos pa med par mi rigs so/_/mtshan nyid dang ni 'jig rten na/_/mthong phyir bstan bcos sgo nas kyang /_/bud shing me bzhin gnyis su ni/_/brjod min mi rung gnyis phyir ro/_/gnyis yod rnam shes skye ba'i phyir/_/de rkyen ma yin don med phyir/_/
[\[32a.6\]]de phyir lta ba po nas ni/_/grol bo'i bar du mi 'gyur ro/_/bdag po nyid cig yin na ni/_/mi rtag mi 'dod 'byung mi byed/_/de yis mtshan nyid bsgrub dgos te/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub gsum la gnod/_/nyes pa gsum phyir lta sogs la/_/de yi byed
[\[32a.7\]]pa rang 'byung min/_/byed pa de yi rkyen can yang /_/lta sogs byed pa med pa yin/_/byed pa min phyir mi rtag phyir/_/cig car rtag tu 'jug pa'i phyir/_/lta la sogs pa'i byed pa ni/_/rang byung nyid du mi rung ngo /_/de bzhin gnas dang zhig pa ni/_/snga
[\[32b\]]
[\[32b.1\]]na med dang mi rtag dang /_/phyogs gsum po yang med pa'i phyir/_/rkyen nyid du ni mi rung ngo /_/'di ltar chos rnams thams cad ni/_/bdag med dam pa'i don du na/_/stong nyid bdag tu dmigs pa ni/_/nyes par bshad pa kho na yin/_/kun nas nyon mongs
[\[32b.2\]]rnam byang ba'i/_/gnas skabs gcod pa'i bye brag dang /_/'jug dang rgyun gyi bye brag kyang /_/gang zag gis ni nye bar bstan/_/bdag tu lta ba bskyed mi dgos/_/goms pa thog ma med dus can/_/gang zag yod na thams cad ni/_/'bad med thar
[\[32b.3\]]pa'am thar pa med/_/de ltar yon tan de dag dang /_/rtag ldan byang chub sems dpa' ni/_/rang gi don yang mi 'dor zhing /_/gzhan gyi don yang sgrub par byed/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_byang chub kyi phyogs dang mthun pa'i le'u ste bcu dgu pa'o//_//_
[\[32b.4\]]rang gi lus dang sdom pa'i phyir/_/phun sum tshogs pa yongs gtong dang /_/nyam chung rnams la bzod pa dang /_/lus dang srog la mi lta bar/_/brtson 'grus rtsom dang bsam gtan gyi/_/bde la ro myang med nyid dang /_/shes rab la ni mi rtog pa/_/blo
[\[32b.5\]]ldan rnams kyi ngo mtshar 'dod/_/de bzhin gshegs rigs skye ba dang /_/lung bstan pa dang dbang bskur dang /_/byang chub rab tu thob pa yang /_/ngo mtshar che ba yin par 'dod/_/'dod chags bral dang snying brtse dang /_/de bzhin bsgom mchog thob pa dang /_/
[\[32b.6\]]sems mnyam phyir na de dag la/_/sbyor ba ngo mtshar che ma yin/_/ji ltar blo ldan sems can la/_/rab tu byams par gyur pa ltar/_/sems can bdag dang chung ma dang /_/bu bshes gnyen la de lta min/_/don gnyer ba la phyogs med dang /_/tshul khrims
[\[32b.7\]]rtag tu ma nyams dang /_/kun du bzod cing thams cad phyir/_/brtson 'grus chen po rtsom pa dang /_/rtag tu bsam gtan dge ba dang /_/shes rab rnam par mi rtog nyid/_/byang chub sems dpa' de dag la/_/de ltar sems mnyam shes par bya/_/snod
[\[33a\]]
[\[33a.1\]]nyid du ni byed pa dang /_/tshul khrims dag la 'god pa dang /_/gnod pa la ni bzod pa dang /_/don byed par ni 'gro ba dang /_/bstan pa 'di la 'dzud pa dang /_/the tshom gcod par byed pa 'di/_/blo ldan rnams kyi sems can la/_/phan 'dogs
[\[33a.2\]]nyid du 'dod pa yin/_/gang dag rtag tu sems can rnams/_/bsam pa mnyam pas 'dzin byed cing /_/'phags pa'i sa la skyed pa dang /_/dge ba 'phel bar byed pa dang /_/nyes byas las ni yongs srung dang /_/thos pa byang bar byed pa ni/_/las lnga dag gis
[\[33a.3\]]rgyal sras rnams/_/sems can ma dang 'dra ba yin/_/sems can kun la rtag par ni/_/dad pa skyed par byed pa dang /_/lhag pa'i khrims sogs slob pa dang /_/rnam par grol la sbyor ba'i phyir/_/sangs rgyas la ni gsol ba dang /_/de dag sgrib pa spong ba'i
[\[33a.4\]]phyir/_/las lnga dag gis rgyal sras rnams/_/sems can pha dang 'dra ba yin/_/gang dag bstan par mi 'os pa/_/sems can rnams la gsang byed cing /_/bslab las nyams la smod pa dang /_/phun sum tshogs pa bsngags pa nyid/_/gdams ngag sbyin
[\[33a.5\]]par byed pa dang /_/bdud rnams sbron par byed pa ste/_/las lnga dag gis rgyal sras rnams/_/sems can rtsa lag 'dra ba yin/_/kun nas nyon mongs rnam byang la/_/gang dag rang blo ma 'khrul pa/_/'jig rten 'jig rten min pa yi/_/phun tshogs zad
[\[33a.6\]]par sbyin par byad/_/skyo ba med pas mi phyed cing /_/rtag tu phan dang bde 'dod pa/_/las lnga dag gis rgyal sras rnams/_/sems can grogs po 'dra ba yin/_/gang dag sems can smin bya la/_/rtag tu brtson pa dang ldan zhing /_/yang dag nges par 'byung
[\[33a.7\]]ba smra/_/log par sgrub pa rnams la bzod/_/phun sum tshogs pa gnyis sbyin byed/_/de yi thabs la mkhas pa ni/_/las lnga dag gis rgyal sras rnams/_/sems can bran dang 'dra ba yin/_/gang dag mi skye'i chos la ni/_/bzod pa thob par 'dod pa
[\[33b\]]
[\[33b.1\]]dang /_/theg pa thams cad ston pa dang /_/rnal 'byor grub par sbyor ba dang /_/bzhin mdzes lan du phan 'dogs dang /_/rnam par smin la mi lta ba/_/las lnga dag gis rgyal sras rnams/_/sems can slob dpon 'dra ba yin/_/sems can don la shin
[\[33b.2\]]tu brtson/_/tshogs rnams rdzogs par byed pa dang /_/tshogs bsags myur du grol bar byed/_/mi mthun phyogs ni spong byed cing /_/'jig rten 'jig rten ma yin pa'i/_/phun sum tshogs pa la sbyor ba/_/las lnga dag gis rgyal sras rnams/_/sems
[\[33b.3\]]can mkhan po 'dra ba yin/_/longs spyod rnams la ma chags dang /_/tshul khrims nyams pa med pa dang /_/byas pa gzo dang ldan pa dang /_/sgrub pa la yang sbyor ba'i phyir/_/pha rol phyin pa drug po la/_/de ltar 'jug pa'i lus can dag_/byang chub
[\[33b.4\]]sems dpa' rnams la ni/_/de bzhin lan du phan 'dogs yin/_/rtag tu 'phel dang nyams pa dang /_/sems can rab tu smin pa dang /_/sa la khyad par 'gro ba dang /_/bla na med pa'i byang chub 'dod/_/'jigs spang yang dag bskyed pa dang /_/the tshom dag
[\[33b.5\]]ni gcod pa dang /_/sgrub pa yi ni gdams ngag la/_/rgyal sras rtag tu chud mi za/_/re ba med pa'i sbyin pa dang /_/yang srid mi 'dod tshul khrims dang /_/thams cad la ni bzod pa dang /_/yon tan kun 'byung brtson 'grus dang /_/de bzhin bsam gtan
[\[33b.6\]]gzugs med min/_/shes rab thabs dang ldan pa ni/_/pha rol phyin pa drug po la/_/brtan pa rnams kyi yang dag sbyor/_/longs spyod chags dang nyams bcas dang /_/nga rgyal nyid dang bsod nyams dang /_/ro myang ba dang rnam rtog ni/_/brtan pa rnams kyi
[\[33b.7\]]nyams pa'i rgyu/_/de dag gnyen po la gnas pa'i/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ni/_/de las bzlog phyir khyad par gyi/_/skal can chos su shes par bya/_/sprul pa dang ni tshul 'chos dang /_/bzhin mdzes pa ni ston pa dang /_/de bzhin 'phral la
[\[34a\]]
[\[34a.1\]]'jug pa dang /_/lus dang ngag ni zhi ba dang /_/de bzhin smra mkhas phun sum tshogs/_/de dag sgrub dang bral ba ni/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams dag gi_/_yang dag min pa nyid du bshad/_/bzlog par rab tu sbyor rnams kyi/_/de dag
[\[34a.2\]]yang dag nyid du bshad/_/blo ldan de dag sa kun du/_/sbyin la sogs pa nyer bsgrubs pas/_/sems can rnams kyi mi mthun phyogs/_/rnam pa drug ni 'dul bar byed/_/gang zag dus kyi bye brag gis/_/blo ldan lung bstan rnam pa gnyis/_/byang chub
[\[34a.3\]]dang ni lung ston pa/_/gzhan yang chen por brjod pa ni/_/mi skye bzod pa thob pa yi/_/nga rgyal rtsol ba spangs pa dang /_/sangs rgyas sras bcas thams cad dang /_/ngo bo gcig tu gyur pa las/_/yang de zhing dang ming dang ni/_/dus dang bskal pa'i ming
[\[34a.4\]]dang ni/_/'khor dang dam pa'i chos dag kyang /_/gnas pa'i sgo nas der 'dod do/_/blo ldan rnam pa thams cad du/_/phun tshogs skyed dang mi skyo dang /_/rtag tu sgom par byed pa dang /_/ting 'dzin nyams pa med pa dang /_/bya ba 'grub dang lhun grub pa'i/_/
[\[34a.5\]]bzod pa 'thob la nges par 'gyur/_/mchod bslab yang dag blang ba dang /_/snying rje dge ba bsgom pa dang /_/de bzhin dgon par bag yod dang /_/thos don ngoms mi shes pa nyid/_/sa rnams kun la brtan pa yi/_/gdon mi za bar bya ba nyid/_/'dod pa'i
[\[34a.6\]]nyes dmigs shes pa dang /_/'khrul pa dag la rtog pa dang /_/sdug bsngal dang du len nyid dang /_/dge ba dag ni sgom pa dang /_/bde la ro myang med nyid dang /_/mtshan ma rnam par mi rtog pa/_/sa rnams kun la brtan pa yi/_/rtag tu bya ba dag yin no/_/
[\[34a.7\]]chos sbyin tshul khrims dag pa dang /_/mi skye bzod pa thob nyid dang /_/theg chen brtson 'grus rtsom pa dang /_/mtha' la snying rje ldan gnas dang /_/shes rab blo dang ldan rnams kyi/_/pha rol phyin pa'i gtso bor 'dod/_/mdo sogs rnam pa'i bye brag
[\[34b\]]
[\[34b.1\]]gis/_/rig pa'i gnas ni rnam gzhag pa/_/sa rnams kun la brtan pa yi/_/chos rnams gzhag pa yin zhes bya/_/de bzhin nyid ni rnam bdun la/_/brten nas bden pa rnam par gzhag_/rigs pa theg pa rnam gzhag pa/_/rnam pa bzhi dang rnam gsum
[\[34b.2\]]nyid/_/tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang /_/yang dag lta ba 'bras ldan dang /_/tshad mas rnam 'byed bsam mi khyab/_/rigs pa bzhir ni shes par bya/_/bsam pa dang ni bshad nyid dang /_/sbyor ba dang ni tshogs dag dang /_/'grub pa'i rab tu dbye ba
[\[34b.3\]]yis/_/theg pa rnam pa gsum du 'dod/_/ming dang dngos dag phan tshun du/_/glo bur ba ni nyid du btsal/_/'dogs pa rnam pa gnyis po 'dir/_/de tsam nyid du tshol ba'o/_/thams cad dmigs su med pa'i phyir/_/yang dag ye shes rnam pa bzhi/_/
[\[34b.4\]]sa rnams kun la brtan pa yi/_/don kun sgrub par byed par 'gyur/_/'ching ba yi ni rten dag dang /_/longs spyod sa bon rgyu mtshan 'dir/_/sems dang sems las byung ba rnams/_/rten bcas sa bon bcas te bcings/_/mdun bzhag mtshan ma gang
[\[34b.5\]]yin dang /_/bdag nyid 'dug pa gang yin pa/_/thams cad rnam 'jig blo ldan gyis/_/byang chub mchog ni thob par 'gyur/_/de bzhin nyid dmigs shes pa dang /_/gnyis su 'dzin pa rnam spangs dang /_/gnas ngan len lus mngon sum pa/_/blo ldan
[\[34b.6\]]de zad byed par 'dod/_/de bzhin nyid dmigs ye shes ni/_/rnam pa tha dad med bsgoms shing /_/yod dang med don mngon sum pa/_/rnam rtog dbang 'byor nyid ces bya/_/byis pa yang dag nyid bsgribs nas/_/yang dag ma yin kun du snang /_/byang
[\[34b.7\]]chub sems dpa' de bsal nas/_/yang dag nyid ni kun du snang /_/don med pa dang don yod dag_/mi snang snang ba yin zhes bya/_/de ni gnas gzhan gyur pa ste/_/'dod dgur spyod phyir thar pa yin/_/don chen rnam pa thams cad du/_/gzhan dang gzhan
[\[35a\]]
[\[35a.1\]]rigs mthun snang ba/_/bar chad byed yin de lta bas/_/yongs shes byas nas de spang ngo /_/yongs smin rnam par sbyang bya dang /_/thob bya smin par rung bya dang /_/yang dag bshad pa'i dngos po ni/_/blo ldan rnams kyi dpag tu med/_/
[\[35a.2\]]byang chub sems ni skye ba dang /_/mi skye ba yi bzod pa nyid/_/dri med mig ni dman pa dang /_/zag pa zad pa nyid dang ni/_/dam chos yun ring gnas pa dang /_/bye brag shes spyod longs spyod nyid/_/de la zhugs pa blo ldan gyi/_/bshad pa'i 'bras bu yin
[\[35a.3\]]zhes bya/_/dmigs pa che ba nyid dang ni/_/de bzhin sgrub pa gnyis dag dang /_/ye shes brtson 'grus rtsom pa dang /_/thabs la mkhas par gyur pa dang /_/yang dag 'grub pa chen po dang /_/sangs rgyas phrin las chen po ste/_/chen po 'di dang ldan
[\[35a.4\]]pa'i phyir/_/theg chen zhes ni nges par brjod/_/rigs dang chos la mos pa dang /_/de bzhin sems ni bskyed pa dang /_/sbyin la sogs pa sgrub pa dang /_/skyon med pa la 'jug nyid dang /_/sems can rnams yongs smin byed dang /_/zhing ni rnam par
[\[35a.5\]]sbyong ba dang /_/mi gnas mya ngan 'das pa dang /_/byang chub mchog dang ston pa'o/_/gcig ni mos pa dang ldan pa/_/lhag pa'i bsam pa dag pa gzhan/_/mtshan ma dang ni mtshan med dang /_/mngon par 'du byed med spyod pa/_lnga po 'di dag sa kun la/_/
[\[35a.6\]]byang chub sems dpa' yin zhes bya/_/'dod la ma chags las gsum rnam par dag_/khro ba zil gnon yon tan mchog lhur len/_/chos las mi g.yo de nyid zab mo mthong /_/byang chub dga' ldan byang chub sems dpa'i yin/_/phan 'dogs 'dod dang gnod
[\[35a.7\]]pa med lta dang /_/gzhan gyi gnod pa dang du len pa dang /_/brtan pa bag yod mang du thos pa dang /_/gzhan gyi don brtson byang chub sems dpa' yin/_/rang gi yongs su gzung ba'i nyes dmigs shes/_/longs spyod ma chags zhe la kho na mi 'dzin/_/rnal
[\[35b\]]
[\[35b.1\]]'byor rgyu mtshan la mkhas lta ngan med/_/nang du rab gnas byang chub sems dpa' yin/_/brtse dang ldan pa ngo tsha yon tan gnas/_/sdug bsngal dang len rang gi bde ma chags/_/dran gtso shin tu mnyam par bzhag pa'i bdag_/theg pa mi 'khrugs byang chub sems
[\[35b.2\]]dpa' yin/_/sdug bsngal sel ba sdug bsngal mi byed nyid/_/sdug bsngal bzod pa sdug bsngal 'jigs pa med/_/sdug bsngal rnam grol sdug bsngal mi rtog pa/_/sdug bsngal khas len byang chub sems dpa' yin/_/chos la mi dga' rang bzhin chos la
[\[35b.3\]]dga'/_/chos la smod cing chos la mngon par brtson/_/chos la dbang ba chos la mun pa med/_/chos gtsor byed pa byang chub sems dpa' yin/_/longs spyod bag yod nges la bag yod dang /_/bsrung la bag yod dge la bag yod dang /_/bde la bag yod chos
[\[35b.4\]]la bag yod dang /_/theg pa bag yod byang chub sems dpa' yin/_/ma gus ngo tsha nyes chung ngo tsha dang /_/mi bzod ngo tsha yongs nyams ngo tsha dang /_/rnam 'phro ngo tsha lta chung ngo tsha dang /_/theg gzhan ngo tsha byang chub sems dpa' yin/_/'di dang pha rol dang ni btang snyoms
[\[35b.5\]]dang /_/'du byed ldan dang dbang 'byor nyid thob dang /_/mtshungs par ston dang 'bras bu chen po yis/_/byang chub sems dpa' phan 'dogs byed la 'jug_/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che/_/blo ldan nyid dang gsal ba'i mchog_/rgyal sras rgyal ba'i
[\[35b.6\]]gzhi dang ni/_/rgyal byed rgyal ba'i myu gu dang /_/rtsal ldan dang ni 'phags mchog dang /_/ded dpon dang ni grags mchog dang /_/snying rje can dang bsod nams che/_/dbang phyug de bzhin chos dang ldan/_/de nyid bzang rtogs don chen legs rtogs dang /_/don kun
[\[35b.7\]]rtogs dang kun du rtogs pa dang /_/thabs rnams rtogs par 'gyur ba'i khyad par rgyu/_/des na byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/_/bdag rjes rtogs dang lta ba phra rtogs dang /_/rnam rig sna tshogs rnam par rtogs dang kun/_/yang dag min rtog yin par
[\[36a\]]
[\[36a.1\]]rtogs pa'i rgyu/_/des na byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/_/ma rtogs rtogs dang rjes su rtogs pa rtogs/_/dngos med rtogs dang rab tu skye ba rtogs/_/ma rtogs rtogs pa so sor rtogs pa'i rgyu/_/des na byang chub sems dpa'
[\[36a.2\]]zhes bya'o/_/don med rtogs dang don dam rtogs pa dang /_/don kun rtogs dang mtha' dag don rtogs dang /_/rtogs bya rtogs gzhi rtogs pa rtogs pa'i rgyu/_/des na byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/_/grub par gyur pa rtogs dang gnas rtogs dang /_/
[\[36a.3\]]lhums rjes rtogs dang rim pa rtogs pa dang /_/rab tu rtogs dang the tshom bsal rtogs rgyur/_/des na byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/_/blo dang ldan pa blo thob ma thob dang /_/rab gnas rtogs dang rjes su rtogs pa dang /_/so sor 'chad blo rjod med nga bcom
[\[36a.4\]]dang /_/nga can blo gros ma smin yang dag smin/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_yon tan gyi le'u ste nyi shu pa'o//_//brtse dang snyan par smra ba dang /_/brtan pa nyid dang lag brkyang nyid/_/dgongs pa zab mo nges 'grel pa/_/'di
[\[36a.5\]]dag blo ldan rnams kyi rtags/_/yongs gzung mos pa thob pa dang /_/mi skyo gnyis kyis bsdu ba'i phyir/_/bsam pa dang ni sbyor ba las/_/rtags lngar rnam par shes par bya/_/byang chub sems dpa' rtag tu ni/_/khyim pa 'khor los sgyur rnams su/_/
[\[36a.6\]]gyur nas skye ba thams cad du/_/sems can rnams kyi don byed do/_/sa rnams kun la blo ldan gyi/_/rab byung len pas thob pa dang /_/chos nyid kyis ni thob pa gzhan/_/rab tu byung bar ston byed yin/_/rab tu byung ba'i phyogs dag ni/_/yon tan
[\[36a.7\]]tshad med rnams dang ldan/_/de ltas sdom brtson khyim pa yi/_/byang chub sems dpa' las khyad 'phags/_/sa rnams kun la brtan pa yi/_/pha rol sdug pa'i 'bras bu dang /_/'di la dge ba 'jug 'dod dang /_/mya ngan 'das par 'dod pa dang /_/

[\[36b.1\]]ma dag rnam dag rab dag pa/_/sems can rnams la bsam par 'dod/_/sa rnams kun la blo ldan pa'i/_/smon lam dang ni sems mnyam dang /_/bdag por gyur pa dag dang ni/_/'khor sdud pa yis yongs su 'dzin/_/blo ldan rnams kyi las dang ni/_

[\[37a\]]
[\[37a.1\]]gnyis yin te/_/chos kyi de nyid dang de ni/_/mi shes shes sogs 'jug pa nyid/_/shes rab spyod yul de lta bas/_/des gnyis la rnam par gnas/_/bslab pa rnams dang bsgom pa yis/_/'bras bu gzhan ni rnam pa bzhi/_/

[\[38a.1\]]byang chub sems dpa' yi/_/sa rnams gnas pa yin par 'dod/_/'byung po dpag med 'jigs med phyir/_/dpag tu med pa de dag la/_/phyi phyir gong du 'gro ldan phyir/_/de dag nyid ni sar 'dod do/_/sa 'thob pa ni

[\[38b.1\]]dang /_/ting nge 'dzin dang ye shes la/_/mnga' brnyes khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/_/thabs dang skyabs dang dag pa dang /_/theg chen nges par 'byung ba la/_/sems can rnams la rab slu ba'i/_/bdud 'joms khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rang gzhan

[\[42a.5\]]dang med de kho na ste/_/ngo bo nyid ni gsum du 'dod/_/'di la chos dang gang zag dang /_/gzung ba dag dang 'dzin pa dang /_/yod dang med par sgro 'dogs dang /_/skur ba 'debs par lta ba dag_/gang shes nas ni mi 'byung ba/_/de de kho na'i mtshan nyid do/_/mi rtag

[\[42b.1\]]ma zhi ba gnyis su 'dod/_/yongs su shes dang spang ba dang /_/thob par mngon sum bya bas ni/_/lam gyi bden pa yang dag bshad/_/btags pa dang ni shes pa dang /_/de bzhin brjod pa rags pa yin/_/dam pa'i don ni gcig pu'o/_/don dang thob dang sgrub pa
