[\[55a.1\]]tshom rtsig pa 'jig mdzad de la 'dud/_/'dus ma byas shing lhun gyis grub/_/gzhan gyi rkyen gyis rtogs min pa/_/mkhyen dang brtse dang nus par ldan/_/don gnyis ldan pa'i sangs rgyas nyid/_/thog ma dbus mtha' med pa yi/_/rang bzhin yin
[\[55a.2\]]phyir 'dus ma byas/_/zhi ba chos kyi sku can phyir/_/lhun gyis grub ces bya bar brjod/_/so so rang gis rtogs bya'i phyir/_/gzhan gyi rkyen gyis rtogs min pa/_/de ltar rnam gsum rtogs phyir mkhyen/_/lam ston phyir na thugs brtse ba/_/nus pa ye shes
[\[55a.3\]]thugs rje yis/_/sdug bsngal nyon mongs spong phyir ro/_/dang po gsum gyis rang don te/_/phyi ma gsum gyis gzhan don yin/_/gang zhig med min yod min yod med ma yin yod med las gzhan du'ang /_/brtag par mi nus nges tshig dang bral so so
[\[55a.4\]]rang gis rig zhi ba/_/dri med ye shes 'od zer snang ldan dmigs pa kun la chags pa dang /_/sdang dang rab rib rnam par 'joms mdzad dam chos nyi ma de la 'dud/_/bsam med gnyis med rtog med pa/_/dag gsal gnyen po'i phyogs nyid kyis/_/gang zhig
[\[55a.5\]]gang gis chags bral ba/_/bden gnyis mtshan nyid can de chos/_/chags bral nyid ni 'gog pa dang /_/lam gyi bden pa dag gis bsdus/_/go rims ji bzhin de dag kyang /_/yon tan gsum gsum gyis rig bya/_/brtag min phyir dang brjod min
[\[55b\]]
[\[55b.1\]]phyir/_/'phags pas mkhyen phyir bsam med nyid/_/zhi nyid gnyis med rtog med de/_/dag sogs gsum ni nyi bzhin no/_/sems de rang bzhin 'od gsal bas na nyon mongs ngo bo med gzigs pas/_/gang dag 'gro kun bdag med mtha' zhi yang dag rtogs nas thams cad
[\[55b.2\]]la/_/rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rjes zhugs gzigs pa sgrib pa med pa'i blo mnga' ba/_/sems can rnam dag mtha' yas yul can ye shes gzigs mnga' de la 'dud/_/ji lta ji snyed nang gi ni/_/ye shes gzigs pa dag pa'i phyir/_/blo ldan phyir mi ldog pa'i tshogs/_/
[\[55b.3\]]bla med yon tan dang ldan nyid/_/'gro ba zhi ba'i chos nyid du/_/rtogs phyir ji lta nyid de yang /_/rang bzhin gyis ni yongs dag phyir/_/nyon mongs gdod nas zad phyir ro/_/shes bya mthar thug rtogs pa'i blos/_/thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos nyid ni/_/sems can
[\[55b.4\]]thams cad la yod par/_/mthong phyir ji snyed yod pa nyid/_/de ltar rtogs pa gang yin de/_/so so rang shes mthong ba nyid/_/dri med dbyings la chags med dang /_/thogs med phyir de dag pa yin/_/ye shes gzigs pa dag pas na/_/sangs rgyas ye shes bla med phyir/_/
[\[55b.5\]]'phags pa phyir mi ldog pa ni/_/lus can kun gyi skyabs yin no/_/ston pa bstan pa bslab don gyis/_/theg pa gsum dang byed gsum la/_/mos pa rnams kyi dbang byas nas/_/skyabs gsum rnam par bzhag pa yin/_/spang phyir bslu ba'i chos can phyir/_/med phyir
[\[55b.6\]]'jigs dang bcas pa'i phyir/_/chos rnams gnyis dang 'phags pa'i tshogs/_/gtan gyi skyabs mchog ma yin no/_/dam pa'i don du 'gro ba yi/_/skyabs ni sangs rgyas nyag gcig yin/_/thub pa chos kyi sku can phyir/_/tshogs kyang de yi mthar thug phyir/_/'byung ba dkon
[\[55b.7\]]phyir dri med phyir/_/mthu ldan phyir dang 'jig rten gyi/_/rgyan gyur phyir dang mchog nyid phyir/_/'gyur ba med phyir dkon mchog nyid/_/dri bcas de bzhin nyid dang dri ma med/_/dri med sangs rgyas yon tan rgyal ba'i mdzad/_/gang las dkon mchog dge ba gsum 'byung ba/_/
[\[56a\]]
[\[56a.1\]]don dam gzigs pa rnams kyi yul nyid do/_/dkon mchog gsum po 'di yi rigs/_/thams cad gzigs pa rnams kyi yul/_/de yang rnam bzhi go rims bzhin/_/rgyu bzhi yis ni bsam mi khyab/_/dag dang nyon mongs dang ldan phyir/_/ku nas nyon mongs med
[\[56a.2\]]dag phyir/_/rnam par dbye ba med chos phyir/_/lhun grub rnam par mi rtog phyir/_/rtogs bya rtogs pa de yi ni/_/yan lag rtogs par byed phyir te/_/go rims ji bzhin gnas gcig de/_/dag rgyu gsum ni rkyen yin no/_/rdzogs sangs sku ni 'phro phyir dang /_/
[\[56a.3\]]de bzhin nyid dbyer med phyir dang /_/rigs yod phyir na lus can kun/_/rtag tu sangs rgyas snying po can/_/sangs rgyas ye shes sems can tshogs zhugs phyir/_/rang bzhin dri med de ni gnyis med de/_/sangs rgyas rigs la de 'bras nyer brtags phyir/_/'gro kun
[\[56a.4\]]sangs rgyas snying po can du gsungs/_/ngo bo rgyu 'bras las ldan 'jug pa dang /_/gnas skabs de bzhin kun tu 'gro ba'i don/_/rtag tu mi 'gyur yon tan dbyer med ni/_/don dam dbyings kyi dgongs don yin zhes bya/_/rin chen nam mkha' chu dag bzhin/_/rtag tu
[\[56a.5\]]rang bzhin nyon mongs med/_/chos mos lhag pa'i shes rab dang /_/ting 'dzin snying brtse las byung ba/_/mthu dang gzhan du mi 'gyur dang /_/brlan pa'i ngo bo'i rang bzhin phyir/_/'di dag nor bu rin chen mkha'/_/chu yi yon tan chos mthun nyid/_/chos la khong khro bdag
[\[56a.6\]]lta dang /_/'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs dang /_/sems can don la ltos med nyid/_/'dod chen mu stegs nyan thos dang /_/rang byung rnams kyi sgrib rnam bzhi/_/dag rgyu lhag par mos pa la/_/sogs pa'i chos ni rnam bzhi nyid/_/theg mchog la mos sa
[\[56a.7\]]bon shes rab ni/_/sangs rgyas chos bskyed ma dang bsam gtan gyi/_/bde ba'i mngal gnas snying rje'i ma ma can/_/gang yin de dag thub pa'i rjes skyes sras/_/gtsang bdag bde dang rtag nyid kyi/_/yon tan pha rol phyin pa 'bras/_/sdug bsngal yid 'byung zhi thob par/_/
[\[56b\]]
[\[56b.1\]]'dun dang smon pa'i las can no/_/'di dag 'bras ni mdor bsdu na/_/chos kyi sku la phyin ci log_/rnam pa bzhi las bzlog pa yi/_/gnyen pos rab tu phye ba nyid/_/de ni rang bzhin dag phyir dang /_/bag chags spang phyir gtsang ba yin/_/bdag dang bdag med spros pa dag_/nye bar zhi
[\[56b.2\]]bas dam pa'i bdag_/yid kyi rang bzhin phung po dang /_/de rgyu log phyir bde ba nyid/_/'khor ba dang ni mya ngan 'das/_/mnyam pa nyid du rtogs phyir rtag_/bdag sred ma lus shes rab kyis bcad de/_/sems can sred phyir brtse ldan zhi thob min/_/de ltar blo brtse byang chub thabs brten
[\[56b.3\]]nas/_/'phags pa 'khor ba'am mya ngan 'da' mi 'gyur/_/gal te sangs rgyas khams med na/_/sdug la skyo bar mi 'gyur zhing /_/mya ngan 'das la 'dod pa dang /_/don gnyer smon pa'ang med par 'gyur/_/srid dang mya ngan 'das la de'i/_/sdug bde'i skyon yon mthong ba 'di/_/
[\[56b.4\]]rigs yod las yin gang phyir de/_/rigs med dag la med phyir ro/_/rgya mtsho che bzhin dpag med pa'i/_/yon tan rin chen mi zad gnas/_/dbyer med yon tan dang ldan pa'i/_/ngo bo nyid phyir mar me bzhin/_/chos sku rgyal ba'i ye shes dang /_/thugs rje'i khams ni bsdus pa'i
[\[56b.5\]]phyir/_/snod dang rin chen chu yis ni/_/rgya mtsho dang ni mtshungs par bstan/_/dri med gnas la mngon shes dang /_/ye shes dri med de nyid dang /_/rnam dbye med phyir mar me yi/_/snang dang dro mdog chos mtshungs can/_/so so'i skye 'phags rdzogs sangs kyi/_/de bzhin nyid dbye'i
[\[56b.6\]]'jug pa las/_/de nyid gzigs pas sems can la/_/rgyal ba'i snying po 'di bstan to/_/so so skye bo phyin ci log_/bden pa mthong ba bzlog pa ste/_/de bzhin gshegs pa ji lta bzhin/_/phyin ci ma log spros med nyid/_/ma dag ma dag dag pa dang /_/shin tu rnam dag go rims
[\[56b.7\]]bzhin/_/sems can byang chub sems dpa' dang /_/de bzhin gshegs pa zhes brjod do/_/ngo bo nyid la sogs pa'i don/_/'di drug gis ni bsdus pa yi/_/khams ni gnas skabs gsum dag tu/_/ming gsum gyis ni bstan pa yin/_/ji ltar rtog med bdag nyid can/_/nam mkha'
[\[57a\]]
[\[57a.1\]]kun tu rjes song ltar/_/sems kyi rang bzhin dri med dbyings/_/de bzhin kun tu 'gro ba nyid/_/de spyi'i mtshan nyid nyes pa dang /_/yon tan mthar thug khyab pa ste/_/gzugs kyi rnam pa dman pa dang /_/bar ma mchog la nam mkha' bzhin/_/
[\[57a.2\]]nyes pa glo bur dang ldan dang /_/yon tan rang bzhin nyid ldan phyir/_/ji ltar sngar bzhin phyis de bzhin/_/'gyur ba med pa'i chos nyid do/_/ji ltar nam mkha' kun song ba/_/phra phyir nye bar gos pa med/_/de bzhin sems can thams cad la/_/gnas 'di nye bar gos pa
[\[57a.3\]]med/_/ji ltar 'jig rten thams cad du/_/nam mkha' la ni skye zhing 'jig_/de bzhin 'dus ma byas dbyings la/_/dbang po rnams ni skye zhing 'jig_/ji ltar nam mkha' me rnams kyis/_/sngon chad nam yang tshig pa med/_/de bzhin 'di ni 'chi ba dang /_/na dang
[\[57a.4\]]rga ba'i mes mi 'tshig_/sa ni chu la chu rlung la/_/rlung ni mkha' la rab tu gnas/_/mkha' ni rlung dang chu dag dang /_/sa yi khams la gnas ma yin/_/de bzhin phung po khams dbang rnams/_/las dang nyon mongs dag la gnas/_/las dang nyon mongs tshul bzhin min/_/yid
[\[57a.5\]]la byed la rtag tu gnas/_/tshul bzhin ma yin yid byed ni/_/sems kyi dag pa la rab gnas/_/sems kyi rang bzhin chos rnams ni/_/thams cad la yang gnas pa med/_/sa dang 'dra ba phung po dang /_/skye mched khams rnams shes par bya/_/chu khams dang 'dra lus
[\[57a.6\]]can gyi/_/las dang nyon mongs shes bya ste/_/tshul bzhin ma yin yid byed ni/_/rlung gi khams dang 'dra bar lta/_/rang bzhin nam mkha'i khams bzhin du/_/de bzhin can min gnas pa med/_/tshul bzhin ma yin yid byed ni/_/sems kyi rang bzhin la gnas te/_
[\[57a.7\]]tshul bzhin ma yin yid byed kyis/_/las dang nyon mongs rab tu phye/_/las dang nyon mongs chu las ni/_/phung po skye mched khams rnams 'byung /_/de 'jig pa dang chags pa ltar/_/skye dang 'jig par 'gyur ba yin/_/sems kyi rang bzhin nam mkha' yi/_/khams ltar rgyu
[\[57b\]]
[\[57b.1\]]med rkyen med de/_/tshogs pa med cing skye ba dang /_/'jig dang gnas la'ang yod ma yin/_/sems kyi rang bzhin 'od gsal gang yin pa/_/de ni nam mkha' bzhin du 'gyur med de/_/yang dag min rtogs las byung 'dod chags sogs/_/glo bur dri mas de nyon mongs mi
[\[57b.2\]]'gyur/_/las dang nyon mongs chu sogs kyis/_/'di ni mngon par 'grub min te/_/'chi dang na dang rga ba'i me/_/mi bzad pas kyang 'tshig mi 'gyur/_/dus mtha' dmyal ba tha mal pa'i/_/me gsum 'chi dang na ba dang /_/rga ba'i me gsum rim bzhin du/_/de dag 'dra
[\[57b.3\]]bar shes par bya/_/skye 'chi na dang rga ba las grol ba/_/'di yi rang bzhin ji bzhin nyid rtogs te/_/skye sogs phongs dang bral yang de yi rgyus/_/blo ldan 'gro la snying rje bskyed phyir bsten/_/'phags pas 'chi dang na ba dang /_/rga ba'i sdug bsngal rtsad nas spangs/_/
[\[57b.4\]]las dang nyon mongs dbang gis skye/_/de la de med phyis de med/_/ji bzhin yang dag mthong ba'i phyir/_/skye sogs rnams las 'das gyur kyang /_/snying rje'i bdag nyid skye ba dang /_/'chi dang rga dang na bar ston/_/rgyal sras 'gyur med chos nyid 'di/_/rtogs nas ma rig
[\[57b.5\]]ldongs rnams kyis/_/skye ba la sogs dag tu ni/_/mthong ba gang yin de smad do/_/'phags pa'i spyod yul thob pa gang /_/byis pa'i spyod yul du ston te/_/de nyid phyir na 'gro ba yi/_/gnyen gyi thabs dang snying rje mchog_/de ni 'jig rten thams cad las/_/'das kyang
[\[57b.6\]]'jig rten las ma g.yos/_/'jig rten don du 'jig rten na/_/'jig rten dri mas ma gos spyod/_/ji ltar pad+ma chu nang du/_/skyes pa chu yis gos pa med/_/de bzhin 'di ni 'jig rten du/_/skyes kyang 'jig rten chos mi gos/_/bya ba sgrub la rtag tu blo/_/me bzhin du
[\[57b.7\]]ni 'bar ba dang /_/zhi ba'i bsam gtan snyoms 'jug la/_/rtag tu snyoms par zhugs pa yin/_/sngon gyi 'phen pa'i dbang dang ni/_/rnam rtog thams cad bral ba'i phyir/_/de ni lus can smin pa yi/_/don du 'bad pa byed ma yin/_/bstan dang gzugs sku dag dang
[\[58a\]]
[\[58a.1\]]ni/_/spyod dang spyod lam gyis kyang rung /_/gang zhig ji ltar gang gis 'dul/_/des de de lta nyid du shes/_/de ltar nam mkha'i mtha' klas kyi/_/'gro la rtag tu lhun grub par/_/thogs med blo ldan de yis ni/_/sems can don ni yang dag 'jug_/_
[\[58a.2\]]byang chub sems dpa'i tshul 'di ni/_/rjes thob de bzhin gshegs rnams dang /_/sems can yang dag sgrol ba la/_/'jig rten na ni mnyam pa nyid/_/de lta mod kyi sa rdul dang /_/rgya mtsho ba glang rmig rjes kyi/_/khyad par gang yin sangs rgyas dang /_/byang chub
[\[58a.3\]]sems dpa'i khyad de nyid/_/gzhan 'gyur min bdag mi zad chos ldan phyir/_/'gro skyabs phyi ma'i mtha' med mur thug phyir/_/de ni rtag tu gnyis med mi rtog phyir/_/'jig med chos kyang ma byas rang bzhin phyir/_/skye ba med cing 'chi ba med/_/gnod med rga ba
[\[58a.4\]]med pa ste/_/de ni rtag dang brtan phyir dang /_/zhi ba'i phyir dang g.yung drung phyir/_/de ni yid kyi rang bzhin gyi/_/lus kyi skye med rtag pa'i phyir/_/bsam mi khyab 'gyur 'chi 'pho yis/_/de ni mi 'chi brtan pa'i phyir/_/bag chags phra mo'i nad rnams kyis/_/gnod med
[\[58a.5\]]zhi ba nyid kyi phyir/_/zag med mngon par 'du byed kyis/_/g.yung drung phyir na rga ba med/_/de la tshig gnyis de bzhin gnyis/_/gnyis dang gnyis kyis go rims bzhin/_/'dus ma byas pa'i dbyings la ni/_/rtag pa la sogs don shes bya/_/mi zad yon tan dang ldan phyir/_/
[\[58a.6\]]gzhan 'gyur min bdag rtag pa'i don/_/mtha' yi mu dang mtshungs pa'i phyir/_/skyabs kyi bdag nyid brtan pa'i don/_/rnam par mi rtog rang bzhin phyir/_/gnyis med chos nyid zhi ba'i don/_/ma bcos yon tan nyid phyir na/_/'jig med don ni g.yung drung nyid/_/gang
[\[58a.7\]]phyir de ni chos sku de ni de bzhin gshegs/_/de ni 'phags pa'i bden pa don dam mya ngan 'das/_/de phyir nyi dang zer bzhin yon tan dbyer med pas/_/sangs rgyas nyid las ma gtogs mya ngan 'das pa med/_/mdor na zag med dbyings la ni/_/don gyi rab tu dbye ba bzhis/_/
[\[58b\]]
[\[58b.1\]]chos kyi sku la sogs pa yi/_/rnam grangs bzhir ni rig par bya/_/sangs rgyas chos dbyer med pa dang /_/de rigs de bzhin thob pa dang /_/brdzun med bslu med chos nyid dang /_/gdon nas rang bzhin zhi nyid do/_/rnam kun mngon rdzogs byang chub dang /_/dri ma bag chags bcas
[\[58b.2\]]spangs pa/_/sangs rgyas mya ngan 'das pa ni/_/dam pa'i don du gnyis med nyid/_/rnam pa thams cad grangs med pa/_/bsam med dri med yon tan dang /_/dbyer med mtshan nyid thar pa ste/_/thar pa gang de de bzhin gshegs/_/ji ltar ri mo 'dri byed pa/_/gzhan dang
[\[58b.3\]]gzhan la mkhas pa dag_/gang zhig yan lag gang shes pa/_/de gzhan nges zin med par 'gyur/_/de nas 'di la khyed kun gyis/_/nga yi gzugs ni gyis shig ces/_/mnga' bdag rgyal pos de dag la/_/bka' yis ras ni byin pa dang /_/de las de ni thos gyur te/_/
[\[58b.4\]]ri mo'i las la rab sbyor ro/_/de la mngon par sbyor rnams la/_/gcig gcig yul gzhan song gyur pa/_/de ni yul gzhan song bas na/_/de ma tshang phyir ri mo de/_/yan lag thams cad yongs rdzogs par/_/mi 'gyur bzhin shes dper byas so/_/de rnams 'dri
[\[58b.5\]]byed gang yin pa/_/sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod la sogs/_/rnam pa kun gyi mchog ldan pa'i/_/stong pa nyid ni gzugs su brjod/_/shes rab ye shes rnam grol rnams/_/gsal dang 'phro dang dag phyir dang /_/tha dad med phyir 'od dang zer/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor
[\[58b.6\]]rnams dang mtshungs/_/des na sangs rgyas ma thob par/_/mya ngan 'das pa mi thob ste/_/'od dang 'od zer spangs nas ni/_/nyi ma lta bar mi nus bzhin/_/de ltar rgyal ba'i snying po ni/_/rnam gzhag rnam pa bcu zhes brjod/_/nyon mongs sbubs nang gnas pa de/_/dpe
[\[58b.7\]]dag gis ni shes par bya/_/sangs rgyas pad ngan sbrang rtsi sbrang ma la/_/sbun la snying po mi gtsang nang na gser/_/sa la gter dang smyug sogs 'bras chung dang /_/gos hrul nang na rgyal ba'i sku dang ni/_/bud med ngan ma'i lto na mi bdag dang /_/sa la rin chen gzugs
[\[59a\]]
[\[59a.1\]]yod ji lta bar/_/glo bur nyon mongs dri mas bsgribs pa yi/_/sems can rnams la de bzhin khams 'di gnas/_/dri ma pad+ma srog chags spun pa mi gtsang sa 'bras gos hrul dang /_/sdug bsngal 'bar bas mngon par gdungs ba'i bud med sa yi
[\[59a.2\]]khams dang mtshungs/_/sangs rgyas sbrang rtsi snying po gser dang gter dang n+ya gro rin chen sku/_/gling bdag mchog dang rin chen gzugs dang dri med khams mchog mtshungs pa nyid/_/ji ltar mdog ngan pad ma'i khong gnas pa/_/mtshan stong gis 'bar de bzhin gshegs
[\[59a.3\]]pa ni/_/dri med lha yi mig ldan mis mthong nas/_/chu skyes 'dab ma'i sbubs nas 'byin byed pa/_/de bzhin bde gshegs mnar med gnas rnams la'ang /_/sangs rgyas spyan gyis rang chos nyid gzigs te/_/sgrib med phyi mtha'i mur gnas thugs rje yi/_/bdag cag sgrib
[\[59a.4\]]pa las ni grol bar mdzad/_/ji ltar mi sdug pad+ma zum la bde bar gshegs pa ni/_/de yi khong gnas lha mig mthong nas 'dab ma gcod byed ltar/_/chags sdang sogs dri sbubs bsgribs rdzogs sangs snying po 'gro gzigs te/_/thugs rjes thub pa de bzhin sgrib pa de ni
[\[59a.5\]]'joms par mdzad/_/ji ltar srog chags tshogs bskor sbrang rtsi ni/_/skyes bu mkhas pas de don gnyer ba yis/_/mthong nas thabs kyis de dang srog chags tshogs/_/kun nas bral bar rab tu byed pa bzhin/_/drang srong chen pos kun mkhyen spyan gyis ni/_/rig
[\[59a.6\]]khams sbrang rtsi dang 'dra de gzigs nas/_/de yi sgrib pa sbrang ma dang 'dra ba/_/gtan nas rab tu spong bar mdzad pa yin/_/ji ltar sbrang rtsi srog chags bye ba khrag khrig stong bsgribs sbrang rtsi don gnyer mis/_/sbrang ma de dag bsal te ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du sbrang rtsi'i bya byed pa/_/
[\[59a.7\]]de bzhin lus can la yod zag pa med pa'i shes pa sbrang ma'i rtsi dang 'dra/_/nyon mongs sbrang ma dang 'dra de 'joms pa la mkhas pa'i rgyal ba skyes bu bzhin/_/ji ltar spun ldan 'bru yi snying po ni/_/mi rnams kyis ni spyad byar mi 'gyur ba/_/zas sogs don du gnyer ba gang yin
[\[59b\]]
[\[59b.1\]]pa/_/de dag gis ni sbun nas de 'byin ltar/_/de bzhin sems can la yod nyon mongs kyi/_/dri ma dang 'dres rgyal ba'ang ji srid du/_/nyon mongs dri ma 'dres las ma grol ba/_/de srid rgyal mdzad srid gsum 'du mi byed/_/ji ltar sA lu bra bo nas 'bru'i snying po spun las
[\[59b.2\]]ma byung gra ma can/_/legs par ma bsgrubs mi rnams kyis ni spyad bya bza' ba zhim por mi 'gyur ltar/_/de bzhin sems can la yod chos kyi dbang phyug nyon mongs sbubs las ma grol lus/_/nyon mongs bkres pas nyen pa'i 'gro la chos kyi dga' ba'i ro ster 'gyur ba min/_/
[\[59b.3\]]ji ltar rab tu rgyu tshe mi yi gser/_/ljan ljin rul ba'i gnas su lhung gyur pa/_/mi 'jig chos can de ni der de bzhin/_/lo brgya mang po dag tu gnas pa de/_/lha mig rnam dag dang ldan lha yis der/_/mthong nas mi la 'di na yod pa'i gser/_/rin chen mchog 'di
[\[59b.4\]]sbyangs te rin chen gyis/_/bsgrub par bya ba gyis zhes smra ba ltar/_/de bzhin thub pas mi gtsang dang 'dra ba'i/_/nyon mongs su bying sems can yon tan ni/_/gzigs nas nyon mongs 'dam de dag bya'i phyir/_/skye dgu rnams la dam chos chu char 'bebs/_/ji ltar ljan ljin rul
[\[59b.5\]]pa'i gnas su lhung ba'i gser ni lha yis mthong gyur nas/_/kun tu dag par bya phyir mchog tu mdzes pa mi la nan gyis ston pa ltar/_/de bzhin rgyal bas nyon mongs mi gtsang chen por lhung gyur rdzogs sangs rin po che/_/sems can rnams la gzigs nas de dag bya phyir lus
[\[59b.6\]]can rnams la chos ston to/_/ji ltar mi dbul khyim nang sa 'og na/_/mi zad pa yi gter ni yod gyur la/_/mi des de ma shes te gter de yang /_/de la nga 'dir yod ces mi smra ltar/_/de bzhin yid kyi nang chud rin chen gter/_/dri med gzhag dang bsal med chos
[\[59b.7\]]nyid kyang /_/ma rtogs pas na dbul ba'i sdug bsngal ni/_/rnam mang rgyun du skye dgu 'dis myong ngo /_/ji ltar dbul po'i khyim nang du ni rin chen gter chud gyur pa'i mi la ni/_/rin chen gter bdag yod ces rjod par mi byed de ni mi yis shes min ltar/_/de bzhin chos
[\[60a\]]
[\[60a.1\]]gter yid kyi khyim gnas sems can rnams ni dbul po lta bu ste/_/de dag rnams kyis de thob bya phyir 'jig rten du ni drang srong yang dag bstams/_ji ltar a mra la sogs shing 'bras la/_/yod pa'i sa bon myu gu 'jig med chos/_/sa rmos chu
[\[60a.2\]]sogs ldan pa'i ljon shing gi_/rgyal po'i dngos po rim gyis 'grub pa ltar/_/sems can rnams kyi ma rig sogs 'bras kyi/_/pags sbubs nang chud chos khams dge ba yang /_/de bzhin dge ba de de la brten nas/_/rim gyis thub pa'i rgyal po'i dngos por 'gyur/_/
[\[60a.3\]]chu dang nyi ma'i 'od dang rlung dang sa dus nam mkha'i rkyen rnams kyis/_/ta la dang ni a mra'i 'bras spubs gseb nas shing skye ji ltar bar/_/sems can nyon mongs 'bras lpags nang chud rdzogs sangs sa bon myu gu yang /_/de bzhin dge rkyen de dang de las chos mthong 'phel
[\[60a.4\]]bar 'gyur ba yin/_/ji ltar rin chen las byas rgyal ba'i gzugs/_/gos hrul dri ngan gyis ni gtums gyur pa/_/lam gnas lha yis mthong nas grol bya'i phyir/_/lam gnas don de de la smra ba ltar/_/thogs med spyan mnga' rnam pa sna tshogs kyi/_/nyon mongs kyis
[\[60a.5\]]gtums bde gshegs dngos po nyid/_/dud 'gro la yang gzigs nas de bzhin de/_/thar par bya ba'i don du thabs ston mdzod/_/ji ltar rin chen rang bzhin de bzhin gshegs sku dri ngan gos gtums pa/_/lam gnas lha yi mig gis mthong nas thar phyir mi la ston pa ltar/_/de bzhin nyon
[\[60a.6\]]mongs gos hrul gyis gtums 'khor ba'i lam na gnas pa'i khams/_/dud 'gro la yang gzigs nas thar par bya phyir rgyal ba chos ston to/_/ji ltar mi mo gzugs ngan mgon med 'ga'/_/mgon med 'dug gnas su ni 'dug gyur la/_/mngal gyis rgyal po'i dpal
[\[60a.7\]]ni 'dzin byed pas/_/rang lto na yod mi bdag mi shes ltar/_/srid par skye ba mgon med khyim bzhin te/_/ma dag sems can mngal ldan bud med bzhin/_/de la gang zhig yod pas mgon bcas pa/_/dri med khams ni de yi mngal gnas bzhin/_/ji ltar bud med
[\[60b\]]
[\[60b.1\]]lus la dri bcas gos gyon mi sdug gzugs ldan pa/_/sa bdag mngal na gnas kyang mgon med khang par sdug bsngal mchog myong ltar/_/de bzhin bdag rang nang gnas mgon yod gyur kyang mgon med blo ldan pa/_/'gro ba nyon mongs dbang gis yid ma zhi bas sdug
[\[60b.2\]]bsngal gzhi la gnas/_/ji ltar nang gi gser zhun gzugs rgyas pa/_/zhi ba phyi rol sa yi rang bzhin can/_/mthong nas de shes pa dag nang gi gser/_/sbyang phyir phyi rol sgrib pa sel byed ltar/_/rang bzhin 'od gsal dri med rnams kyang ni/_/glo bur bar ni rnam par
[\[60b.3\]]gzigs gyur nas/_/rin chen 'byung gnas lta bu'i 'gro ba rnams/_/sgrib pa dag las sbyong mdzad byang chub mchog_/ji ltar dri med gser 'bar las byas sa yi nang du chud gyur gzugs/_/zhi de rang bzhin mkhas pas rig nas sa dag sel bar byed par ltar/_/de
[\[60b.4\]]bzhin kun mkhyen dag pa'i gser 'dra zhi ba'i yid ni mkhyen gyur nas/_/chos 'chad tshul gyis brdeg spyad sgrub pas sgrib pa dag ni sel bar mdzad/_/pad+ma srog chags bung ba dang /_/sbun pa dang ni mi gtsang sa/_/'bras shun gos hrul bud med kyi/_/mngal dang sa yi sbubs
[\[60b.5\]]na yang /_/sangs rgyas sbrang rtsi snying po bzhin/_/gser bzhin gter bzhin ljon pa bzhin/_/rin chen sku dang 'khor lo yis/_/bsgyur ba bzhin dang gser gzugs bzhin/_/sems can khams kyi nyon mongs sbubs/_/ma 'brel thog ma med pa na/_/
[\[60b.6\]]sems kyi rang bzhin dri med ni/_/thog ma med pa yin par brjod/_/chags dang sdang dang rmongs dang de'i/_/kun ldang drag dang bag chags dang /_/mthong sgom lam spang ma dag dang /_/dag pa'i sa la brten pa yi/_/dri ma rnam dgu pad+ma yi/_/sbubs sogs
[\[60b.7\]]dpe ni rab bstan te/_/nye ba'i nyon mongs sbubs kyi ni/_/dbye ba bye ba mtha' las 'das/_/chags sogs dri ma dgu po 'di/_/mdor bsdus nas ni go rims bzhin/_/pad+ma'i sbubs la sogs pa yi/_/dpe dgu dag gis yang dag bstan/_/dri 'di dag gis byis
[\[61a\]]
[\[61a.1\]]rnams dang /_/dgra bcom slob pa blo ldan rnams/_/rim bzhin bzhi dang gcig dang ni/_/gnyis dang gnyis kyis ma dag nyid/_/ji ltar pad+ma 'dam skyes de/_/mdun du gyur na yid dga' dang /_/phyis nas dga' ba med 'gyur ba/_/'dod
[\[61a.2\]]chags dga' ba de bzhin no/_/ji ltar srog chags sbrang ma ni/_/shin tu 'khrugs te mdung brdeg ltar/_/de bzhin zhe sdang skye bas na/_/snying la sdug bsngal skyed par byed/_/ji lta 'bras sogs snying po ni/_/phyi rol sbun pas bsgribs pa ltar/_/de bzhin snying po'i
[\[61a.3\]]don mthong ba/_/ma rig sgo nga'i sbubs kyis bsgribs/_/ji ltar mi gtsang mi mthun pa/_/de bzhin chags dang bcas rnams kyi/_/'dod pa bsten pa'i rgyu yin phyir/_/kun nas ldang ba mi gtsang 'dra/_/ji ltar nor ni bsgribs pas na/_/mi shes gter mi thob pa
[\[61a.4\]]ltar/_/de bzhin skye la rang byung nyid/_/ma rig bag chags sa yis bsgribs/_/ji ltar myug sogs rim skye bas/_/sa bon shun pa gcod pa ltar/_/de bzhin de nyid mthong ba yis/_/mthong spang rnams ni bzlog par 'gyur/_/'phags pa'i lam dang 'brel
[\[61a.5\]]pa las/_/'jig tshogs snying po bcom rnams kyis/_/bsgom lam ye shes spang bya rnams/_/gos hrul dag dang mtshungs par bstan/_/sa bdun la brten dri ma ni/_/mngal sbubs dri ma dag dang mtshungs/_/mngal sbubs bral 'dra mi rtog pa'i/_/ye shes
[\[61a.6\]]rnam par smin pa bzhin/_/sa gsum rjes 'brel dri ma rnams/_/sa 'dam gos bzhin shes bya ste/_/bdag nyid chen po rdo rje lta'i/_/ting nge 'dzin gyis gzhom bya yin/_/de ltar chags sogs dri ma dgu/_/pad+ma la sogs dag dang mtshungs/_/rang bzhin
[\[61a.7\]]gsum gyis bsdus phyir khams/_/sangs rgyas sogs dang chos mtshungs so/_/'di yi rang bzhin chos sku dang /_/de bzhin nyid dang rigs kyang ste/_/de ni dpe gsum gcig dang ni/_/lnga rnams kyis ni shes par bya/_/chos sku rnam gnyis shes bya ste/_/chos
[\[61b\]]
[\[61b.1\]]dbyings shin tu dri med dang /_/de yi rgyu mthun zab pa dang /_/sna tshogs tshul ni ston pa'o/_/'jig rten 'das phyir 'jig rten na/_/'di la dpe ni mi dmigs pas/_/de bzhin gshegs pa nyid dang khams/_/'dra ba nyid du bstan pa yin/_/phra mo zab mo'i tshul
[\[61b.2\]]bstan ni/_/sbrang rtsi ro gcig pa bzhin te/_/rnam pa sna tshogs tshul bstan ni/_/sna tshogs sbubs snying bzhin shes bya/_/rang bzhin 'gyur ba med pa dang /_/dge dang rnam par dag pa'i phyir/_/de bzhin nyid 'di gser gyi ni/_/gzugs dang mtshungs par
[\[61b.3\]]brjod pa yin/_/gter dang 'bras bu'i shing bzhin du/_/rigs de rnam gnyis shes bya ste/_/thog med rang bzhin gnas pa dang /_/yang dag blang ba mchog nyid do/_/rigs 'di gnyis las sangs rgyas kyi/_/sku gsum thob par 'dod pa yin/_/dang po'i sku ni
[\[61b.4\]]dang po ste/_/gnyis pa yis ni phyi ma gnyis/_/ngo bo nyid sku mdzes pa ni/_/rin chen sku 'drar shes bya ste/_/rang bzhin gyis ni byas min dang /_/yon tan rin chen gter yin phyir/_/chos chen rgyal srid che ldan phyir/_/rdzogs longs 'khor los sgyur bzhin no/_/
[\[61b.5\]]gzugs brnyan gyi ni rang bzhin phyir/_/sprul pa gser gyi gzugs lta bu/_/rang byung rnams kyi don dam de/_/dad pa nyid kyis rtogs bya yin/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'od 'bar ba/_/mig med pas ni mthong ba med/_/'di la bsal bya ci yang med/_/gzhag par bya ba
[\[61b.6\]]cung zad med/_/yang dag nyid la yang dag lta/_/yang dag mthong na rnam par grol/_/rnam dbye bcas pa'i mtshan nyid can/_/glo bur dag gis khams stong gi_/rnam dbye med pa'i mtshan nyid can/_/bla med chos kyis stong ma yin/_/sprin dang rmi lam sgyu bzhin
[\[61b.7\]]de dang der/_/shes bya thams cad rnam kun stong pa zhes/_/gsungs nas yang 'dir rgyal rnams sems can la/_/sangs rgyas snying po yod ces ci ste gsungs/_/sems zhum sems can dman la brnyas pa dang /_/yang dag min 'dzin yang dag chos la skur/_/bdag
[\[62a\]]
[\[62a.1\]]cag lhag pa'i skyon lnga gang dag la/_/yod pa de dag de spang don du gsungs/_/yang dag mtha' ni 'dus byas kyis/_/rnam pa thams cad dben pa ste/_/nyon mongs las dang rnam smin don/_/sprin la sogs pa bzhin du brjod/_/nyon
[\[62a.2\]]mongs sprin 'dra bya ba yin/_/las ni rmi lam longs spyod bzhin/_/nyon mongs las kyi rnam par smin/_/phung po sgyu ma sprul pa bzhin/_/sngar ni de ltar rnam bzhag nas/_/slar yang bla ma'i rgyud 'dir ni/_/nyes pa lnga dag spang ba'i phyir/_/khams yod nyid
[\[62a.3\]]ces bstan pa yin/_/'di ltar de ni ma thos par/_/bdag la brnyas pa'i nyes pa yis/_/sems ni zhum pa 'ga' zhig nas/_/byang chub sems ni skye mi 'gyur/_/gang la byang chub sems skyes pas/_/bdag ni mchog ces rlom pa na/_/byang chub sems ma skyes
[\[62a.4\]]pa la/_/dman pa'i 'du shes rab tu 'jug_/de ltar sems pa de la ni/_/yang dag shes pa mi skye ba/_/des na yang dag min 'dzin cing /_/yang dag don ni rig mi 'gyur/_/bcos ma glo bur ba nyid phyir/_/sems can skyon de yang dag min/_/yang dag nyes
[\[62a.5\]]de bdag med pa/_/yon tan rang bzhin dag pa yin/_/yang dag min pa'i nyes 'dzin cing /_/yang dag yon tan skur 'debs pa/_/blo ldan bdag dang sems can la/_/mtshungs mthong byams pa thob mi 'gyur/_/'di ltar de ni thos pa las/_/spro dang ston pa bzhin
[\[62a.6\]]gus dang /_/shes rab ye shes byams chen skye/_/chos lnga skye phyir de las ni/_/kha na ma tho med mtshungs lta/_/skyon med yon tan ldan pa dang /_/bdag dang sems can mtshungs byams las/_/sangs rgyas nyid ni myur du 'thob/_/theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma'i bstan bcos
[\[62a.7\]]dkon mchog gi rigs rnam par dbye ba las/_de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po'i skabs te dang po'o//_//dag thob bral ba rang bzhin don/_/de brten zab dang rgya che dang /_/bdag nyid chen po de yang ni/_/ji srid dus dang ji lta nyid/_/ngo bo rgyu dang 'bras bu dang /_/
[\[62b\]]
[\[62b.1\]]las dang ldan la 'jug pa dang /_/de rtag bsam mi khyab nyid kyis/_/sangs rgyas sa ni mnyam par gzhag_/rang bzhin 'od gsal zhes brjod gang yin nyi dang mkha' bzhin glo bur gyi/_/nyon mongs shes bya'i sprin tshogs stug po'i sgrib pa yis ni bsgribs
[\[62b.2\]]gyur pa/_/dri med sangs rgyas yon tan kun ldan rtag brtan g.yung drung sangs rgyas nyid/_/de ni chos la mi rtog rnam 'byed ye shes dag la brten nas 'thob/_/sangs rgyas nyid ni dbyer med pa/_/dag pa'i chos kyis rab phye ba/_/nyi ma mkha' bzhin ye shes dang /_/
[\[62b.3\]]spangs pa gnyis kyi mtshan nyid do/_/'od gsal byas min dbyer med par/_/'jug can gang gA'i klung gi ni/_/rdul las 'das phyir sangs rgyas kyi/_/chos rnams kun dang ldan pa nyid/_/rang bzhin gyis ni ma grub dang /_/khyab dang glo bur ba nyid kyis/_/nyon mongs
[\[62b.4\]]shes bya'i sgrib pa der/_/sprin dang 'dra bar brjod pa yin/_/sgrib pa gnyis dang bral ba yi/_/rgyu ni ye shes gnyis yin te/_/mi rtog pa dang de yi ni/_/rjes thob de ni ye shes 'dod/_/dri med chu ldan rim rgyas pad+mas khebs pa'i mtsho bzhin dang /_/sgra gcan kha
[\[62b.5\]]nas thar ba'i zla ba nya ba lta bu dang /_/sprin tshogs nyon mongs dag las grol ba'i nyi ma lta bur ni/_/dri med yon tan ldan phyir 'od zer snang ldan de nyid do/_/thub pa khyu mchog sbrang rtsi snying po dang /_/rin chen gser dang gter dang ljon pa bzhin/_/dri med rin chen bde gshegs
[\[62b.6\]]sku dang ni/_/sa bdag gser gyi gzugs 'dra rgyal ba nyid/_/chu mtsho sogs bzhin 'dod chags sogs/_/glo bur nyon mongs dag pa ni/_/mdor na mi rtog ye shes kyi/_/'bras bu yin par rab tu brjod/_/rnam pa kun gyi mchog ldan pa'i/_/sangs rgyas sku ni nges
[\[62b.7\]]thob pa/_/de ni rjes las thob pa yi/_/ye shes 'bras bu yin par ston/_/'dod chags rdul ni spang phyir dang /_/gdul bya yi ni pad+ma la/_/bsam gtan chu ni 'bab phyir de/_/chu dag rdzing dang mtshungs pa nyid/_/zhe sdang sgra gcan las grol bas/_/snying rje byams
[\[63a\]]
[\[63a.1\]]chen 'od zer gyis/_/'gro ba khyab pa'i phyir na de/_/dri med zla ba nya ba bzhin/_/gti mug sprin las rnam grol ba/_/'gro bar ye shes 'od zer gyis/_/mun pa sel phyir sangs rgyas nyid/_/de ni dri med nyi ma bzhin/_/mi mnyam mnyam pa'i chos phyir dang /_/
[\[63a.2\]]dam chos ro ni sbyin mdzad dang /_/shun pa dang ni bral phyir de/_/bde gshegs sbrang rtsi snying po bzhin/_/dag phyir yon tan rdzas kyis ni/_/dbul ba sel bar byed phyir dang /_/rnam grol 'bras bu 'byin byed phyir/_/gser dang gter dang ljon pa bzhin/_/rin chen chos kyi
[\[63a.3\]]sku phyir dang /_/rkang gnyis bdag po'i mchog phyir dang /_/rin chen gzugs kyi rnam pa'i phyir/_/de ni rin chen rgyal gser bzhin/_/zag pa med khyab 'jig med chos can te/_/brtan zhi rtag pa 'pho med gnas yin no/_/de bzhin gshegs pa mkha' bzhin dag pa yi/_/dbang
[\[63a.4\]]po drug don nyams su myong ba'i rgyu/_/'byung med gzugs don blta dang gtam bzang ni/_/gtsang ma mnyan dang bde gshegs tshul khrims kyi/_/dri gtsang snom dang 'phags chen dam chos ro/_/myang dang ting 'dzin reg bde nyams myong dang /_/rang gi ngo bo nyid kyi zab pa'i tshul/_/
[\[63a.5\]]rtogs pa'i rgyur gyur zhib mor bsams pa na/_/don dam bde mdzad de bzhin gshegs pa ni/_/nam mkha' bzhin du rgyu mtshan rnams dang bral/_/mdor na ye shes gnyis po yi/_/las su 'di ni shes bya ste/_/grol ba'i sku ni rdzogs pa dang /_/chos kyi sku ni sbyong ba'o/_/
[\[63a.6\]]rnam grol chos kyi sku dag ni/_/rnam gnyis rnam gcig shes bya ste/_/zag pa med phyir khyab pa'i phyir/_/'dus ma byas phyir gnas nyid phyir/_/nyon mongs rnams ni bag chags dang /_/bcas pa 'gags phyir zag med de/_/chags med thogs pa med pa'i phyir/_/ye shes
[\[63a.7\]]khyab pa nyid du 'dod/_/gtan du 'jig pa med pa yi/_/rang bzhin yin phyir 'dus ma byas/_/'jig med nyid ni bstan pa ste/_/brtan sogs rnams kyis de bshad do/_/'jig pa rnam bzhir shes bya ste/_/brtan sogs dag las bzlog phyir ro/_/myags dang
[\[63b\]]
[\[63b.1\]]rnam 'gyur chad pa dang /_/bsam mi khyab 'gyur 'pho ba ste/_/de med phyir na brtan zhi dang /_/rtag dang 'pho med shes par bya/_/dri med shes de dkar po yi/_/chos kyi rten yin phyir na gnas/_/ji ltar rgyu min nam mkha' ni/_/gzugs mthong ba dang sgra dang dri/_/ro dang
[\[63b.2\]]reg dang chos rnams ni/_/thos la sogs pa'i rgyu yin ltar/_/de bzhin sku gnyis sgrib med pa'i/_/sbyor bas bstan pa'i dbang don la/_/zag pa med pa'i yon tan dag_/skye ba yi ni rgyu yin no/_/bsam med rtag brtan zhi ba g.yung drung nyid/_/rab tu zhi khyab rtog
[\[63b.3\]]bral nam mkha' bzhin/_/chags med kun tu thogs med rtsub reg spangs/_/lta gzung med dge sangs rgyas dri ma med/_/rnam grol chos kyi sku dag gis/_/rang dang gzhan gyi don bstan te/_/rang gzhan don rten de la ni/_/bsam mi khyab sogs yon tan ldan/_
[\[63b.4\]]thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yul/_/sangs rgyas shes gsum yul min phyir/_/ye shes lus can rnams kyis ni/_/bsam mi khyab par rtogs par bya/_/phra phyir thos pa'i yul min te/_/don dam yin phyir bsam bya'i min/_chos nyid zab phyir 'jig rten pa'i/_/
[\[63b.5\]]bsgom pa la sogs yul ma yin/_/gang phyir gzugs la dmus long bzhin/_/byis pas de sngon mthong ma myong /_/btsas pa'i khyim nas bu chung gis/_/nyi ma'i gzugs bzhin 'phags pas kyang /_/skye dang bral phyir rtag pa ste/_/'gag med phyir na brtan pa yin/_/
[\[63b.6\]]gnyis med phyir de zhi ba ste/_/g.yung drung chos nyid gnas phyir ro/_/rab zhi 'gog pa'i bden pa'i phyir/_/thams cad rtogs phyir khyab pa nyid/_/gnas pa med phyir rtog med de/_/nyon mongs spangs phyir chags pa med/_/shes bya'i sgrib kun dag pa'i phyir/_/thams
[\[63b.7\]]cad du ni thogs pa med/_/gnyis med las su rung ba'i phyir/_/rtsub pa'i reg dang bral ba yin/_/de gzugs med phyir bltar med de/_/mtshan ma med phyir gzung du med/_/dge ba rang bzhin dag pa'i phyir/_/dri med dri ma spangs phyir ro/_/thog ma dbus mtha'
[\[64a\]]
[\[64a.1\]]med cing rnam dbyer med/_/gnyis med gsum bral dri med rnam rtog med/_/chos dbyings rang bzhin gang yin de rtogs pa/_/mnyam par bzhag pa'i rnal 'byor pa yis mthong /_/gzhal med gang gA'i bye ma las 'das pa/_/bsam med mnyam
[\[64a.2\]]med yon tan rnams dang ldan/_/de bzhin gshegs pa'i dri med dbyings de ni/_/bag chags bcas pa'i nyes pa rnam spangs pa'o/_/sna tshogs dam chos 'od zer mnga' ba'i skus/_/'gro ba'i rnam grol don grub la brtson pa/_/mdzad pa yid bzhin nor bu'i rgyal bzhin
[\[64a.3\]]te/_/sna tshogs dngos kyang de yi rang bzhin min/_/'jig rten zhi ba'i lam la 'jug pa dang /_/rab tu smin dang lung ston rgyu yi gzugs/_/gang yin de yang 'dir ni rtag gnas te/_/nam mkha'i khams su gzugs kyi khams bzhin no/_/rang byung rnams kyi
[\[64a.4\]]thams cad mkhyen/_/sangs rgyas nyid ces gang brjod pa/_/mchog tu mya ngan 'das bsam med/_/dgra bcom so so'i bdag gyur pa/_/de dbye zab dang rgya che dang /_/bdag nyid chen po'i yon tan gyi/_/chos kyis rab phye rang bzhin la/_/sogs pa'i sku gsum dag gis
[\[64a.5\]]'jug_/de la sangs rgyas rnams kyi ni/_/ngo bo nyid sku mtshan nyid lnga/_/mdor na yon tan lnga dang ni/_/ldan pa nyid du rig par bya/_/'dus ma byas shing rnam dbyer med/_/mtha' gnyis dag ni rnam par spangs/_/nyon mongs shes bya snyoms 'jug gi_/sgrib gsum
[\[64a.6\]]las ni nges grol te/_/dri med rnam par rtog med dang /_/rnal 'byor rnams kyi yul yin phyir/_/chos dbyings ngo bo nyid kyis ni/_/dag pa'i phyir na 'od gsal ba/_/gzhal med grangs med bsam med pa/_/mnyam med dag pa'i mthar thug pa'i/_/yon tan rnams dang yang
[\[64a.7\]]dag par/_/ngo bo nyid kyi sku ldan te/_rgya che'i phyir dang grangs med phyir/_/rtog ge'i yul ni min phyir dang /_/'ba' zhig bag chags bcas spang phyir/_/gzhal med la sogs go rims bzhin/_/sna tshogs chos la rdzogs longs spyod/_/rang bzhin chos ni snang phyir
[\[64b\]]
[\[64b.1\]]dang /_/thugs rje dag pa'i rgyu mthun pa/_/'gro don rgyun mi 'chad phyir dang /_/rnam par rtog med lhun grub par/_/'dod pa ji bzhin yongs skong phyir/_/yid bzhin nor bu'i rdzu 'phrul gyis/_/rdzogs par longs spyod rnam par gnas/_/brjod ston mdzad rgyun mi
[\[64b.2\]]'chad dang /_/mngon par 'du byed med pa dang /_/de yi ngo bo min ston la/_/'dir ni sna tshogs rnam lngar ston/_/ji ltar tshon ni sna tshogs kyis/_/nor bu de dngos min snang ltar/_/de bzhin 'gro rkyen sna tshogs pas/_/khyab bdag de dngos min par snang /_/thugs rje
[\[64b.3\]]chen pos 'jig rten mkhyen/_/'jig rten kun la gzigs nas ni/_/chos kyi sku las ma g.yos par/_/sprul pa'i rang bzhin sna tshogs kyis/_/skye ba mngon par skye ba dang /_/dga' ldan gnas nas 'pho ba dang /_/lhums su 'jug dang bltams pa dang /_/bzo yi gnas la
[\[64b.4\]]mkhas pa dang /_/btsun mo'i 'khor dgyes rol pa dang /_/nges 'byung dka' ba spyod pa dang /_/byang chub snying por gshegs pa dang /_/bdud sde 'joms dang rdzogs par ni/_/byang chub chos kyi 'khor lo dang /_/mya ngan 'das par gshegs mdzad rnams/_/yongs su
[\[64b.5\]]ma dag zhing rnams su/_/srid pa ji srid gnas par ston/_/mi rtag sdug bsngal bdag med dang /_/zhi ba'i sgra yis thabs mkhyen pas/_/sems can srid gsum skyo bskyed nas/_/mya ngan 'das la rab 'jug mdzad/_/zhi ba'i lam la rab zhugs pa/_/mya ngan 'das thob 'du

[\[65a\]]
[\[65a.1\]]can zad med dang /_/brtse dang 'phrul dang mkhyen dang phun tshogs ldan/_/chos kyi dbang phyug 'chi ba'i bdud bcom dang /_/ngo bo med phyir 'jig rten mgon pos brtag_/lus dang srog dang longs spyod rnams/_/btang nas dam chos 'dzin phyir dang /_/
[\[65a.2\]]sems can kun la phan ba'i phyir/_/dang por dam bcas mthar phyin phyir/_/sangs rgyas nyid ni gtsang ba dang /_/dag pa'i thugs rje rab 'jug phyir/_/rdzu 'phrul rkang pa ston par ni/_/de yis gnas par spyod pa'i phyir/_/mkhyen pas 'khor dang mya ngan 'das/_/gnyis

[\[65a.5\]]phyir don dam gyis bsdus phyir/_/rtogs gnas min phyir dpe las 'das pa'i phyir/_/bla na med phyir srid zhis ma bsdus phyir/_/rgyal yul 'phags rnams kyis kyang bsam mi khyab/_/bsam med brjod du med phyir te/_/brjod med don dam yin phyir ro/_/don dam
[\[65a.6\]]brtag bya min phyir te/_/brtag min rjes dpag bya min phyir/_/dpag min bla na med pa'i phyir/_/bla na med pa ma bsdus phyir/_/ma bsdus gnas pa med phyir te/_/yon tan skyon rtog med phyir ro/_/rgyu lnga dag gis phra ba'i phyir/_/chos sku bsam mi khyab pa ste/_/drug
[\[65a.7\]]pas de yi dngos min phyir/_/gzugs sku bsam mi khyab pa'o/_/bla med ye shes thugs rje che sogs yon tan gyis/_/yon tan pha rol byon pa'i rgyal ba bsam mi khyab/_/des na rang byung rnams kyi tha ma'i tshul 'di ni/_/drang srong chen po dbang thob rnams kyis kyang rig min/_/
[\[65b\]]
[\[65b.1\]]theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma'i bstan bcos dkon mchog gi rigs rnam par dbye ba las/_byang chub kyi skabs te gnyis pa'o//_//rang don gzhan don don dam sku dang ni/_/de la brten pa kun rdzob sku nyid de/_/bral dang rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ni/_/yon tan

[\[66a\]]
[\[66a.1\]]rgyu ba ltar/_/de bzhin tshogs nang thub pa'i dbang po seng ge yang /_/legs gnas ltos med brtan pa'i rtsal dang ldan par gnas/_/'khrul dang ca co mi mnga' ste/_/ston la dran pa nyams mi mnga'/_/mnyam par ma bzhag thugs mi mnga'/_/

[\[66b.1\]]dman med pa dang /_/phyag ring yongs su dag pa'i sku/_/'od kyi dkyil 'khor dang ldan dang /_/mgrin pa dri med dung 'dra dang /_/'gram pa ri dgas rgyal po 'dra/_/tshems ni bzhi bcu mnyam pa dang /_/rab dag tshems thags bzang ba dang /_/rnam dag tshems mnyam

[\[67a.1\]]gang phyir brtan pa mi phyed phyir/_/mi phyed phyir na rdo rje bzhin/_/'jigs pa med phyir ltos med phyir/_/brtan phyir rtsal ni phun tshogs pas/_/thub pa seng ge seng ge bzhin/_/'khor gyi tshogs su 'jigs mi mnga'/_/kun mngon mkhyen pas gang

[\[67a.6\]]dkon mchog gi rigs rnam par dbye ba las/_yon tan gyi skabs te gsum pa'o//_//gdul bya'i khams dang 'dul ba'i thabs dang ni/_/gdul bya'i khams kyi gdul bya'i bya ba dang /_/de yi yul dang dus su gshegs pa la/_/khyab bdag rtag tu

[\[67b\]]
[\[67b.1\]]kun la khyad med rnam gzigs nas/_/nyon mongs shes bya'i sprin gyi dra ba sangs rgyas rnams kyi thugs rje'i rlung gis rnam par gtor/_/gang zhig gang gis gdul ba yi/_/bya gang gang du gang gi tshe/_/de yi rnam rtog skye med phyir/_/thub pa rtag tu lhun gyis grub/_/

[\[67b.5\]]sems can thams cad nyer 'tsho'i phyir/_/tshogs gnyis dag ni nyi ma bzhin/_/rgya che mtha' dang dbus med phyir/_/byang chub nam mkha'i khams bzhin no/_/yang dag rdzogs sangs chos nyid phyir/_/sems can khams ni gter dang 'dra/_/glo bur khyab dang ma grub
[\[67b.6\]]phyir/_/de yi nyon mongs sprin tshogs bzhin/_/de 'thor bar ni nyer gnas phyir/_/thugs rje mi bzad rlung dang 'dra/_/gzhan gyi dbang gis nges 'byung dang /_/bdag dang sems can mtshungs gzigs dang /_/mdzad pa yongs su ma rdzogs phyir/_/'khor ba srid
[\[67b.7\]]du mdzad mi 'chad/_/brgya byin rnga sprin tshangs pa dang /_/nyi ma nor bu rin chen bzhin/_/de bzhin gshegs pa sgra brnyan bzhin/_/nam mkha' dang ni sa bzhin no/_/ji ltar baiDUr dag pa yi/_/rang bzhin sa steng 'dir 'gyur te/_/dag phyir lha yi dbang po der/_/
[\[68a\]]
[\[68a.1\]]lha yi bu mo'i tshogs dang bcas/_/rnam par rgyal ba'i khang bzang dang /_/lha gnas de las gzhan dag dang /_/de yi gzhal yas sna tshogs dang /_/lha rdzas rnam mang de mthong ngo /_/de nas skyes pa bud med tshogs/_/sa yi steng na gnas pa
[\[68a.2\]]rnams/_/snang ba de ni mthong gyur te/_/nged kyang ring por mi thogs par/_/lha dbang 'di 'drar gyur cig ces/_/de 'dra'i smon lam 'debs byed cing /_/de thob don du dge ba ni/_/yang dag blangs te gnas par gyur/_/de dag dge ba'i las des ni/_/'di snang tsam
[\[68a.3\]]zhes de lta bur/_/shes pa med kyang sa steng nas/_/'phos te lha ru skye bar 'gyur/_/snang ba de ni shin tu yang /_/rtog pa med cing g.yo ba med/_/de lta mod kyi sa steng na/_/don chen gyis ni nye bar gnas/_/de bzhin dad sogs dri med can/_/dad sogs yon
[\[68a.4\]]tan bsgom pa yi/_/rang sems la snang rdzogs sangs rgyas/_/mtshan dang dpe byad ldan pa dang /_/'chag pa dang ni bzhengs pa dang /_/bzhugs pa dang ni gzims pa dang /_/spyod lam sna tshogs mdzad pa can/_/zhi ba'i chos ni gsung ba dang /_/mi gsung mnyam
[\[68a.5\]]par bzhag gyur pa/_/cho 'phrul rnam pa sna tshogs dag_/mdzad pa gzi mdangs chen po can/_/sems can rnams kyis mthong bar 'gyur/_/de mthong nas kyang 'dod ldan pa/_/sangs rgyas nyid ces rab sbyor te/_/de rgyu yang dag blangs nas ni/_/'dod pa'i go 'phang thob
[\[68a.6\]]par byed/_/snang ba de ni shin tu yang /_/rtog med g.yo ba med pa nyid/_/de lta na yang 'jig rten na/_/don chen pos ni nye bar gnas/_/'di ni rang sems snang ba zhes/_/so so'i skye bos mi shes mod/_/de lta na yang gzugs mthong ste/_/de dag la ni don yod
[\[68a.7\]]'gyur/_/rim gyis de mthong la brten nas/_/theg pa 'di la gnas pa rnams/_/nang gi dam pa chos sku ni/_/ye shes mig gis mthong bar 'gyur/_/ji ltar sa kun nyam nga'i gnas gzhan dang bral dri med bai DUr+ya/_/gsal mdzes nor bu'i yon tan dri bral dpal
[\[68b\]]
[\[68b.1\]]ldan steng ni mnyam gyur te/_/dag phyir der ni lha dag sna tshogs lha dbang lha yi gzugs shar ste/_/rim gyis sa yi yon tan bral phyir de ni slar yang mi snang 'gyur/_/de dngos thob phyir bsnyen gnas brtul zhugs nges par sbyin sogs la phyogs pa/_/bud

[\[68b.3\]]lha dbang lus kyi gzugs brnyan snang ba ltar/_/de bzhin 'gro sems gzhi gtsang ma la/_/thub pa'i dbang po'i sku yi gzugs brnyan 'char/_/'gro bar gzugs brnyan 'char nub rnyog med dang /_/rnyog pa'i rang sems rab 'jug dbang gis 'jug_/ji ltar
[\[68b.4\]]'jig rten dag na gzugs snang ltar/_/de bzhin yod dang zhig ces de mi lta/_/ji ltar lha nang lha rnams kyi/_/sngon gyi dkar po'i mthu yis ni/_/'bad dang gnas dang yid gzugs dang /_/rnam par rtog pa med bzhin du/_/mi rtag sdug bsngal bdag med dang /_/
[\[68b.5\]]zhi ba'i sgra yis bag med pa'i/_/lha rnams thams cad yang dang yang /_/chos kyi rngas ni skul byed ltar/_/de bzhin khyab bdag 'bad sogs dang /_/bral yang 'gro ba ma lus pa/_/sangs rgyas gsung gis khyab mdzad de/_/skal ldan rnams la chos ston to/_/ji
[\[68b.6\]]ltar lha nang lha rnams kyi/_/rnga sgra rang gi las las byung /_/de bzhin 'jig rten thub pa'i chos/_/gsung ba rang gi las las byung /_/'bad nas lus dang sems bral ba'i/_/sgra de ji ltar zhi sgrub ltar/_/de bzhin 'bad sogs dang bral ba'i/_/chos de zhi bsgrub
[\[68b.7\]]par byed/_/ji ltar lha yi grong na rnga sgra'i rgyus byung mi 'jigs sbyin pa ni/_/nyon mongs g.yul du 'jug tshe lha min dpung rgyal rtsed mo sal ba ltar/_/de bzhin 'jig rten dag na bsam gtan gzugs med la sogs rgyus byung ba/_/sems can nyon mongs sdug
[\[69a\]]
[\[69a.1\]]bsngal rab 'joms zhi ba bla med lam tshul brjod/_/gang phyir skye kun pha nyid dang /_/phan bde cho 'phrul gsum ldan pa/_/de phyir thub dbyangs lha rdzas kyi/_/sil snyan rnams las khyad par 'phags/_/lhar ni rnga yi sgra chen po/_/sar
[\[69a.2\]]gnas rnams kyi rnar mi 'gro/_/sangs rgyas rnga sgra 'khor ba yi/_/sa 'og 'jig rten dag tu 'gro_/lhar ni lha yi sil snyan bye ba mang /_/'dod me mngon par 'phel ba'i don du sgrog_/thugs rje'i bdag nyid rnams kyi dbyangs gcig kyang /_/sdug bsngal
[\[69a.3\]]me rab zhi ba'i don du 'jug_/lhar ni mdzes shing yid 'ong sil snyan sgra/_/sems kyi rgod pa 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i rgyu/_/thugs rje'i bdag nyid de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung /_/ting 'dzin sems gtod bsam pa skul byed nyid/_/mdor na ma
[\[69a.4\]]lus 'jig rten khams su yang /_/lha dang sa gnas bde ba'i rgyu gang yin/_/de ni ma lus 'jig rten khyab snang ba/_/dbyangs nyid la ni rab tu brten par brjod/_/ji ltar rna ba dang bral bas/_/phra mo'i sgra ni mi myong zhing /_/thams cad lha yi rna bar yang /_/
[\[69a.5\]]rna lam du ni mi 'gro bzhin/_/de bzhin chos phra mchog tu ni/_/zhib mo'i ye shes spyod yul yang /_/nyon mongs med yid 'ga' zhig gi_/rna ba'i lam du 'gyur ba yin/_/ji ltar dbyar gyi dus na sprin/_/lo tog phun sum tshogs pa'i rgyu/_/chu yi phung po
[\[69a.6\]]'bad med par/_/sa la rgyun du 'bebs pa ltar/_/de bzhin thugs rje'i sprin las ni/_/rgyal ba'i dam chos chu yi char/_/'gro ba'i dge ba'i lo tog rgyu/_/rnam par rtog pa med par 'bebs/_/ji ltar 'jig rten dge ba'i lam 'jug na/_/rlung skyes chu char sprin
[\[69a.7\]]gyis 'bebs pa ltar/_/de bzhin brtse rlung 'gro dge mngon 'phel phyir/_/sangs rgyas sprin las dam chos char pa 'bebs/_/srid la mkhyen dang brtse chen 'gyur ba dang /_/mi 'gyur mi gos nam mkha'i dkyil gnas pa/_/ting 'dzin gzungs chu dri med snying
[\[69b\]]
[\[69b.1\]]po can/_/thub dbang sprin ni dge ba'i lo tog rgyu/_/ji ltar bsil dang zhim dang 'jam pa dang /_/yang ba'i chu ni sprin de las thon pa/_/sa la ba tsha la sogs gnas 'brel bas/_/shin tu mang po'i ror ni 'gyur ba bzhin/_/de bzhin 'phags pa'i yan lag brgyad
[\[69b.2\]]chu'i char/_/rab yangs brtse sprin snying po las thon pa/_/'gro ba'i rgyud kyi gnas kyi dbye ba las/_/rnam pa mang po'i ro dang ldan par 'gyur/_/theg pa mchog la dang ba dang /_/bar ma dang ni sdang ba yi/_/phung po gsum ni mi dag dang /_/rma bya dang ni yi dgas 'dra/_/
[\[69b.3\]]dpyid mthar sprin med pa ni mi dang mkha' mi rgyu ba'i bya dag dang /_/dbyar tshes la char babs pa na yi dgas dag ni sdug pa ltar/_/snying rje'i sprin tshogs dag gis chos chu byung dang ma byung ba las kyang /_/chos 'dod pa dang chos la sdang ba'i 'jig rten dag na dpe de nyid/_/
[\[69b.4\]]thigs pa rags 'bebs rdo tshan dang ni rdo rje'i me ni 'bebs pa na/_/srog chags phra dang ri sul song ba dag la ji ltar sprin ltos med/_/phra dang rgya chen rigs pa'i tshul gyis mkhyen pa dang ni brtse ba'i sprin/_/nyon mongs dag 'gyur bdag lta'i bag nyal dag la rnam
[\[69b.5\]]kun ltos pa med/_/'khor ba'i skye 'chi thog ma med der 'gro ba'i lam ni rnam pa lnga/_/mi gtsang ba la dri zhim med bzhin 'gro lnga dag na bde ba med/_/de yi sdug bsngal rtag tu mes mtshon rgya tsha la sogs reg skyes bzhin/_/thugs rje'i sprin las dam chos char chen
[\[69b.6\]]der bzhi byed rab tu 'bebs/_/lha la 'chi 'pho mi la yongs tshol sdug bsngal zhes byar rtogs pa'i phyir/_/shes rab ldan pa lha mi'i dbang phyug mchog la'ang mngon par 'dod med de/_/shes rab dang ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rab dad pa'i rjes 'brangs la/_/
[\[69b.7\]]'di ni sdug bsngal 'di rgyu 'di ni 'gog ces shes pas mthong phyir ro/_/nad ni shes bya nad kyi rgyu ni spang bya la/_/bde gnas thob bya sman ni bsten par bya ba ltar/_/sdug bsngal rgyu dang de 'gog pa dang de bzhin lam/_/shes bya spang bya reg par bya zhing bsten par bya/_/ji ltar tshangs
[\[70a\]]
[\[70a.1\]]pa tshangs pa yi/_/gnas nas 'phro ba med bzhin du/_/lha yi gnas ni thams cad du/_/snang ba 'bad med ston pa ltar/_/de bzhin thub pa chos sku las/_/bskyod pa med par khams kun du/_/skal ldan rnams la 'bad med par/_/
[\[70a.2\]]sprul pa dag ni ston par mdzad/_/ji ltar tshangs rtag gzhal yas khang na mi g.yo 'dod khams zhugs pa de/_/lha rnams kyis mthong de mthong de yang yul la dga' ba spong byed ltar/_/de bzhin bde gshegs chos kyi sku las mi bskyod 'jig rten khams kun du/_/
[\[70a.3\]]skal ldan gyis mthong de mthong de yang rtag tu dri ma kun sel byed/_/sngon gyi rang nyid smon lam dang /_/lha rnams kyi ni dge ba'i mthus/_/ji ltar tshangs pa 'bad med snang /_/rang byung sprul sku de bzhin no/_/'pho dang lhums 'jug bltams dang yab kyi khab gshegs
[\[70a.4\]]dang /_/dges rol pa dang dban par spyod dang bdud bcom dang /_/byang chub che brnyes zhi ba'i grong du lam ston dag_/bstan nas thub pa skal med mig gi lam mi 'gyur/_/ji ltar nyi mas gdungs pa'i dus gcig tshe nyid la/_/pad sogs rgyas dang ku mu ta ni rab zum pa/_/chu skyes bye dang
[\[70a.5\]]zum pa'i yon tan skyon dag la/_/nyi ma rtog med 'dir ni 'phags pa'i nyi de bzhin/_/ji ltar nyi ma rtog med par/_/rang 'od cig car spros pa yis/_/pad+ma rgyas par byed pa dang /_/gzhan dag smin par byed pa ltar/_/de bzhin de bzhin gshegs pa yi/_/nyi ma dam chos 'od zer dag_/_
[\[70a.6\]]gdul bya'i skye bo'i pad+ma la/_/rnam par rtog pa med par 'jug_/chos dang gzugs kyi sku dag gis/_/byang chub snying po mkhar shar ba'i/_/kun mkhyen nyi ma 'gro bar ni/_/ye shes 'od zer spro bar mdzad/_/gang phyir gdul bya dag pa yi/_/chu yi snod ni thams cad la/_/bde gshegs nyi
[\[70a.7\]]ma'i gzugs brnyan ni/_/dpag tu med pa cig car 'char/_/rtag tu thams cad la khyab pa'i/_/chos dbyings nam mkha'i dkyil du ni/_/sangs rgyas nyi ma gdug bya yi/_/ri la ji ltar 'os par 'bab/_/ji ltar rgya chen 'od zer stong ldan nyi shar 'di/_/'jig rten kun du snang bar byas nas
[\[70b\]]
[\[70b.1\]]rim gyis ni/_/mchog dang bar ma dman pa'i ri la 'bab de bzhin/_/rgyal ba'i nyi ma sems can tshogs la rim gyis 'bab/_/zhing kun nam mkha'i mthil spro nyi ma la med la/_/mi shes mun bkab shes bya'i don ston pa yang min/_/thugs rje'i bdag nyid sna tshogs mdog
[\[70b.2\]]bkye'i 'od tshogs kyis/_/gsal ba dag ni 'gro la shes bya'i don ston mdzad/_/sangs rgyas grong du gshegs tshe mig dang mi ldan pa yi skye bo rnams/_/mthong zhing don med tshogs bral don de mthong ba las ni myong ba dang /_/gti mug gis ldongs srid pa'i mtshor lhung lta ba'i
[\[70b.3\]]mun pas bsgribs pa rnams/_/sangs rgyas nyi ma'i 'od kyis blo snang ma mthong ba yi gnas mthong 'gyur/_/ji ltar yid bzhin nor bu ni/_/rtog pa med kyang cig car du/_/spyod yul gnas pa rnams kyi ni/_/bsam kun so sor rdzogs byed ltar/_/de bzhin sangs rgyas yid bzhin la/_/brten
[\[70b.4\]]nas bsam pa tha dad rnams/_/sna tshogs chos ni thos gyur kyang /_/de ni de la rnam mi rtog_/ji ltar nor bu rin chen rtog med 'dod pa'i nor/_/'bad pa med par gzhan pa dag la rab ster ltar/_/de bzhin thub pa 'bad med ji ltar 'os par ni/_/gzhan gyi don du srid pa ji srid rtag tu bzhugs/_/gang
[\[70b.5\]]phyir rgya mtsho sa 'og gnas de la 'dod pas/_/ji ltar nor bu bzang po 'gro 'dir rab rnyed dka'/_/de bzhin 'gro ba shin tu skal ngan nyon mongs zin/_/yid 'dir bde gshegs mthong ba rnyed dkar shes par bya/_/ji ltar sgra brnyan gyi ni sgra/_/gzhan gyi rnam rig las byung ba/_/rnam rtog med
[\[70b.6\]]cing bzo med la/_/phyi dang nang na mi gnas ltar/_/de bzhin de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung /_/gzhan gyi rnam rig las byung ba/_/rnam par rtog med bzo med cing /_/phyi dang nang na gnas ma yin/_/cung zad med cing snang ba med/_/dmigs pa med cing rten med la/_/mig gi lam las rab 'das pa/_/
[\[70b.7\]]gzugs med bstan du med pa yi/_/mkha' la ji ltar mtho dang dma'/_/mthong yang de ni de lta min/_/de bzhin thams cad sangs rgyas la/_/mthong yang de ni de lta min/_/ji ltar sa las skye ba kun/_/rtog med sa la brten nas ni/_/'phel dang brten dang yangs 'gyur ltar/_/de bzhin

[\[71a.1\]]rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas sa/_/rnam rtog med pa la brten nas/_/'gro ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams/_/ma lus par ni 'phel bar 'gyur/_/'bad rtsol med par bya ba 'ga'/_/byed pa mthong med de bas na/_/gdul bya'i the tshom bcad pa'i phyir/_/dpe rnams dgu ni bstan
[\[71a.2\]]pa yin/_/gang du dpe dgu po 'di dag_/rgyas par rab tu bstan gyur pa/_/mdo sde yi ni ming nyid kyis/_/de yi dgos pa bstan pa nyid/_/thos pa las byung shes pa yi/_/snang ba rgya chen 'dis brgyan pa'i/_/blo ldan myur du sangs rgyas kyi/_/spyod yul kun la 'jug par 'gyur/_/de don baiDUr

[\[71a.4\]]rtsol rgyun kun rab zhi ba/_/rnam par rtog pa med pa'i thugs/_/dri med baiDUr brgya byin gyi/_/gzugs brnyan shar ba la sogs bzhin/_/'bad rtsol zhi ba dam bcas te/_/rtog med thugs ni gtan tshigs so/_/rang bzhin don ni grub don du/_/dpe ni brgya byin gzugs
[\[71a.5\]]sogs yin/_/'dir ni skabs don 'di yin te/_/ston pa la sogs rnam dgu ni/_/ston pa skye 'chi dang bral ba/_/'bad pa med par rab 'jug pa'o/_/gang zhig brgya byin rnga dang sprin bzhin dang /_/tshangs nyid rin chen yid bzhin nor rgyal bzhin/_/sgra brnyan nam
[\[71a.6\]]mkha' sa bzhin srid pa'i bar/_/'bad med gzhan don mdzad de rnal 'byor rig_/rin chen lha dbang snang zhing ston pa ste/_/legs par 'doms mdzad lha yi rnga dang 'dra/_/khyab bdag mkhyen dang brtse chen sprin tshogs ni/_/mtha' yas 'gro ba srid rtse'i bar du khyab/_/tshangs
[\[71a.7\]]bzhin zag med gnas las mi bskyod par/_/sprul pa rnam pa du ma rab tu ston/_/nyi bzhin ye shes snang ba rab spro gang /_/rnam dag rin chen yid bzhin nor 'dra'i thugs/_/rgyal ba rnams kyi gsung de brag ca bzhin du yi ge med/_/sku ni nam mkha' lta bur khyab dang gzugs med

[\[71b.1\]]rtag pa nyid/_/sa gzhi 'gro ba'i dkar po'i chos kyi sman rnams ma lus pa'i/_/rnam pa kun tu gzhir gyur pa ni sangs rgyas sa yin no/_/dag pa be+e DUr+ya 'dra yi/_/sems la sangs rgyas mthong ba'i rgyu/_/de dag sa ni mi zlog pa'i/_/dad pa'i dbang po brtas pa

[\[72a\]]
[\[72a.1\]]sems can gyis kyang bsam bya min/_/'di ni 'dren pa rnams kyi spyod yul yin/_/blo ldan rgyal ba'i yum de la mos pa/_/sangs rgyas yon tan tshogs kyi snod 'gyur te/_/bsam med yon tan tshogs la mngon dga' bas/_/sems can kun gyi

[\[72a.3\]]ba de las bsod nams ches mang thob par 'gyur/_/blo ldan gang zhig bla med byang chub 'dod pas bskal pa du mar yang /_/lus ngag yid kyi 'bad pa med par tshul khrims dri med srung byed la/_/gzhan gang 'di las tshig tsam thos shing thos nas kyang ni mos na 'di/_/

[\[72b.1\]]sogs yon tan snod/_/byang chub sems ni de dag la/_/rtag tu nye bar gnas par 'gyur/_/de ni rtag tu nyer gnas pas/_/rgyal ba'i sras po phyir mi ldog_/bsod nams pha rol phyin rdzogs dang /_/yongs su dag pa nyid du 'gyur/_/bsod nams pha rol phyin pa lnga/_/de la rnam gsum rtog

[\[72b.5\]]tu bshad/_/gang zhig don ldan chos dang nyer 'brel zhing /_/khams gsum kun nas nyon mongs spong byed gsung /_/zhi ba'i phan yon ston par mdzad pa gang /_/de ni drang srong gsung yin bzlog pa gzhan/_/gang zhig rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'ba' zhig gi/_/dbang byas rnam g.yeng med yid can gyis bshad/_/

[\[73a.5\]]mtshan gang gi phyir/_/ji lta bur ni gang bshad dang /_/rgyu mthun pa ni gang yin te/_/tshigs su bcad pa bzhis bstan to/_/gnyis kyi bdag nyid dag pa yi/_/thabs dang gcig gis nyams pa'i rgyu/_/de nas tshigs su bcad pa ni/_/gnyis kyis 'bras bu bstan pa yin/_/'khor gyi dkyil

[\[84a.7\]]pa la skyabs su song ba/_nges par 'byung ba tshol [#]ba slob pa bya ba dang bcas pa dang /_bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la zhugs pa ma yin no/_/ji ltar 'jigs pa dang bcas she [#]na/_gang gi phyir dgra bcom pa yang srid pa spangs pa rnams kyang bag
[\[84b\]]
[\[84b.1\]]chags ma spangs pa'i phyir rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par 'du byed thams cad la mi bzad par 'jigs pa'i 'du shes nye bar gnas par 'gyur te/_dper na ral gri gdengs pa'i gshed ma'i skyes bu la bya ba bzhin te/_des na de dag kyang gtan du bde ba'i nges par
[\[84b.2\]]'byung ba thob pa ma yin no/_/skyabs ni skyabs tshol ba ma yin no/_/ji ltar sems can skyabs med pa 'jigs pa de dang des 'jigs pa dag de dang [#]de las nges par 'byung ba tshol ba [#]de bzhin du dgra bcom pa la yang [#]'jigs pa de yod do/_/gang gi phyir de dag
[\[84b.3\]]'jigs pas 'jigs te/_de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la skyabs su 'gro ba yin no/_/gang zhig de ltar 'jigs pa dang bcas pa'i phyir skyabs su 'gro ba de ni gdon mi za bar 'jigs pa las nges par 'byung ba tshol la/_nges par 'byung ba tshol ba'i phyir ni/_
[\[84b.4\]]'jigs pa'i gzhi spang [#]ba'i dbang du byas nas slob pa [#]bya ba dang bcas par 'gyur ro/_/slob pa'i phyir ni 'jigs [#]pa med pa khyu mchog gi gnas [#]thob par bya ba'i phyir zhugs par 'gyur ba yin te/_'di lta ste/_bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
[\[84b.5\]]la zhugs pa'o[#]/_/de'i phyir de yang de'i yan lag gi [#]skyabs yin pa'i phyir gtan gyi skyabs ma yin no/_/de ltar skyabs gnyis po 'di ni mthar thug pa'i dus na skyabs ma yin par brjod do/_/dam pa'i don du 'gro ba yi/_/skyabs ni sangs rgyas nyag gcig
[\[84b.6\]]nyid[#]/_/thub pa chos kyi sku can phyir/_/tshogs kyang de yi mthar thug phyir/_/'dis ni sngar bshad pa'i tshul gyis skye ba med pa dang /_'gag pa med pas rab tu phye ba'i thub pa rnam par byang ba'i bden pa gnyis kyi mtshan nyid 'dod chags dang bral ba'i chos
[\[84b.7\]]kyi sku can yin pa'i phyir dang /_theg pa gsum po'i tshogs kyang chos kyi sku rnam par dag pa mthar thug pa thob pas mthar phyin par 'gyur ba'i phyir na/_skyob pa med cing skyabs med pa'i [#]'jig rten na phyi ma'i mtha'i mu dang mnyam pa mi zad pa'i skyabs/_rtag_
[\[85a\]]
[\[85a.1\]]pa'i skyabs/_g.yung drung gi skyabs/_don dam pa'i skyabs ni gcig nyid de/_'di lta ste/_de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas so/_/rtag pa g.yung drung zhi ba brtan pa'i skyabs gcig pu 'di rgyas
[\[85a.2\]]par/_'phags pa dpal phreng gi mdo'i rjes su 'brangs nas rtogs par bya'o/_/'byung ba dkon phyir dri med phyir/_/mthu ldan phyir dang 'jig rten gyi/_/rgyan gyur [#]phyir dang mchog nyid phyir/_/'gyur ba med phyir dkon mchog nyid/_/mdor bsdu na chos mthun pa rnam
[\[85a.3\]]pa drug gis na sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun zhes bya ba'i dkon mchog gsum po 'di rin po che dang 'dra bar brjod de/_'di lta ste 'byung ba dkon par chos mthun pas na [#]bskal pa yongs su 'gyur ba mang por yang dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bskrun pa rnams de dang phrad [#]pa mi 'thob pa'i
[\[85a.4\]]phyir ro/_/dri ma med par chos mthun pas ni rnam pa thams cad du dri ma dang bral ba'i phyir ro/_/mthu dang ldan par chos mthun pas ni mngon par shes pa drug la sogs pa yon tan gyi mthu bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa'i phyir ro/_/'jig rten gyi rgyan du chos mthun pas
[\[85a.5\]]ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsam pa dge ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro/_/rin po che bsnyan ma [#]las ches mchog nyid du chos mthun pas ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i phyir ro/_/bstod [#]pa dang smad [#]pa la sogs pas rnam par mi 'gyur ba'i chos mthun pas ni 'dus ma byas kyi rang bzhin
[\[85a.6\]]yin pa'i phyir ro/_/dkon mchog gsum bstan pa'i rjes thogs la gang yong na 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam par dag pa skye ba'i gnas ni dkon mchog gsum skye bar 'gyur ba de'i dbang du byas nas [#]tshigs su bcad pa/_dri bcas de bzhin nyid dang dri
[\[85a.7\]]ma med/_/dri med sangs rgyas yon tan rgyal ba'i mdzod[#]/_/gang las dkon mchog dge ba gsum 'byung ba/_/don dam gzigs pa rnams kyi yul nyid do/_/'dis ci zhig gsal bar byas she na/_dkon mchog gsum po 'di yi [#]rigs/_/thams cad gzigs
[\[85b\]]
[\[85b.1\]]pa rnams kyi yul/_/de yang rnam bzhi go rims bzhin/_/rgyu bzhi yis ni bsam mi khyab/_/de la dri ma dang bcas pa'i de bzhin nyid ni nyon mongs pa'i sbubs las ma grol ba'i khams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po zhes brjod pa gang yin pa'o/_/dri ma med pa'i de
[\[85b.2\]]bzhin nyid ni de nyid [#]sangs rgyas kyi sar gnas yongs su gyur pa'i mtshan nyid de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku zhes brjod pa gang yin pa'o/_/dri ma med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yon tan ni gnas gyur pa'i [#]mtshan nyid de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku de nyid la yod pa 'jig rten
[\[85b.3\]]las 'das pa stobs bcu la sogs pa sangs rgyas kyi chos gang dag yin pa'o/_/rgyal ba'i mdzad pa ni stobs bcu la sogs pas [#]sangs rgyas kyi chos de nyid kyi so so rang gi bla na med pa'i phrin las te/_gang zhig med par ma gyur zhing chad pa med la rgyun ma [#]chad pas byang
[\[85b.4\]]chub sems dpa' lung bstan pa'i gtam rgyun mi 'chad [#]pa'o/_/gnas bzhi po 'di dag kyang go rims ji lta [#]bzhin du rgyu bzhis bsam gyis mi khyab pa nyid kyi phyir thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul yin no zhes brjod do/_/bzhi po gang dag gis shes [#]na/_/dag dang
[\[85b.5\]]nyon mongs dang ldan phyir/_/kun nas nyon mongs med dag phyir/_/rnam par dbye ba med chos phyir/_/lhun grub rnam par mi rtog phyir/_/de la dri ma dang bcas pa'i de bzhin nyid ni cig car dus gcig [#]tu rnam par dag pa yang [#]yin la/_kun nas nyon mongs pa yang [# ]
[\[85b.6\]]yin pa'i phyir/_gnas 'di bsam gyis mi khyab ste/_zab mo'i chos kyi tshul la mos pa rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi [#]yang spyod yul du ma gyur pa'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro/_/gang gi phyir lha mo chos 'di gnyis ni rtogs par dka' [#]ba ste/_sems rang bzhin gyis
[\[85b.7\]]rnam par dag pa rtogs par dka' [#]ba dang /_sems de nyid kyi nye bar nyon mongs pa rtogs par dka' [#]ba'o/_/lha mo chos 'di gnyis nyan par byed pa ni khyod dam yang na chos chen po dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams yin no/_/lha mo lhag ma nyan thos dang rang
[\[86a\]]
[\[86a.1\]]sangs rgyas kyis ni chos 'di gnyis de bzhin gshegs pa la dad pas rtogs par bya ba nyid do zhes gsungs pa yin no/_/de la dri ma med pa'i de bzhin nyid ni sngar dri mas kun nas nyon mongs par ma gyur pa phyis rnam par dag par gyur pa'i phyir gnas 'di
[\[86a.2\]]bsam gyis mi khyab po/_/gang gi [#]phyir sems ni rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba ste/_de ni de kho na bzhin shes so/_/des na skad cig ma gcig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so zhes
[\[86a.3\]]gsungs pa yin no/_/de la dri ma med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi [#]yon tan ni gcig tu kun nas nyon mongs pa so so'i skye bo'i sa la yang rnam pas [#]dbyer med pa'i chos nyid snga phyir khyad par med pa [#]yod pa'i phyir gnas 'di bsam gyis mi khyab ste/_gang gi phyir gang la de bzhin gshegs
[\[86a.4\]]pa'i ye shes mtha' dag rjes su ma zhugs pa'i sems can de ni sems can gyi ris na 'ga' yang med do/_/'on kyang 'du shes kyi 'dzin pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes mi mngon no/_/'du shes kyi 'dzin pa dang bral ba las ni/_thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes
[\[86a.5\]]rang byung gi ye shes thogs pa med par rab tu 'byung ngo /_/kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste/_dper na stong gsum gyi [#]stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshad dang mnyam pa'i dar yug chen po gcig yod par gyur [#]la/_dar yug chen po de la yang stong gsum gyi stong
[\[86a.6\]]chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rdzogs par bris par gyur te/_'di lta ste/_khor [#]yug chen po'i tshad du ni khor yug chen po bris/_sa chen po'i tshad du ni sa chen po/_stong gnyis pa'i 'jig rten gyi [#]khams kyi tshad du ni stong gnyis pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams/_stong gi
[\[86a.7\]]'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshad du ni stong gi 'jig rten gyi khams/_gling bzhi'i [#]'jig rten gyi [#]khams kyi tshad du ni gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams/_rgya mtsho chen po'i tshad du ni rgya mtsho chen po/_'dzam bu'i gling gi tshad du ni 'dzam bu'i gling /_shar gyi lus 'phags kyi gling gi tshad du ni shar gyi
[\[86b\]]
[\[86b.1\]]'phags kyi gling /_nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi gling gi tshad du ni nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi gling /_byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi gling gi tshad du ni byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi gling /_ri rab kyi tshad du ni ra rib/_sa la spyod pa'i lha'i gzhal yas khang gi tshad du ni sa la spyod pa'i lha'i gzhal yas
[\[86b.2\]]khang /_'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha'i gzhal yas khang gi tshad du ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha'i gzhal yas khang /_gzugs na spyod pa'i lha'i gzhal yas khang gi tshad du ni gzugs na spyod pa'i lha'i gzhal yas khang bris so/_/dar yug chen po de yang chu zheng stong gsum
[\[86b.3\]]gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshad tsam du gyur la/_dar yug chen po de yang rdul phra rab kyi rdul gcig tu bcug par gyur to/_/ji ltar rdul phra rab kyi rdul gcig tu dar yug chen po de bcug pa de bzhin du rdul phra rab kyi rdul ma lus pa rnams su de'i tshad kyi
[\[86b.4\]]dar yug chen po de nang du bcug [#]par gyur to/_/de nas mkhas pa mdzangs [#]pa gsal ba yid gzhungs pa der nye bar zhugs pa'i spyod pa dang ldan pa'i skyes bu 'ga' zhig skyes te/_de'i mig lha'i mig tu gyur cing kun tu yongs su dag pa [#]'od gsal bar gyur pa zhig la
[\[86b.5\]]des lha'i mig gis rnam par bltas te/_'di lta bur gyur pa'i dar yug chen po 'di rdul phra rab kyi rdul chung ngu 'di nyid la gnas te/_sems can 'ga' la yang nye bar mkho bar ma gyur to/_/de 'di snyam [#]du sems te/_kye ma gang bdag gi [#]brtson pa chen
[\[86b.6\]]po'i stobs dang mthus rdul phra rab kyi rdul 'di rdo rjes phye ste/_dar yug chen po [#]'di 'gro ba thams cad kyi nye bar 'tsho bar bya'o snyam pas/_des brtson pa chen po'i stobs kyi mthus bskyed de/_rdo rje phra mos rdul phra rab kyi rdul de phye nas bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du dar
[\[86b.7\]]yug chen po de 'gro ba mtha' dag la nye bar 'tsho [#]bar byed cing /_gcig la ji lta ba de [#]bzhin du rdul phra rab lus pa med pa mtha' dag las de kho na bzhin byed do/_/kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes tshad med pa'i ye shes sems can thams cad
[\[87a\]]
[\[87a.1\]]nye bar 'tsho ba'i ye shes kyang sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyud la ma [#]tshang ba med par rjes su zhugs te/_sems can gyi sems kyi rgyud de dag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes dang 'dra bar tshad med do/_/de lta mod kyi 'du shes kyi 'dzin pas
[\[87a.2\]]bcings pa'i byis pa rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes mi shes rab tu mi shes shing nyams su mi myong /_mngon du mi byed do/_/des na de bzhin gshegs pa chags pa med pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyis chos kyi dbyings sems can gyi gnas thams cad la rnam par
[\[87a.3\]]gzigs nas/_slob dpon gyi 'du shes su [#]gyur te/_kye ma ma la sems can 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin mi shes pa dang /_de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes rjes su zhugs pa dag ste/_gang yang ngas sems can 'di dag
[\[87a.4\]]la 'phags pa'i lam nye bar bstan pas 'du shes kyis byas pa'i 'ching ba thams cad bsal bar byas te/_ji ltar rang nyid 'phags pa'i ye shes kyi stobs bskyed pas ye shes kyi mdud pa chen po bsal nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes so sor mngon par shes shing /_de
[\[87a.5\]]bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes [#]dang mnyam pa nyid rjes su thob pa [#]bzhin du de dag la [#]de bzhin gshegs pa'i lam bstan pas 'du shes kyis byas pa'i 'ching ba thams cad zlog [#]par byed do/_/'du shes kyis byas pa'i 'ching ba thams cad log pa dag la ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i
[\[87a.6\]]ye shes tshad med pa de 'gro ba mtha' dag gi nye bar 'tsho bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so/_/de la rgyal ba'i mdzad pa ni cig car thams cad la dus thams cad du lhun gyis grub cing rnam par mi rtog [#]par bsam pa ji lta ba dang /_gdul bya ji lta ba bzhin du sems can
[\[87a.7\]]rnams la ma tshang ba med cing rjes su mthun par 'jug pa'i phyir gnas 'di bsam gyis mi khyab ste/_gang gi phyir sems can rnams gzhug pa'i don du de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes tshad med pa yin yang mdor bsdus pa tsam gyi sgo nas tshad dang ldan par bstan mod kyi/_rigs
[\[87b\]]
[\[87b.1\]]kyi bu 'on kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i yang dag pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i phrin las gang yin pa de ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa tshad med pa 'jig rten thams cad kyis shes par bya ba ma yin pa/_yi ge brjod du med pa/_gzhan gyis sgrub [#]par dka' ba/_sangs rgyas kyi zhing
[\[87b.2\]]thams cad du gnas pa/[# ]sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid rjes su thob pa/_'bad rtsol dang bya ba thams cad las 'das pa/_nam mkha' dang mnyam pa nyid kyis rnam par rtog pa med pa/_chos kyi dbyings kyi bya ba nyid kyi tha dad du dbyer med pa zhes bya ba nas/_
[\[87b.3\]]nor bu bai DUr+ya rnam par dag pa'i dper mdzad nas/_rgyas par bstan te/_rigs kyi bu rnam grangs 'dis 'di ltar rig par [#]bya ste/_de bzhin gshegs pa'i phrin las ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnyam pa nyid rjes su thob pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med pa dus gsum dang
[\[87b.4\]]rjes su 'brel pa/_dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung [#]mi 'chad par byed pa'o/_/bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i phrin las gang la rab tu zhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku nam mkha'i rang bzhin yang mi 'dor la/_sangs rgyas kyi [#]zhing thams cad
[\[87b.5\]]du yang kun tu ston [#]to/_/gsung brjod du med pa'i chos nyid kyang mi 'dor la/_sgra rnam par rig pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can rnams la chos kyang ston to/_/sems kyi dmigs pa thams cad dang yang bral la/_sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod
[\[87b.6\]]pa dang bsam pa yang rab tu shes so zhes gsungs so/_/rtogs bya rtogs pa de yi ni/_/yan lag rtogs par byed phyir te/_/go rims ji bzhin gnas gcig ste/_/dag rgyu gsum ni rkyen yin no/_/don gyi gnas bzhi po 'di dag las kyang shes bya thams cad bsdus pa'i phyir
[\[87b.7\]]dang po ni rtogs par bya ba'i gnas su blta [#]bar bya'o/_/de'i rjes su rtogs pa ni rtogs pa yin pa'i phyir gnyis pa byang chub kyi gnas so/_/byang chub kyi yan lag tu gyur pa ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan yin pa'i phyir gsum pa byang chub kyi yan lag gi [#]gnas so/_/byang
[\[88a\]]
[\[88a.1\]]chub kyi [#]yan lag rnams [#]nyid kyis gzhan dag rtogs par byed pa'i phyir bzhi pa rtogs par byed pa'i gnas so/_/de ltar gnas bzhi po 'di dbang du byas te rgyu dang rkyen gyi [#]dngos pos dkon mchog gsum gyi [#]rigs rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o/_/de
[\[88a.2\]]la gnas bzhi po 'di dag las dang po ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi sa bon yin pa'i phyir so so rang nyid tshul bzhin yid la byed pa'i gnas kyis de rnam par dag pa la brten nas dkon mchog gsum gyi rgyur rtogs par byed par bya ste/_de ltar gnas gcig ni rgyu yin no/_/ji ltar
[\[88a.3\]]gsum rkyen yin zhe na/_de bzhin gshegs pa bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzo gas par sangs rgyas nas stobs bcu la sogs pa sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i phrin las rnam pa sum cu rtsa gnyis mdzad pa na/_gzhan
[\[88a.4\]]gyi sgra la brten nas de rnam par dag pa la brten nas dkon mchog 'byung ba'i rkyen du rtogs par bya ste/_de ltar gsum po 'di ni rkyen yin no/_/'di phan chad gzhung lhag mas gnas bzhi po 'di dag nyid kyis mthar gyis rnam par dbye ba rgyas par ston par [#]rig par bya'o/_/de la dri ma
[\[88a.5\]]dang bcas pa'i de bzhin nyid kyi dbang du mdzad nas sems can thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po can no zhes gsungs pa gang yin pa de don gang gi [#]yin zhe na/_rdzogs sangs sku ni 'phro phyir dang /_/de bzhin nyid dbyer med phyir dang /_/rigs yod phyir na lus can
[\[88a.6\]]kun/_/rtag tu sangs rgyas snying po can/_/mdor bsdu na don rnam pa gsum gyis sems can thams cad ni rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po can no zhes bcom ldan 'das kyis [#]gsungs te/_sangs rgyas ye shes sems can tshogs zhugs phyir/_/rang bzhin dri med
[\[88a.7\]]de ni [#]gnyis med de/_/sangs rgyas rigs la de 'bras nyer brtags phyir/_/'gro kun sangs rgyas snying po can du gsungs/_/don de rnam pa thams cad don gang gis gsung [#]rab thams cad du khyad par med par bstan par 'gyur ba de'i dbang du byas te bshad par
[\[88b\]]
[\[88b.1\]]bya'o/_/'di lta ste/_sems can thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi skus 'phro ba'i don dang /_de bzhin gshegs pa'i de bzhin nyid rnam par dbyer med pa'i don dang /_de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yod pa'i don gyis so/_/don gyi gnas gsum po
[\[88b.2\]]'di dag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po'i mdo'i [#]rjes su 'brangs te 'og nas ston par 'gyur ro/_/sdom ni/_ngo bo rgyu 'bras las ldan 'jug pa dang /_/gnas skabs de bzhin kun tu 'gro ba'i don/_/rtag tu mi 'gyur yon tan dbyer med ni/_/don dam dbyings
[\[88b.3\]]kyi dgongs don yin zhes bya/_/mdor bsdu na don rnam pa [#]bcu la dgongs nas/_de kho na'i ye shes dam pa'i yul de bzhin gshegs pa'i khams rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o/_/don rnam pa bcu gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_ngo bo'i don dang /_rgyu'i don dang /_'bras
[\[88b.4\]]bu'i don dang /_las kyi don dang /_ldan pa'i don dang /_'jug pa'i don dang /_gnas skabs kyis [#]rab tu dbye ba'i don dang /_kun tu 'gro ba'i don dang /_mi 'gyur ba'i don dang /_dbyer med pa'i don to/_/de la ngo bo'i don dang rgyu'i don las brtsams nas tshigs su bcad pa/_rin chen
[\[88b.5\]]nam mkha' chu dag bzhin/_/rtag tu rang bzhin nyon mongs med/_/chos mos lhag pa'i shes rab dang /_/ting 'dzin snying rje las byung ba/_/de la tshigs su bcad pa phyed snga mas ci bstan zhe na/_mthu dang gzhan du mi 'gyur dang /_/brlan pa'i ngo bo rang bzhin phyir/_/
[\[88b.6\]]'di dag nor bu rin chen mkha'/_/chu yi yon tan chos mthun nyid/_/gsum po 'di dag ni 'dir sngar bstan zin pa ste/_gsum po 'di dag la go rims ji lta ba bzhin kho nar rang gi mtshan nyid dang spyi'i mtshan nyid las brtsams nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i khams yid
[\[88b.7\]]bzhin gyi [#]nor bu dang /_nam mkha' dang /_chu rnam par dag pa'i yon tan dang /_chos mthun pa nyid du rig par bya'o/_/de la re zhig de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku la [#]ni bsam pa'i don grub pa la sogs pa mthu'i ngo bo nyid rang gi mtshan nyid las bsams [#]nas yid
[\[89a\]]
[\[89a.1\]]bzhin gyi nor bu dang chos mthun pa nyid du rig par bya'o/_/de bzhin nyid la ni gzhan du ma yin pa nyid kyi rang gi ngo bo'i rang gi mtshan nyid las brtsams nas nam mkha' dang chos mthun pa nyid du rig par bya'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs la ni sems
[\[89a.2\]]can la snying brtse bas brlan pa'i rang gi ngo bo nyid kyi [#]mtshan nyid las brtsams nas chu dang chos mthun pa nyid du rig par bya'o/_/'dir thams cad kyang rtag tu rang bzhin gyis shin tu nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa [#]rang bzhin gyis yongs su dag pa'i spyi'i mtshan nyid las brtsams nas de
[\[89a.3\]]nyid yid bzhin gyi [#]nor bu dang /_nam mkha' dang chu rnam par dag pa'i yon tan dang /_chos mthun par rig par bya'o/_/de la tshigs su bcad pa phyed 'og mas ci bstan zhe na/_chos la khong khro bdag lta dang /_/'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs dang /_/sems
[\[89a.4\]]can don la ltos med pa[#]/_/'dod chen mu stegs [#]nyan thos dang /_/rang byung rnams kyi sgrib rnam bzhi/_/dag rgyu lhag par mos pa la[#]/_/sogs pa'i chos ni rnam bzhi nyid/_/mdor bsdu na sems can gyi [#]tshogs na sems can gyi rnam pa 'di gsum yod de/_srid pa
[\[89a.5\]]'dod pa dang /_srid pa dang bral bar 'dod pa dang /_de gnyis ka mngon par mi 'dod pa'o/_/de la srid pa 'dod pa ni rnam pa gnyis su rig par bya ste/_thar pa'i lam dang zhe 'gras pa yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i rigs can gyi [#]sems can 'khor ba nyid

[\[89b\]]
[\[89b.1\]]la zhugs pa'o/_/de la thabs ma yin pa la zhugs pa la yang rnam pa gsum ste/_'di las phyi rol du gyur pa tsa ra ka dang /_kun tu rgyu dang /_gcer bu pa [#]la sogs pa'i rnam pa du ma'i mu stegs pa mang po dang /_de dang mthun par spyod pa chos 'di pa nyid dad pa yod
[\[89b.2\]]kyang /_nges par gzung dka' ba'i lta ba 'dzin pa ste/_de dag kyang gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_don dam pa la mi [#]mos pa gang zag tu lta [#]ba ste/_gang la [#]bcom ldan 'das kyis stong pa nyid la mos pa med pa ni mu stegs pa dag [#]dang khyad par med pa yin no zhes gsungs pa dang /_

[\[90a\]]
[\[90a.1\]]gang dag srid pa dang bral bar 'dod kyang thabs ma yin pa la zhugs pa de dag ni/_ma nges pa'i sems can gyi phung po zhes bya'o/_/gang dag srid pa dang bral bar 'dod pa thabs la zhugs pa dang /_de gnyis ka mngon par mi 'dod pa mnyam pa nyid thob

[\[91b.1\]]'dzin pa la mngon par dga' ba las bzlog nas shes rab kyi [#]pha rol tu phyin pa bsgoms pa las ni 'bras bu bdag dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa 'thob par blta'o/_/'di ltar mu stegs pa gzhan thams cad ni gzugs la sogs pa de'i rang bzhin ma yin pa'i dngos po bdag tu khas len

[\[91b.3\]]ji ltar gzigs pa'i bdag med pa yang bdag [#]yod pa ma yin pa'i mtshan nyid kyis mi slu ba dang ldan pa'i phyir dus thams cad du bdag tu 'dod do/_/bdag med pa nyid bdag tu byas pa ste/_ji skad du/_mi gnas pa'i tshul gyis gnas pa zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/_/'khor ba'i

[\[91b.7\]]bu ni go rims ji lta ba bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku [#]gtsang ba dang /_bdag dang /_bde ba dang /_rtag pa'i yon tan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam pa bzhi 'grub bo/_/de bzhin gshegs pa ni 'di dag gis chos kyi dbyings kyi mthar thug pa nam mkha'i khams kyi mthas [# ]

[\[92a.1\]]klas pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug [#]pa zhes brjod do/_/'di ltar theg pa chen po'i chos dam pa la [#]lhag par mos pa bsgoms pas ni de bzhin gshegs pa shin tu gtsang ba'i chos kyi dbyings kyi [#]mthar thug pa [#]brnyes pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyi mthar thug pa nyid 'grub po/_/

[\[92a.3\]]phyir nam mkha'i khams kyi mthas klas pa'o/_/snying rje chen po bsgoms pas sems can thams cad la dus mu [#]mtha' med par snying rje dang ldan pa'i phyir na phyi ma'i mtha'i [#]mur thug pa yin no/_/zag pa med pa'i [#]dbyings la gnas pa'i dgra bcom pa dang /_rang sangs rgyas rnams dang /_

[\[92a.5\]]mtshan nyid do/_/de la rkyen gyi [#]mtshan nyid ni/_ma rig pa'i bag chags kyis te/_'du byed rnams kyis ma rig pa bzhin no/_/rgyu'i mtshan nyid ni ma rig pa'i bag chags kyi sa'i rkyen can zag pa med pa'i las nyid de/_'du byed bzhin no/_/'byung ba'i mtshan nyid ni ma rig pa'i bag

[\[92b\]]
[\[92b.1\]]cad kyi rten du gyur pa ma rig [#]pa'i bag chags kyis ma spangs pas na [#]nyon mongs pa'i dri ma dri nga ba'i bag chags thams cad dang ldan pa'i phyir gtsang [#]ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa rab kyi mthar phyin pa mi 'thob po/_/ma rig pa'i bag chags kyis de nyid la brten nas mtshan ma'i spros pa kun du spyod pa phra mo

[\[93a.1\]]rgyas par 'byung ngo /_/gang gi phyir dgra bcom pa dang /_rang sangs rgyas dang /_dbang thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yid kyi rang bzhin gyi lus 'di gsum la gtsang ba dang /_bdag dang /_bde ba dang /_rtag pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa med pa de'i [#]phyir/_de

[\[93b\]]
[\[93b.1\]]pa rtag pa zhes bgyi bar lta na[#]/_de ni de'i rtag pa'i lta bar 'gyur te/_de ni de'i yang dag pa ma lags pa'i lta bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs pa bzhin no/_/chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul gyi sgo 'dis ni don dam par 'khor ba nyid mya ngan las 'das par brjod pa yin te/_gnyis
[\[93b.2\]]ka ltar rnam par mi rtog pa mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa mngon du byed pa'i phyir ro/_/de lta mod kyi rgyu gnyis kyis [#]khyad par med par [#]sems can thams cad la nye ba dang ring ba [#]'brel pas mi gnas pa'i gnas thob pa tsam bstan pa yin no/_/rgyu gnyis po gang dag
[\[93b.3\]]gis she na/_'di la byang chub sems dpa' ni khyad par med par sems can thams cad la nye ba [#]ma yin te/_shes rab kyis sred pa'i bag la nyal mtha' dag spangs pa'i phyir ro/_/ring ba yang yod pa ma yin te/_snying rje chen pos de dag yongs su ma btang

[\[107b.1\]]ltar/_/de bzhin thub pas mi gtsang dang 'dra ba'i/_/nyon mongs su bying sems can yon tan ni/_/gzigs nas nyon mongs 'dam de dag bya'i phyir/_/skye dgu rnams la dam chos chu char 'bebs/_/ji ltar ljan ljin rul pa'i nang du lhung ba'i gser ni lha yis mthong gyur nas/_/kun

[\[112a\]]
[\[112a.1\]]so zhes bstan cing [#]rab tu gzhag pa gang yin pa'o/_/khams zhes bya ba ni/_ji skad du/_bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po [#]gang lags pa 'di ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi snying po rang bzhin gyis yongs su dag pa'i chos kyi snying po'o zhes
[\[112a.2\]]gsungs so/_/chos rnams kun gyi gnas yin te/_/zhes bya ba ni/_ji skad du/_bcom ldan 'das de'i slad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po ni 'brel pa/_rnam par dbye ba med pa/_bral mi shes pa/_'dus ma byas pa'i chos rnams kyi gnas dang [#]gzhi dang rten lags la/_
[\[112a.3\]]bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po ni ma 'brel [#]ba rnam par dbye ba dang bcas pa'i chos/_bral shes pa/_'dus byas kyi chos rnams kyi yang gzhi dang /_gnas dang /_rten lags so zhes gsungs pa'o/_/de yod na ni 'gro kun dang /_/zhes bya ba ni/_ji skad du/_bcom
[\[112a.4\]]ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po mchis na de la 'khor ba zhes tshig gis btags pa lags so zhes gsungs so/_/mya ngan 'das pa'ang thob par 'gyur/_/zhes bya ba ni/_ji skad du/_bcom ldan 'das gal te de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po ma mchis na sdug bsngal la
[\[112a.5\]]yang yid 'byung bar mi 'gyur zhing [#]mya ngan las 'das pa la yang 'dod pa dang /_don du gnyer ba dang /_smon par yang mi 'gyur ro zhes rgyas par gsungs so/_/chos kyi sku ltar rgya che ba de bzhin gshegs pa dang dbyer med pa'i mtshan nyid nges pa'i rigs kyi rang bzhin de bzhin gshegs
[\[112a.6\]]pa'i snying po de yang thams cad kyi tshe thams cad la khyad par med pa'i tshul du yod do zhes bya ba'i bar ni/_chos nyid tshad mar byas nas blta bar bya ste/_ji skad du/_rigs kyi bu 'di ni chos rnams kyi chos kyi chos nyid de[#]/_de bzhin gshegs pa rnams byung yang rung ma byung yang rung ste/_

[\[112b.1\]]pa dang /_sems yang dag par shes pa la ni/_chos nyid kyi rtogs [#]pa dang /_chos nyid kyi rigs [#]pa yin no de ni bsam par mi bya/_rnam par brtag par mi bya'i[#]/_lhag par [#]mos par bya ba 'ba' zhig tu zad do/_/rang byung rnams kyi [#]don dam de[#]/_/dad pa nyid kyis rtogs bya yin/_/nyi ma'i
