[\[112b.3\]]rgyas dang /_theg pa la gsar du zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ste/_ji skad du/_bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po 'di ni 'jig [#]tshogs la lta bar lhung ba rnams dang /_phyin ci log la mngon par 'dod pa [#]rnams dang /_stong pa nyid las [#]sems rnam par
[\[112b.4\]]g.yengs pa rnams kyi spyod yul ma lags so zhes gsungs pa bzhin no/_/de la 'jig tshogs la lta bar lhung ba ni byis pa so so'i skye bo la brjod de/_'di ltar de dag ni gtan du phung po la sogs pa'i chos zag pa dang bcas pa rnams la bdag dang bdag gi ba nyid du khas blangs
[\[112b.5\]]nas ngar 'dzin pa dang /_nga yir 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pas na 'jig [#]tshogs 'gags pa zag pa med pa'i dbyings la lhag par mos par mi nus pa dag ste/_de dag gis thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po rtogs par ltag la 'gyur te 'di ni
[\[112b.6\]]gnas med do/_/de la phyin ci log la mngon par dga' ba ni/_nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas [(]dgal [,]dag la [)]brjod do/_/de ci'i phyir zhe na/_'di lta ste/_de dag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po rtag pa nyid du bsgom par bya ba las/_slar [#]de rtag pa'i 'du shes su sgom [#]pa las

[\[113a.1\]]dang /_de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po bdag tu bsgom par bya ba las/_slar de la bdag gi 'du shes su sgom [#]pa las bzlog nas/_bdag med pa'i 'du shes su sgom [#]pa la dga' ba nyid dang /_de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po gtsang bar bsgom par

[\[113a.3\]]ba dang /_bdag dang /_sdug pa'i mtshan nyid kyi khams de ni nyan thos dang /_rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang spyod yul ma yin no zhes bshad pa yin no/_/de ltar phyin ci log la mngon par dga' ba[#]/_mi rtag pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_bdag med pa dang /_mi sdug pa'i
[\[113a.4\]]'du shes can rnams kyi spyod yul ma yin pa de ltar rgyas par yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i mdor/_bcom ldan 'das kyis rdzing gi chu'i nor bu'i dpe rab tu bsgrubs te/_'di lta ste/_dge slong dag dper na so ga'i dus la bab pa na/_skye bo dag khrus ras bcings te/_

[\[113a.6\]]dag la nor bu'o snyam nas bzung ste/_bdag gis nor bu rnyed do snyam ste [#]phyung ngo /_/phyung nas rdzing bu'i 'gram du bltas pa na 'di ni nor bu ma yin no snyam pa'i 'du shes rab tu 'jug go/_/rdzing gi chu de yang nor bu'i mthus nor bu'i 'od dang 'dra bar snang ngo /_/de dag de ltar snang ba'i
[\[113a.7\]]chu de yang e ma'o nor bu'o snyam du yon tan gyi [#]'du shes rab tu zhugs so/_/de nas de la thabs mkhas shing yid gzhungs pa cig [#]gis nor bu de de kho na bzhin du rnyed par gyur to/_/dge slong dag de bzhin du nor bu ltar chos kyi don de kho na mi shes pa khyed kyis thams cad

[\[113b.1\]]mi rtag pa dang /_thams cad sdug bsngal ba dang /_thams cad bdag med pa dang /_thams cad mi sdug pa'o zhes 'dzin pa thams cad kyis sgom zhing /_sgom [#]pa lan mang du byas shing mang du byas pas [#]nye bar gzhag pa de thams cad ni don med do/_/dge slong dag de'i phyir rdzing [#]de

[\[113b.4\]]bstan pa ni mdo ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs par bya'o/_/de la stong pa nyid las sems rnam par g.yengs pa ni theg pa la gsar du zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' stong pa nyid kyi tshul du de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po las nyams pa dag la brjod do/_/gang dag yod pa'i chos nyid dus
[\[113b.5\]]phyis rgyun 'chad cing zhig pa yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'o zhes dngos po gzhig pa'i phyir stong pa nyid kyi rnam par thar pa'i sgo 'dod pa'am/_yang gang dag gang zhig rtogs [#]par bya ba dang /_bsgom [#]par bya ba stong pa nyid ces bya ba gzugs la sogs pa las tha dad pa'i dngos

[\[114a.1\]]pa'i khams 'di las bsal bar bya ba kun nas nyon mongs pa'i rgyu mtshan ni 'ga' yang med la/_glo bur ba'i dri ma dang bral ba ni 'di'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro/_/'di la rnam par byang ba'i rgyu mtshan can gzhag par bya ba yang cung zad kyang yod pa ma yin

[\[114a.3\]]bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos gang gA'i klung gi bye ma las 'das pa ni mi stong ngo zhes gsungs so/_/de ltar na gang zhig gang na med pa de ni des stong ngo zhes yang dag par rjes su mthong la/_gang zhig lhag par gyur pa de ni de la rtag par yod do zhes yang dag pa ji lta ba
[\[114a.4\]]bzhin du shes so/_/tshigs su bcad pa 'di gnyis kyis ni sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' dang bral ba'i phyir/_phyin ci ma log pa stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid bstan to/_/de la gang zhig stong pa nyid kyi tshul 'di las sems [#]phyi rol tu rnam par g.yeng zhing rnam par 'phro [#]la
[\[114a.5\]]mnyam par mi 'jog cing rtse gcig tu mi 'gyur ba des na de dag stong pa nyid las sems rnam par g.yengs pa zhes brjod do/_/de la don dam pa stong pa nyid kyi ye shes med par ni rnam par rtog pa med pa'i dag pa'i [#]dbyings rtogs shing mngon par 'du bya bar mi nus so/_'di la dgongs
[\[114a.6\]]nas gsungs pa ni/_de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po'i ye shes nyid ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid kyi ye shes yin la/_de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po de [#]yang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis [#]sngar ma mthong ma rtogs pa'o zhes rgyas par gsungs
[\[114a.7\]]so/_/de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po [#]ji ltar chos kyi sku'i snying po [#]yin pa de ltar ni/_'jig tshogs la lta bar lhung ba rnams kyi spyod yul ma yin par brjod do/_/chos kyi dbyings ni lta ba'i gnyen po yin pa'i phyir ro/_/ji ltar chos kyi sku 'jig rten las 'das pa'i snying
[\[114b\]]
[\[114b.1\]]po yin pa de ltar ni phyin ci log la mngon par dga' ba rnams kyi spyod yul ma yin no zhes brjod do/_/'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi sku ni mi rtag pa la sogs pa 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi gnyen por bstan pa'i phyir ro/_/ji ltar chos kyi sku yongs su dag pa'i chos kyi snying po yin pa de ltar

[\[116b.2\]]su bcad pa gnyis po 'di'i don ni mdor bsdu na/_tshigs su bcad pa brgyad kyis rig par bya ste/_/chu mtsho sogs bzhin 'dod chags sogs/_/glo bur nyon mongs dag pa ni/_/mdor na mi rtog ye shes kyi[#]/_/'bras bu yin par rab tu brjod/_/rnam pa [#]kun gyi mchog ldan pa'i[#]/_
[\[116b.3\]]sangs rgyas sku ni nges thob pa/_/de ni rjes las [#]thob pa yi/_/ye shes [#]'bras bu yin par bstan/_/'dod chags rdul ni spang phyir dang /_/gdul [#]bar bya ba'i pad+ma la/_/bsam gtan chu ni 'bab phyir de/_/chu dang rdzing dang mtshungs pa yin/_/zhe sdang sgra gcan las grol bas/_/snying rje
[\[116b.4\]]byams chen 'od zer gyis/_/'gro ba khyab pa'i phyir na de/_/dri med zla ba nya ba bzhin/_/gti mug sprin las rnam grol bas/_/'gro ba ye shes 'od zer gyis/_/mun pa sel phyir sangs rgyas nyid/_/de ni dri med nyi ma bzhin/_/mi mnyam mnyam pa'i chos nyid phyir/_/dam chos ro ni
[\[116b.5\]]sbyin mdzad dang /_/shun pa dang ni bral phyir te[#]/_/bde gshegs sbrang rtsi'i snying po bzhin/_/dag phyir yon tan rdzas kyis ni/_/dbul ba [#]sel bar byed phyir dang /_/rnam grol 'bras bu smin byed phyir/_/gser dang gter dang ljon pa bzhin/_/rin chen chos kyi sku phyir dang /_/rkang gnyis

[\[121a.1\]]dang /_/thal gong bar med rgyas pa dang /_/dpung pa [#]legs zlum phyag 'jam ring /_/zlum zhing mthon dman med pa dang /_/phyag ring yongs su dag pa yi[#]/_/'od kyi dkyil 'khor dag dang ldan/_/mgrin pa dri med dung 'dra dang /_/'gram pa ri
[\[121a.2\]]dgas rgyal po 'dra/_/tshems ni bzhi bcu mnyam pa dang /_/rab dang sa tshems thags bzang ba dang /_/rnam [#]dag tshems mnyam nyid dang ni/_/mche ba rab mchog dkar ba nyid/_/ljags ring mtha' med bsam med pa/_/ro bro ba yi mchog nyid dang /_/rang byung ka la ping ga yi/_/
[\[121a.3\]]sgra dang tshangs pa'i dbyangs nyid dang /_/spyan bzangs [#]ut+pal khyu mchog rdzi 'dra dang /_/zhal mdzes dri med mdzod spu dkar bar ldan/_/gtsug tor dbu ldan dag cing srab pa dang /_/pags pa gser gyi [#]mdog 'dra sems can mchog/_/ba spu legs phra 'jam zhing re re nas/_/
[\[121a.4\]]sku yi gyen [#]du g.yas phyogs 'khyil ba dang /_/dbu skra dri med rin chen mthon mthing bzhin/_/n+ya gro rdzogs pa'i ljon shing dkyil 'khor 'dra/_/kun tu bzang po dpe med drang srong che/_/sred med bu yi stobs mnga' [#]mkhregs pa'i sku/_/bsam mi khyab par sum cu rtsa gnyis po/_/
[\[121a.5\]]'di dag ston pas mi dbang mtshan du gsungs/_/chu zla bzhin [#]zhes bya ba ni/_/ji ltar sprin med nam mkha'i zla ba'i gzugs/_/ston ka'i chu sngon mtshor [#]ni mthong ba ltar/_/de bzhin rgyal sras tshogs kyi [#]khyab bdag gzugs/_/rdzogs sangs [#]dkyil 'khor nang du mthong
[\[121a.6\]]bar 'gyur/_/de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang /_mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang /_sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang /_skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis po de dag rnam pa gcig tu mngon par bsdus te drug cu rtsa bzhir 'gyur ro/_/yon tan
[\[121a.7\]]drug cu rtsa bzhi po/_/'di dag so sor [#]rgyur bcas te/_/go rims ji bzhin rin chen gyi/_/mdo yi [#]rjes 'brangs shes par bya/_/ji skad bstan pa nyid kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan drug cu rtsa bzhi po 'di dag gi [#]rnam par dbye ba go rims 'di nyid kyis bstan pa ni/_bu mo rin po che'i

[\[121b.1\]]mdo'i rjes su 'brangs te shes par bya'o/_/gnas 'di dag la go rims bzhin du rdo rje dang /_/seng ge dang /_nam mkha' dang /_chu zla'i dpe brjod pa gang yin pa de'i bsdus pa'i don [#]tshigs su bcad pa bcus rig [#]par bya ste/_mi phyed pa dang mi zhan dang /_/mtshungs pa med dang g.yo
[\[121b.2\]]med phyir/_/rdo rje seng ge mkha' dag dang /_/chu yi zla ba'i dpes bstan to/_/stobs sogs rnams las stobs drug dang /_/gsum dang gcig gis rim pa bzhin/_/shes bya snyoms par 'jug pa dang /_/bag [#]chags bcas pa kun bsal [#]bas/_/go cha rtsig pa shing bzhin du/_/
[\[121b.3\]]phug dang bshig dang bcad phyir ro/_/gling dang snying brtan mi phyed pas/_/drang srong stobs ni rdo rje 'dra/_/gang phyir brling ba snying po'i phyir/_/gang phyir snying po bstan [#]pa'i phyir/_/gang phyir brtan pa mi phyed phyir/_/mi phyed phyir na rdo rje bzhin/_/'jigs med phyir dang ltos med phyir/_/
[\[121b.4\]]brtan phyir rtsal ni phun tshogs pas/_/thub pa seng ge seng ge bzhin/_/'khor gyi tshogs su 'jigs mi mnga'/_/kun mngon mkhyen pas gang las kyang /_/'jigs med par ni rnam par gnas/_/dag pa'i sems can dang yang [#]bdag/_/mi mnyam gzigs phyir ltos pa med/_/

[\[122a.1\]]gnyis/_/theg pa chen po [#]rgyud bla ma'i bstan bcos dkon mchog gi rigs rnam par dbye ba las/_yon tan gyi skabs te le'u gsum pa'o/_/[#]dri ma med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yon tan bshad zin to//_//da ni de'i las rgyal ba'i mdzad pa brjod par bya'o/_/de

[\[122a.3\]]gdul bya'i bya ba dang /_/de yi yul dang dus su gshegs pa la[#]/_/khyab bdag rtag tu lhun gyis grub par 'jug/_/yon tan rin chen mchog tshogs dang ldan ye shes chu mtsho bsod nams ye shes nyi 'od can/_/theg pa ma lus nges par bsgrubs te mtha' dang dbus med rgya chen nam mkha' ltar

[\[122a.5\]]dang brgyad kyis rig [#]par bya ste/_gang zhig [#]gang gis 'dul ba yi/_/bya gang gang du gang gi tshe/_/de ni rnam rtog skye med phyir/_/thub pa rtag tu lhun gyis grub/_/gdul bya'i khams ni gang zhig gi/_/gdul ba'i [#]thabs mang gang dag gis[#]/_/gdul bya'i bya gang gang du ni/_/gang tshe yul dang
[\[122a.6\]]dus de dag_/nges 'byin de yi rton pa dang /_/de'i 'bras de yi yongs 'dzin dang /_/de sgrib de gcod rkyen la ni/_/rnam par rtog pa med phyir ro/_/nges par 'byin pa sa bcu ste/_/tshogs gnyis dag ni de yi rgyu/_/de 'bras byang chub mchog yin te/_/byang chub sems can yongs su
[\[122a.7\]]'dzin/_/de sgrib mtha' yas nyon mongs dang /_/nye ba'i nyon mongs bag chags so/_/dus kun tu ni de 'joms pa'i/_/rkyen ni thugs rje chen po yin/_/gnas drug 'di rnams go rims bzhin/_/rgya mtsho nyi ma nam mkha'i [#]gter/_/sprin dang rlung bzhin shes par bya/_/shas chu yon tan
[\[122b\]]
[\[122b.1\]]rin chen dang /_/ldan phyir sa rnams rgya mtsho bzhin/_/sems can thams cad nyer 'tsho'i phyir/_/tshogs gnyis dag ni nyi ma bzhin/_/rgya che mtha' dang dbus med phyir/_/byang chub nam mkha'i khams bzhin no/_/yang dag rdzogs sangs chos nyid phyir/_/sems can khams ni gter dang 'dra/_/glo
[\[122b.2\]]bur khyab dang ma grub phyir/_/de yi nyon mongs sprin tshogs bzhin/_/de gtor ba yi nyer gnas phyir/_/thugs rje mi bzad rlung dang 'dra/_/gzhan gyi dbang gis nges 'byung dang /_/bdag dang sems can mtshungs gzigs dang /_/mdzad pa yongs su ma rdzogs phyir/_/'khor ba [#]srid du mdzad [#]mi 'chad/_/
[\[122b.3\]]skye ba dang 'gag pa med pas rab tu phye ba zhes brjod pa'i sangs rgyas nyid gang yin pa de/_'dir ni ji ltar na 'dus ma byas pas 'jug pa med pa'i mtshan nyid sangs rgyas nyid las lhun gyis grub cing rgyun mi 'chad par 'jig rten ji srid du/_rnam par [#]rtog pa med par sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa
[\[122b.4\]]rgyun du 'jug ces sangs rgyas kyi che ba'i bdag nyid chos nyid las brtsams te/_the tshom dang som nyi med [#]pa rnams sangs rgyas kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mos pa bskyed pa'i phyir/_dpe'i che ba'i bdag nyid [#]las tshigs su bcad pa/_brgya byin rnga sprin tshangs pa dang /_/nyi ma nor bu rin chen

[\[123a\]]
[\[123a.1\]]dag blangs te gnas par 'gyur/_/de dag dge ba'i las nges na/_/'di snang tsam zhes de lta bur/_/shes pa med kyang sa steng na[#]/_/'phos te lhar ni skye bar 'gyur/_/snang ba de ni shin tu yang /_/rtogs [#]pa med cing g.yo ba med/_/de lta mod kyi sa stengs [#]na/_/

[\[123a.3\]]tshogs mdzes pa can/_/zhi ba'i chos ni gsung ba [#]dang /_/mi gsung [#]mnyam par gzhag gyur pa/_/cho 'phrul rnam pa sna tshogs dag_/mdzad pa gzi mdangs chen po can/_/sems can rnams kyis mthong bar 'gyur/_/de mthong nas kyang 'dod ldan pa/_/sangs rgyas nyid phyir rab
[\[123a.4\]]sbyor te/_/de rgyu yang dag blangs nas ni/_/'dod pa'i go 'phang thob par byed/_/snang ba de ni shin tu yang /_/rtog med g.yo ba med pa nyid/_/de lta na yang 'jig rten na/_/don chen pos ni nye bar gnas/_/'di ni rang sems snang ba zhes/_/so so'i [#]skye bos mi shes mod[#]/_/de lta na
[\[123a.5\]]yang gzugs mthong ste/_/de dag la ni don yod 'gyur/_/rim gyis [#]de mthong la brten nas/_/theg pa 'di la gnas pa rnams/_/nang gi dam pa'i chos sku ni/_/ye shes mig gis mthong bar 'gyur/_/ji ltar sa kun dman [#]pa'i gnas gzhan dang bral dri [#]med bai DUr+ya/_/gsal mdzes
[\[123a.6\]]nor bu'i yon tan dri bral dpal ldan steng ni mnyam gyur te/_/dag phyir der [#]ni lha dag gnas [#]tshogs lha dbang lha yi gzugs shar te/_/rim gyis sa yi yon tan bral phyir de ni slar yang mi snang 'gyur/_/de dngos thob phyir bsnyen gnas brtul zhugs nges par sbyin sogs la phyogs pa/_/
[\[123a.7\]]bud med skyes tshogs smon pa'i sems kyis me tog la sogs 'thor [#]ba ltar/_/dag pa'i bai DUr+ya 'dra [#]sems la snang ba'i thub dbang thob bya'i phyir/_/rab dga'i [#]sems ldan rgyal ba'i sras rnams de bzhin sems [#]rab skyed par byed/_/ji ltar bai DU ra sa gzhi [#]gtsang ma la/_/lha

[\[123b.1\]]dbang lus kyi gzugs brnyan snang ba ltar/_/de bzhin 'gro sems sa gzhi gtsang ma la/_/thub pa'i dbang po'i sku yi gzugs brnyan 'char/_/'gro bar gzugs brnyan 'char nub rnyog med dang /_/rnyog pa'i rang sems rab 'jug dbang gis 'jug_/ji ltar 'jig rten dag na
[\[123b.2\]]gzugs snang ltar/_/de bzhin yod dang zhig ces de mi lta/_/lha'i rnga bzhin zhes bya ba ni/_ji ltar lha nang lha rnams kyi/_/sngon gyi [#]dkar po'i mthu yis ni/_/'bad dang gnas dang yid gzugs dang /_/rnam par rtog pa med bzhin du/_/mi rtag sdug bsngal bdag med dang /_/
[\[123b.3\]]zhi ba'i sgra yis bag med pa'i/_/lha rnams thams cad yang nas yang /_/chos kyi rngas ni skul byed ltar/_/de bzhin khyab bdag 'bad sogs dang /_/bral dang 'gro ba ma lus pa/_/sangs rgyas gsung gis khyab mdzad de/_/skal ldan rnams la chos ston to/_/ji ltar lha nang [#]lha rnams

[\[123b.5\]]rnga sgra'i rgyun 'byung mi 'jigs sbyin pa ni/_/nyon mongs g.yul du 'jug tshe lha min g.yul rgyal rtsed mo sel ba bzhin/_/de bzhin 'jig rten dag na bsam gtan gzugs med la sogs rgyus byung ba/_/sems can nyon mongs sdug bsngal rab 'joms zhi ba bla med lam tshul brjod/_/
[\[123b.6\]]ci'i phyir 'dir chos kyi rnga nyid kyi dbang du byas kyi/_lha'i sil snyan gyi rnam pa de las gzhan pa dag kyang ma yin te/_de dag lha rnams kyi sngon byas pa'i las kyi dbang gis mod kho nar lha'i rna bar yid 'phrog pa'i sgra'i rjes su 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhe na/_de bzhin gshegs pa'i [#]dbyangs
[\[123b.7\]]dang de dag chos mi mthun pa'i yon tan rnam pa bzhi'o/_/de dag kyang gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_nyi tshe ba nyid dang /_phan pa ma yin pa nyid dang /_bde ba [#]ma yin pa nyid dang /_nges par 'byin par byed pa ma yin pa nyid do/_/chos kyi rnga ni bag med pa'i lha'i [#]tshogs mtha'

[\[124a.1\]]dag bskul ba nyid dang /_de'i dus la mi 'da' bas na nyi tshe ba ma yin pa nyid du bstan to/_/lha ma yin la sogs pa pha rol gyi tshogs nye bar 'tshe ba'i 'jigs pa las yongs su skyob pa nyid dang /_bag yod pa'i gnas la rab tu sbyor bas na phan pa nyid dang /_
[\[124a.2\]]dam pa ma yin pa'i 'dod pa'i dga' ba de rnam par 'byed pa nyid dang /_chos kyi kun dga'i dga' bde nye bar sgrub [#]pas na bde ba nyid do/_/mi rtag pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_stong pa dang /_bdag med pa'i sgra sgrogs pa nyid dang /_nye bar 'tshe ba'i phongs [#]pa thams cad nye bar zhi bar
[\[124a.3\]]byed pas na nges par 'byin par byed pa nyid du bstan to/_/mdor bsdu na rnam pa bzhi po 'di dag gis chos kyi rnga dang chos mthun pas na/_sangs rgyas kyi dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor khyad par du 'phags so/_/des na sangs rgyas kyi [#]dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor las brtsams te tshigs su bcad pa/_

[\[124a.5\]]lhar ni rnga yi sgra chen po/_/sar gnas rnams kyi rnar mi 'gro/_/sangs rgyas rnga sgra 'khor ba yi/_/sa 'og 'jig rten dag tu 'gro/_/lhar ni lha yi sil snyan bye ba mang /_/'dod me mngon par 'phel ba'i don du sgrogs/_/thugs rje'i bdag nyid rnams kyi [#]dbyangs gcig kyang /_/sdug bsngal
[\[124a.6\]]mi rab zhi ba'i don du 'jug_/lhar ni mdzes shing yid 'ong sil snyan sgra/_/sems kyi rgod pa 'phel bar gyur pa'i rgyu/_/thugs rje'i bdag nyid de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung [#]/_/ting 'dzin sems gtong bsam pa skul byed nyid/_/mdor na ma lus 'jig rten khams rnams
[\[124a.7\]]su'ang /_/lha dang sa yi [#]bde ba'i rgyu gang yin/_/de ni ma lus 'jig rten khyab snang ba/_/dbyangs nyid la ni rab tu brten par brjod/_/lus kyi cho 'phrul gyis phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi [#]khams ma lus par khyab pas ni/_rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul zhes bstan to/_/sems kyi
[\[124b\]]
[\[124b.1\]]rnam grangs mkhyen pas de rtogs pa sems can gyi sems kyi spyod pa zab mo [#]snang ba ni kun brjod pa'i cho 'phrul lo/_/ngag gi dbyangs brjod pas nges par 'byin pa'i lam [#]las brtsams te 'doms pa dang rjes su bstan pa ni/_rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul lo/_/de ltar thogs pa med
[\[124b.2\]]par 'gro ba'i sangs rgyas kyi dbyangs [#]kyi dkyil 'khor nam mkha'i khams ltar yongs su chad pa med par 'jug kyang thams cad du rnam pa [#]thams cad kyis dmigs par ma gtogs pa gang yin pa der sangs rgyas kyi dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi nyes pa ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa'i don du
[\[124b.3\]]de ma gtogs pa rnams kyi bdag nyid kyi nyes pa las brtsams te tshigs su bcad pa[#]/_ji ltar rna ba dang bral bas/_/phra mo'i sgra ni mi myong bzhin/_/thams cad lha yi rna bar yang /_/rna lam du ni mi 'gro bzhin/_/de bzhin chos phra mchog tu ni/_/zhib mo'i ye shes spyod yul
[\[124b.4\]]yang /_/nyon mongs med yid 'ga' zhig gi/_/rna ba'i lam du 'gyur ba yin/_/sprin bzhin zhes bya ba ni/_ji ltar dbyar gyi dus na sprin/_/lo tog phun sum tshogs pa'i rgyu/_/chu yi phung po 'bad med par/_/sa la mngon par [#]'bebs pa ltar/_/de bzhin thugs rje'i
[\[124b.5\]]sprin las ni/_/rgyal ba'i dam chos chu yi char/_/'gro ba'i dge ba'i lo tog rgyu/_/rnam par rtog pa med par 'bebs/_/ji ltar 'jig rten dge ba'i lam 'jug pa[#]/_/rlung bskyod [#]chu char sprin gyis 'bebs pa ltar/_/de bzhin brtse rlung 'gro dge mngon 'phel phyir/_/sangs
[\[124b.6\]]rgyas sprin las dam chos char pa [#]'bebs/_/srid la mkhyen dang brtse chen 'gyur ba dang /_/mi 'gyur ma gos nam mkha'i dkyil gnas pa/_/ting 'dzin gzungs chu dri med snying po can/_/thub dbang sprin ni dge ba'i lo tog rgyu/_/snod rnams sna tshogs nyid las ni/_/ji ltar
[\[124b.7\]]bsil zhing mngar dang 'jam pa dang /_/yang ba'i chu ni sprin de las 'thon [#]pa/_/sa la ba tsha [#]la sogs gnas 'brel bas/_/shin tu mang po'i ror ni 'gyur ba bzhin/_/de bzhin 'phags [#]pa'i yan lag brgyad chu'i [#]char/_/rab yangs brtse sprin snying po las 'thon [#]pa/_/

[\[125a.1\]]'gro ba'i rgyud kyi gnas kyi dbye ba las/_/rnam pa mang po'i ro dang ldan par 'gyur/_/ltos pa med par 'jug pa las ni/_theg pa mchog la dang ba dang /_/bar ma dang ni sdang ba yi/_/phung po gsum ni mi dag dang /_/rma bya dang ni yi dgas 'dra/_/dpyid mthar

[\[125a.3\]]ni rdo rje'i me ni 'bebs pas ni/_/srog chags phra dang ri sul song ba dag la ji ltar sprin ltos med/_/phra dang rgya chen rigs [#]thabs tshul gyis mkhyen pa dang ni brtse ba'i sprin/_/nyon mongs dag 'gyur bdag lta'i bag chags dag las rnam pa [#]kun ltos med/_/sdug bsngal gyi me rab tu
[\[125a.4\]]'jil ba las ni/_'khor ba'i skye 'chi thog mtha' med der 'gro ba'i lam ni rnam pa lnga/_/mi gtsang ba la dri zhim med bzhin 'gro lnga dag la bde ba med/_/de'i sdug [#]rtag tu mi mtshon kha ba rgya tsha [#]la sogs reg skyes bzhin/_/thugs rje'i sprin las dam chos char chen de rab zhi byed rab tu

[\[134a.2\]]dmigs kyi tshigs su bcad pa/_don sgra ji bzhin yongs rtogs na/_/bdag nyid snyems shing blo nyams 'gyur/_/legs par gsungs pa'ang spangs pas na/_/brlag 'gyur chos la khong khro sgrib/_/bdag nyid snyems zhes bya ba ni/_bdag nyid kyi lta ba mchog tu 'dzin gyi [#]mkhas pa
[\[134a.3\]]las don mi tshol ba'o/_/blo nyams 'gyur zhes bya ba ni/_yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin shes pa las ma thob par yongs su nyams pa'i phyir ro/_/legs par bshad pa'i chos spong ba [#]ni/_de'i gzhi las bsod [#]nams ma yin pa 'phel ba'i phyir brlag par 'gyur ro/_/chos la khong khro ba'i
[\[134a.4\]]sgrib pa ni chos kyis phongs par 'gyur ba'i las te/_'di la nyes dmigs ni de yin no/_/sgra ji bzhin ma yin pa'i don mi [#]shes par yang khong khro bar rigs [#]pa ma yin pas khong khro bar mi rung bar tshigs su bcad pa/_yid kyi nyes pa rang bzhin gdug pa ste/_/mi rigs pa yi gzugs la'ang
[\[134a.5\]]mi rigs na/_/the tshom za ba'i chos la smos ci dgos/_/de phyir btang snyoms [#]bzhag legs nyes pa med/_/rang bzhin gdug pa zhes bya ba ni/_rang bzhin gyis kha na ma tho ba dang bcas pa ste/_de lta bas na btang snyoms su gzhag pa bla'o[#]/_/ci'i phyir zhe na/_de ni nyes pa med kyi khong khro
[\[134a.6\]]ba ni nyes pa dang bcas pa yin no/_/theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan las/_theg pa [#]chen po sgrub pa'i [#]skabs rdzogs so//_//skyabs su 'gro ba'i khyad par bsdu [#]bar tshigs su bcad pa/_kun tu 'gro dang khas len rtogs dang zil gnon par/_/dbye ba'i rang bzhin don rnam [#]bzhi yi khyad par

[\[134b.1\]]khas len pa dang /_rtogs pa dang /_zil gyis gnon par byed pa'i sgo nas rig par bya ste/_kun tu 'gro ba'i don dang /_khas len pa'i don dang /_rtogs [#]pa'i don dang /_zil gyis gnon pa'i don te/_de dag ni 'og nas ston to/_/de lta mod kyi mchog la skyabs su 'gro ba bya dka' ba

[\[135a.1\]]don du gnyer ba ste/_de'i yon tan gyi khyad par shes pa nyid kyis rab tu dga' ba mang ba'i phyir ro/_/sgrub pa'i khyad par ni/_'di ltar skyo ba med par dka' ba spyod pa'o/_/thob pa'i khyad par ni 'di ltar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas sangs rgyas thams cad

[\[135b.1\]]par skyes so zhes bya bar shes te/_'di lta ste/_gzugs phun sum tshogs pa dang /_stobs phun sum tshogs pa dang /_bde ba phun sum tshogs pa dang /_rang gi bzo shes pa phun sum tshogs pa'o/_/yang legs par skyes pa de nyid sangs rgyas kyi gdung rgyun [#]mi gcod pa'i sgo nas tshigs

[\[135b.4\]]bskur ba thob [#]pa dang /_ye shes thogs pa med pa'i phyir chos thams cad la dbang [#]dang ldan pa dang /_sangs rgyas kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du ston pa'i rnam pa [#]shes pa dang /_bslab pa'i gzhi bca' bas nyes pa dang ldan pa dang yon tan dang ldan pa rnams tshar bcad pa dang phan 'dogs par byed pa nyid do/_/

[\[136a.1\]]gsang ba rnam pa gsum 'dzin pa dang /_sems can mtha' yas pa'i don byed pa'i phyir/_rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par sems can mang po'i don byed pa'o/_/rtogs pa'i don du tshigs su bcad pa/_bsod nams phung chen srid gsum bla ma srid pa'i bde ba dang /_/

[\[138a.7\]]po'i don gnas phyir/_/rin po che'i rigs chen po ni rin po che bzhi'i gnas su 'gyur te/_rigs dang ldan pa dang /_kha dog phun sum tshogs pa dang /_dbyibs phun sum tshogs pa dang /_tshad phun sum tshogs pa'i'o[#]/_/byang chub sems dpa'i rigs kyang de dang 'dra bar rig [#]par bya ste/_
[\[138b\]]
[\[138b.1\]]byang chub chen po'i rgyu mtshan yin pa'i phyir dang /_ye shes chen po'i rgyu mtshan yin pa'i phyir dang /_'phags pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyu mtshan yin pa'i phyir te/_ting nge 'dzin ni sems yang dag par gnas pa'o/_/sems can mang po yongs su smin par byed pa'i rgyu mtshan yin pa'i phyir te/_sems
[\[138b.2\]]can mtha' yas pa yongs su smin par byed pa'i phyir ro[#]/_/rigs med pa la gnas pa rnam par dbye bar tshigs su bcad pa/_la la gcig tu nyes par spyod nges yod/_/la la dkar po'i chos rnams kun tu bcom/_/la la thar ba'i cha mthun dge ba med/_/dkar po dman pa yod pa rgyu dang bral/_/
[\[138b.3\]]don 'di la ni rigs med pa la gnas pa yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can yin par bzhed do/_/de yang mdor bsdu na rnam pa gnyis te/_de'i [#]dus dang gtan yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can no/_/de'i dus su yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can yang rnam
[\[138b.4\]]pa bzhi ste/_/gcig tu nyes par spyod pa dang /_dge ba'i rtsa ba kun tu chad pa dang /_thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba med pa dang /[ #]dge ba'i rtsa ba dman pa yod pa tshogs [#]yongs su ma rdzogs pa'o/_/gtan yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can ni rgyu dang bral ba ste/_gang

[\[138b.7\]]chen po 'byung zhing sgrub pa la [#]yang mi skyo la/_tha mar yang phun sum tshogs pa rnam pa gnyis kyi mchog byang chub chen po phun sum tshogs pa 'thob par 'gyur ba [#]yin pa de ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs rang bzhin gyis yon tan dang ldan pa dang rgyas pa'i che ba yin par rig [#]par bya'o/_/rnam pa gnyis
[\[139a\]]
[\[139a.1\]]zhes bya ba ni/_gnyis po 'jig rten pa dang nyan thos dag go/_/mchog ces bya ba ni khyad par du 'phags pa'o/_/'bras bu'i sgo nas rigs khyad par du [#]bya bar tshigs su bcad pa/_yon tan shin tu rgya che byang chub shing bskyed phyir/_/bde dang sdug bsngal chen po zhi ba thob bya'i

[\[139a.3\]]so//_//sems bskyed pa'i mtshan nyid du tshigs su bcad pa/_spro ba che dang rtsom [#]pa che/_/don che ba dang 'byung ba che/_/byang chub sems dpa'i sems dpa' [#]ste/_/don gnyis ldan pa'i sems 'byung ba/_/spro ba chen po ni go cha'i brtson 'grus kyis te/_zab mo dang yun ring por dka' ba

[\[139b.1\]]'dod/_/rtag tu sems can phan par sems/_/chos la mos dang de bzhin de'i/_/ye shes tshol bar dmigs pa'o/_/gong du 'dun [#]pa 'gro ba ste/_/sdom pa rgya chen de yi rten/_/lam 'gog pa ni mi mthun phyogs/_/slong zhing dang du len pa'o/_/bsod nams ye shes rang bzhin gyi/_/
[\[139b.2\]]dge ba'i 'phel ba de'i phan yon/_/pha rol phyin la rtag sbyor ba/_/de ni nges par 'byung bar brjod/_/'di yi mthar thug sa yin te/_/so so rang gi [#]der sbyor bas/_/byang chub sems dpa'i sems bskyed pa/_/rnam par nges par shes par bya/_/de la rnam par gtan la dbab pa ni 'di yin te/_
[\[139b.3\]]byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa rnam pa bzhi po 'di'i rtsa ba ni gang /_bsam pa ni gang /_mos pa ni gang /_dmigs pa ni gang /_'gro ba ni gang /_rten [#]ni gang /_nyes dmigs ni gang /_phan yon ni gang /_nges par 'byung ba ni gang /_mthar thug pa ni gang zhe na/_smras pa/_snying rje chen po ni rtsa

[\[140a\]]
[\[140a.1\]]skye ba yang yod do/_/rgyu'i stobs las te/_rigs kyi mthus skye ba yang yod do/_/dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs las te/_de'i rigs rgyas pa'i sgo nas skye ba yang yod do/_/thos pa'i stobs las skye ba yang yod de/_chos kyi rnam grangs de dang de bshad pa na

[\[140a.7\]]pa'i khyad par dag gis sems bskyed pa don dam pa nyid du ston par byed do/_/don dam pa'i sems bskyed [#]pa de yang sa rab tu dga' ba [#]yin pas de'i rab tu dga' ba khyad par du [#]'phags pa'i rgyu ston te/_de la chos rnams la sems mnyam pa nyid ni chos la bdag med par rtogs pa'i

[\[140b.1\]]phyir ro/_/sems can rnams la sems mnyam pa nyid ni bdag dang gzhan mnyam pa nyid du rtogs pa'i phyir ro/_/sems can gyi bya ba dag la sems mnyam pa nyid ni bdag nyid kyi sdug bsngal dang 'dra bar de dag gi [#]sdug bsngal zad par 'dod pa'i phyir ro/_/sangs rgyas nyid la sems mnyam

[\[140b.7\]]ni rgyal po 'drar shes bya/_/de bzhin gzhan ni mdzod lta bu/_/lam po che dang 'drar shes bya/_/theg pa 'dra bar shes bya ste/_/sems bskyed bkod ma 'dra ba yin/_/kun dga'i sgra dang 'dra ba ste/_/klung [#]chen rgyun dang 'dra ba'o/_/rgyal sras rnams kyis [#]sems bskyed pa/_/sprin
[\[141a\]]
[\[141a.1\]]dang 'dra bar bstan pa ste/_/de phyir de ltar yon tan phyug_/sems ni dga' bas yang dag bskyed/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa dang po ni sa dang mtshungs te/_sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang de'i tshogs 'phel ba'i rten du gyur pa'i
[\[141a.2\]]phyir ro/_/bsam pa dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa ni gser bzang po dang 'dra ste/_phan pa dang bde ba'i bsam pa gzhan [#]du 'gyur ba mi sten [#]pa'i phyir ro/_/sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni zla ba yar gyi ngo'i tshes pa bzhin te/_dge ba'i chos 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/lhag pa'i bsam pa
[\[141a.3\]]dang ldan pa ni me dang 'dra ste/_shing gi bye brag dag gis me bzhin du gong nas gong du khyad par du 'gro ba'i phyir ro/_/lhag pa'i bsam pa ni khyad par rtogs pa'i bsam pa'o/_/sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni gter chen po bzhin te/_zang zing gi longs spyod kyis sems
[\[141a.4\]]can dpag tu med pa tshim par byed pa dang mi zad pa'i phyir ro/_/tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni rin po che'i 'byung gnas lta bu ste/_de las yon tan rin po che thams cad 'byung ba'i phyir ro/_/bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni rgya mtsho dang 'dra [#]ste/_nyam nga ba 'byung ba
[\[141a.5\]]thams cad kyis mi 'khrugs pa'i phyir ro/_/brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni rdo rje lta bu ste/_mi shigs pa nyid kyis sra ba'i phyir ro/_/bsam gtan gyi [#]pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni ri'i rgyal po dang 'dra ste/_rnam par [#]g.yeng bas mi g.yo ba'i phyir ro/_/shes rab kyi
[\[141a.6\]]pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni sman gyi rgyal po lta bu ste/_nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'i nad rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i phyir ro/_/tshad med pa dang ldan pa ni mdza' bo chen po dang 'dra ste/_gnas skabs thams cad du sems can thams cad yal bar mi 'dor ba'i phyir ro/_/mngon
[\[141a.7\]]par shes pa dang ldan pa ni yid bzhin gyi nor bu dang 'dra ste/_ji ltar mos pa bzhin de'i 'bras bu 'byor pa'i phyir ro/_/bsdu ba'i dngos po dang ldan pa bzhi [#]ni nyi ma dang 'dra ste/_gdul ba'i lo tog yongs su smin par byed pa'i phyir ro/_/so so yang dag par rig pa dang ldan pa ni dri za'i
[\[141b\]]
[\[141b.1\]]dbyangs snyan pa lta bu ste/_gdul bya 'dul bar [#]byed [(]ba'i [,]pa'i [)]chos ston pa'i phyir ro/_/rton pa dang ldan pa ni rgyal po lta bu ste/_chud mi za ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro/_/bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs dang ldan pa ni mdzod lta bu ste/_bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs mang po'i
[\[141b.2\]]mdzod kyi gnas yin pa'i phyir ro/_/byang chub kyi phyogs dang mthun pa dang ldan pa ni lam po che lta bu ste/_'phags pa'i gang zag thams cad gshegs shing rjes su gshegs pa'i phyir ro/_/zhi gnas dang lhag mthong dang ldan pa ni/_theg pa lta bu ste/_bde blag tu khyer ba'i phyir ro/_/
[\[141b.3\]]gzungs dang spobs pa dang ldan pa ni bkod ma lta bu ste/_chu 'dzin zhing mi zad par 'byin pa dang chos mthun par thos pa dang ma [#]thos pa'i chos kyi tshig dang don 'dzin zhing mi zad pa 'byin pa'i phyir ro/_/chos bshad pa dang ldan pa ni/_kun dga' ba'i sgra dang 'dra ste/_thar pa 'dod pa'i
[\[141b.4\]]gdul bya rnams la snyan pa thos par byed pa'i phyir ro/_/bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam dang ldan pa ni rlung gi rgyun dang 'dra ste/_mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pa na rang gi [#]ngang gis 'byung ba'i phyir ro/_/bgrod pa gcig pa nyid ni/_sa der gtogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bya ba byed pa tha mi
[\[141b.5\]]dad pa'i phyir ro/_/thabs la mkhas pa dang ldan pa ni sprin lta bu ste/_ji ltar snod kyi 'jig rten gyi 'byor pa thams cad sprin las 'byung ba ltar/_dga' ldan gyi [#]gnas na bzhugs pa la sogs pa ston pa'i sgo nas sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba rnams de la rag [#]las pa'i phyir ro/_/dpe nyi

[\[141b.7\]]dang de yi thabs rnyed dang /_/dgongs chen don dang de nyid mchog mthong bas/_/bde ba de spangs zhi bar 'gro bar 'gyur/_/sems bskyed pa de spangs pa'i sems can rnams kyis bde ba rnam pa bzhi mi 'thob ste/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzhan gyi don sems pas bde ba gang yin pa dang /_
[\[142a\]]
[\[142a.1\]]gzhan gyi don gyi thabs rnyed pas bde ba gang yin pa dang /_dgongs pa chen po'i don mthong ba ste/_theg pa chen po'i mdo zab mo dgongs pa can gyi don rtogs pas bde ba gang yin pa dang /_de kho na nyid mchog gi don chos la bdag med pa mthong bas bde ba gang yin
[\[142a.2\]]pa'o/_/ngan 'gro dang yongs su skyo bas 'jigs pa med pa'i phyir/_sems bskyed pa bsngags par tshigs su bcad pa/_blo ldan sems mchog skyes ma thag tu yang /_/mtha' yas nyes pa byed las sems rab bsdoms[#]/_/gnyis 'phel byed pas rtag tu dge ba dang /_/brtse ldan bde dang
[\[142a.3\]]sdug bsngal dag gis dga'/_/byang chub sems dpa'i [#]sems kyi mchog de skyes ma thag tu sems can mtha' yas pa'i rten can gyi nyes pa byed pa las sems rab tu bsdams par 'gyur te/_de'i phyir 'di ngan 'gros 'jigs par mi 'gyur ro/_/de ni dge ba'i las dang snying brtse ba gnyis
[\[142a.4\]]'phel bar byed pas rtag tu dge ba dang ldan [(]ba [,]pa [)]dang /_snying brtse ba dang ldan par yang 'gyur te/_des na de dge ba dang ldan pa'i phyir/_bde bas kyang dga' la snying brtse ba dang ldan pa'i phyir gzhan gyi don byed pa'i rgyu mtshan can gyi sdug bsngal gyis kyang dga'o/_/de'i phyir 'di bya ba mang pos
[\[142a.5\]]yongs su skyo bas kyang 'jigs par mi 'gyur ro/_/mi byed pa'i sdom pa thob par tshigs su bcad pa/_gang tshe gzhan gyi don phyir lus dang ni/_/srog la mi lta rab ngal khas len pa/_/de lta bu de gzhan gyi gnod pa yis/_/ji ltar ngan par byed pa'i las la 'jug_/de'i bsdus pa'i
[\[142a.6\]]don ni/_gang zhig gzhan gyi don gyi phyir lus dang srog la yang mi lta ba'i phyir/_gzhan nyid ches sdug gi bdag nyid ni ma yin pa de ji ltar gzhan gyis gnod pa byas pas bdag gi [#]don du nyes par byed pa'i las la 'jug par 'gyur/_sems mi ldog par tshigs su bcad pa gnyis
[\[142a.7\]]te/_/de yis chos kun sgyu ma lta bu dang /_/skye [#]ba skyed mos tshal 'gro ltar rtogs nas/_/'byor pa'i dus na rgud pa'i dus na'ang 'di/_/nyon mongs sdug bsngal dag gis 'jigs pa med/_/rang gi yon tan sems can phan 'dogs dga'/_/bsams [#]bzhin skye ba rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul/_/
[\[142b\]]
[\[142b.1\]]rgyan dang ston mo sa mchog rtse dga' ba/_/snying rje'i bdag nyid min pa rnams la med/_/byang chub sems dpa' des chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur mthong ba'i phyir/_'byor pa'i dus na nyon mongs pa rnams kyis mi 'jigs la/_skye ba skyed mos tshal du 'gro ba lta bur mthong ba'i phyir/_
[\[142b.2\]]rgud pa'i dus na sdug bsngal gyis mi 'jigs na/_de'i byang chub kyi sems 'jigs pa gang gis ldog par 'gyur/_gzhan yang rang gi yon tan gyis [#]rgyan dang /_gzhan la phan 'dogs pas dga' ba'i ston mo dang /_bsams bzhin du skye ba'i skyed mos tshal gyis dang /_rdzu [# ]
[\[142b.3\]]'phrul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa'i rtsed mos dga' ba'i byang chub sems dpa' dag kho na la yod kyi/_byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa rnams la ni med na de dag gis [#]sems ji ltar zlog [#]par 'gyur/_sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs pa dag ga par tshigs su bcad pa/_gzhan don brtson ldan snying
[\[142b.4\]]rje'i bdag nyid 'di/_/gang tshe mnar med pa la'ang dga' [#]'dzin pa/_/de 'dra ba dag srid na gzhan rten can/_/sdug bsngal 'byung [#]ba rnams kyis ga la 'jigs/_/gzhan yang gzhan gyi don la brtson pa gang zhig snying rje'i bdag nyid can yin pa'i phyir/_mnar med pa la yang dga' bar

[\[143a.1\]]brtson pa brgya 'gyur du ni bya ba'i rigs/_/byang chub sems dpa' mgo la sems can gyi khur chen po thogs nas pha rol gnon pa dal ba ni mi [#]mdzes kyi/_des nyan thos kyi brtson 'grus pas brtson 'grus brgya 'gyur du bya bar rigs te/_'di ltar de ni bdag

[\[156b.1\]]gos la tshon bkra mi bkra ba/_/de bzhin 'phen pa'i dbang gis na/_/grol ba'i ye shes bkra mi bkra/_/ji ltar mdud pa'i khyad par gyis gos la kha cig tu ni tshon khra bo nyid du 'gyur la/_kha cig tu ni khra bo nyid du mi 'gyur ba de bzhin du sngon gyi smon lam gyi spyod pa'i stobs bskyed pa'i khyad

[\[159b.1\]]'khor dang /_sangs rgyas kyi zhing dang /_mtshan dang /_sku dang /_chos la longs spyod rdzogs pa dang /_mdzad pa dag gis tha dad pa yin no/_/rang bzhin sku ni mnyam pa dang /_/phra zhing de dang 'brel pa dang /_/dgyes dgur longs spyod ldan [#]pa la/_/longs spyod rdzogs 'byor rgyur 'dod do/_/

[\[160a.1\]]rten dang dgongs pa dang /_/phrin las kyis ni mnyam pa nyid/_/rang bzhin dang ni rgyun mi 'chad/_/rgyun gyis de dag rtag pa nyid/_/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku gsum po de dag ni go rims bzhin du rnam pa gsum gyis khyad par med de/_rten gyis ni chos kyi dbyings tha mi

[\[160b.4\]]bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku nges par ston par mdzad pa yin te/_'di ltar sems can kha cig gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa kha dog sngon por/_kha cig gis ni kha dog ser por mthong ngo zhes bya ba de lta bu la sogs pa'o/_/so sor rtog [#]pa'i ye shes ni/_/shes bya kun la rtag mi thogs/_/

[\[192b.1\]]so/_/de ni 'di'i bzod pa'i gnas skabs yin no/_/de'i tshe bar chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzin la yang myur du reg par 'gyur te/_de ni 'di'i 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog gi gnas skabs yin no/_/ci'i phyir de 'di'i bar chad med pa zhes bya zhe na/_'di ltar de yi mjug [# ]
[\[192b.2\]]thogs su/_/'dzin pa'i rnam par g.yeng ba spang [#]/_/'di dag go rims bzhin du ni/_/dro bar gyur pa yin zhes bya/_/de ltar na 'di dag ni nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun par dro bar gyur pa la sogs pa yin no/_/de nas des ni 'jig rten las/_/'das pa'i ye shes bla med
[\[192b.3\]]pas/_/rnam par mi rtog dri ma med/_/'dzin pa gnyis dang bral ba 'thob/_/de yan chad ni mthong ba'i lam gyi gnas [#]skabs yin te/_bla na med pa ni ye shes bla na med pas so/_/rnam par mi rtog pa ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro/_/dri ma
[\[192b.4\]]med pa ni mthong bas spang [#]bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa spangs pa'i phyir te/_'dis ni rdul dang bral ba dang /_dri ma dang bral ba zhes bshad pa yin no/_/'dzin pa gnyis dang bral ba ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro/_/de 'di'i gnas yongs gyur pa ste/_/sa ni dang po
[\[192b.5\]]yin par 'dod/_/'di'i de bskal pa dpag med kyis/_/shin tu rnam par dag par 'gyur/_/tshigs su bcad pa 'di'i don ni [#]go bar zad do/_/chos kyi dbyings ni mnyam pa nyid/_/rab tu rtogs nas de yi tshe/_/rtag tu sems can thams cad la/_/bdag dang mtshungs
[\[192b.6\]]pa'i sems 'thob ste/_/sems can rnams la bdag med dang /_/sdug bsngal dang ni don bya dang /_/lan mi re la 'di sems snyoms/_/rgyal sras gzhan dang 'dra ba yin/_/chos la bdag med pas chos [#]mnyam pa nyid rtogs nas mtshungs pa nyid rnam pa lngas rtag tu sems
[\[192b.7\]]can thams cad la bdag dang mtshungs pa'i sems nyid 'thob ste/_bdag med pa'i mtshungs pa nyid dang /_sdug bsngal mtshungs pa nyid kyis ni rang dang gzhan [#]gyi rgyud dag la bdag med pa dang /_sdug bsngal dag khyad par med pa'i phyir ro/_/bya ba mtshungs pa nyid kyis
[\[193a\]]
[\[193a.1\]]ni rang dang gzhan gyi sdug bsngal spang bar [#]bya dgos par mtshungs pa'i phyir ro/_/lan mi re ba mtshungs pa nyid kyis ni bdag nyid las bzhin du gzhan las lan mngon par mi 'dod pa'i phyir ro/_/de las [#]gzhan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dang mtshungs pa nyid
[\[193a.2\]]kyis ni/_ji ltar de dag gi mngon par rtogs pa de bzhin du mngon par rtogs pa'i phyir ro/_/des ni khams gsum 'dus byas rnams/_/yang dag ma yin kun rtog par/_/ye shes shin tu rnam dag pa/_/gnyis su med pa'i don gyis mthong /_/des ni khams gsum pa'i
[\[193a.3\]]'dus byas rnams yang dag pa ma yin pa'i kun du rtog pa tsam du mthong ste/_ye shes shin tu rnam par dag pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i phyir ro/_/gnyis su med pa'i don gyis zhes bya ba ni gzung ba med pa dang /_'dzin pa med pa'i don gyis so/_/de dag med pa'i ngo bo ni/_/
[\[193a.4\]]mthong ba'i spang bya rnams las grol/_/de nas de tshe mthong ba'i lam/_/thob pa zhes ni nges par brjod/_/gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa de'i ngo bo chos kyi dbyings mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams las rnam par grol bar mthong ngo /_/med pa'i stong pa nyid shes
[\[193a.5\]]shing /_/de bzhin yod pa'i stong nyid dang /_/rang bzhin stong pa nyid shes pas/_/stong pa shes pa zhes brjod do/_/byang chub sems dpa' de ni stong pa nyid rnam pa gsum shes pa'i phyir stong pa shes pa [#]zhes bya'o/_/med pa'i stong pa nyid ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid
[\[193a.6\]]de/_rang gi mtshan nyid kyis med pa'i phyir ro/_/de bzhin du yod pa'i stong pa nyid ni gzhan gyi [#]dbang ste/_de ni ji ltar brtags pa de ltar med kyi/_rang gi mtshan nyid kyis ni yod do/_/rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid de/_stong pa nyid kyi ngo bo nyid
[\[193a.7\]]yin pa'i phyir ro/_/mtshan med gzhi ni rnam rtog [#]rnams/_/yang dag zad pa yin zhes bya/_/smon pa med par gyur pa ste[#]/_/yang dag ma yin kun rtog go/_/mtshan ma med pa'i gzhi ni rnam par rtog pa rnams yang dag par zad pa yin la/_smon pa med pa'i gzhi dmigs pa de ni
[\[193b\]]
[\[193b.1\]]yang dag pa ma yin pa'i kun tu rtog pa dmigs pa yin par shes par bya'o/_/rgyal sras byang chub phyogs mthun par[#]/_rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad ni/_/rtag tu mthong ba'i lam de dang /_lhan cig tu ni thob par 'dod/_/byang chub sems dpa'i byang chub kyi phyogs dang mthun
[\[193b.2\]]pa'i chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa la sogs pa rnam pa [#]sna tshogs thams cad mthong ba'i lam de dang lhan cig 'thob bar rig par bya'o/_/gang zhig blo yis 'gro ba 'dus byas tsam/_/bdag med sdug bsngal rgyas pa tsam shes te/_/don med rang bzhin bdag lta rnams spangs
[\[193b.3\]]nas/_/bdag nyid che lta don chen rnyed pa gang /_/'di na bdag lta med par [#]bdag tu blta[#]/_/sdug bsngal med par shin tu sdug bsngal gyur[#]/_/rang la phan byas bdag la ji lta bar/_/don kun byed la lan kyang re ba med/_/gang zhig grol ba mchog gis sems grol la/_
[\[193b.4\]]'ching ba mi bzad yun [#]yang ring por [#]bcings/_/sdug bsngal mthar thug pa ni ma mthong yang /_/rab tu sbyor ba nyid dang byed pa nyid/_/'di na 'jig rten tshe gcig rang sdug bkur mi nus/_/'jig rten gnas pa srid du gzhan sdug bsngal/_/bsdoms pa smos ci dgos te bsam du med/_/
[\[193b.5\]]byang chub sems dpa' de las bzlog pa yin/_/rgyal sras sems can rnams la dga' ba dang /_/byams pa gang yin sbyor dang mi skyo gang /_/de ni srid pa dag na ngo mtshar che/_/sems can bdag dang mtshungs phyir de lta'ang min/_/tshigs su bcad pa lnga po 'di dag gis ni
[\[193b.6\]]byang chub sems dpa' mthong ba'i lam thob pa'i che ba'i bdag nyid brjod de/_don med pa'i rang bzhin gyis [#]bdag tu lta ba ni/_'jig tshogs la lta ba nyon mongs pa can gang yin pa'o/_/bdag nyid chen po'i lta ba don chen po ni sems can thams cad la bdag dang mnyam pa'i sems
[\[193b.7\]]rnyed pa'i phyir/_bdag tu lta ba gang yin pa ste/_de ni don thams cad byed pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir don chen po yin no/_/don med pa'i rang bzhin gyis [#]bdag tu lta ba med par bdag tu lta ba ni don chen po gang yin pa'o/_/rang gi rgyud las skyes pa'i sdug bsngal med par yang sems
[\[194a\]]
[\[194a.1\]]can thams cad kyi rgyud las skyes pas shin tu sdug bsngal bar gyur pa'o/_/grol ba mchog ni theg pa bla na med pas sems can [#]mthong ba'i lam gyis spang bar bya ba rnams las grol la[#]/_sems can thams cad kyi rgyud las byung ba'i 'ching ba mi zad [# ]
[\[194a.2\]]pa yun ring pos kyang bcings pa'o/_/sems can gyi khams nam mkha' bzhin du mtha' yas pa'i phyir/_sdug bsngal gyi mthar thug pa ma mthong yang sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal mthar bya ba'i phyir rab tu yang sbyor la/_sems can tshad med pa'i don byed pa nyid
[\[194a.3\]]do/_/byang chub sems dpa' de las bzlog pa yin no/_/de ni 'jig rten gnas pa ji srid par sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal bsdoms pa bkur bar nus so/_/byang chub sems dpa' sems can rnams la dga' ba gang yin pa dang /_/phan pa dang bde bar 'dod pa
[\[194a.4\]]gang yin pa dang /_de'i don du sbyor ba gang yin pa dang /_der sbyor ba la mi skyo ba gang yin pa de thams cad ni 'jig rten na shin tu ngo mtshar yang che la/_sems can thams cad bdag dang mtshungs pa'i phyir ngo mtshar yang mi che'o/_/de nas 'di [#]ni lhag ma [#]yi/_/sa rnams
[\[194a.5\]]sgom ba'i lam 'di la/_/ye shes rnam pa gnyis po dag_/bsgom [#]phyir rab tu sbyor bar byed/_/rnam par mi rtog ye shes de/_/sangs rgyas chos ni sbyong bar byed/_/gzhan ni ji bzhin rnam 'jog pa/_/sems can rnams ni yongs smin byed/_/grangs med gnyis
[\[194a.6\]]ni rdzogs pa yis/_/sgom [#]pa yi ni tshar phyin te/_/sgom pa tha ma thob nas ni/_/byang chub sems dpa' dbang bskur ba/_/rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin/_/rtogs [#]pas mi shigs thob nas ni/_/gnas gzhan gyur pa mthar thug pa/_/sgrib pa kun gyi [#]dri med dang /_/gang
[\[194a.7\]]la gnas nas sems can kun/_/phan phyir rab tu sgrub byed pa/_/rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa yi/_/go 'phang bla na med pa 'thob/_/'di dag gis ni sgom pa'i lam bstan te/_ye shes rnam pa gnyis la rnam par mi rtog pa ni gang gis na bdag nyid kyis [#]sangs rgyas kyi
[\[194b\]]
[\[194b.1\]]chos rnam par sbyong bar byed pa yin no/_/ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par 'jog pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rjes la [#]thob pa 'jig rten pa ste/_gang gis na sems can yongs su smin par byed pa yin no/_/grangs med pa gnyis kyis [#]sgom pa'i tha ma mjug tu phyin pa thob nas dbang
[\[194b.2\]]bskur ba'i byang chub sems dpa' ni rnam par rtog pa'i bag la nyal gyis mi shigs pa'i don gyis rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin 'thob po/_/de'i 'og tu gnas gzhan du gyur pa'i mthar phyin pa dang /_gang la gnas nas 'khor ba ji [#]srid par mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa dang /_
[\[194b.3\]]yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa yang dag par ston pa la sogs pas sems can rnams la phan pa rab tu sgrub par byed pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi go 'phang bla na med pa nyon mongs pa dang /_shes bya'i sgrib pa thams cad kyi dri ma med pa 'thob po/_/de ltar mthong dka'i
[\[194b.4\]]thub pa rtag mthong ba/_/thos pa mnyam med las byung rab dang ba'i/_/shugs kyis rtag par shin tu sems tshim pa/_/ji lta bur na don chen 'gyur ma yin/_/chos kyi sgo la rnam par gnas pa la/_/de bzhin gshegs rtag mngon sum 'doms mdzad cing /_/
[\[194b.5\]]co nas 'dren bzhin nyes pa'i [#]tshang tshing nas/_/tshan gyis drangs te byang chub la 'god do/_/sangs rgyas rnams ni rtag tu rang don yang dag sbyor la legs par bsngags pa dang /_/log par sbyor la smod mdzad gnas dang rnam 'byed lhur len mchog gi sems can la/_/gang
[\[194b.6\]]zhig spangs dang bsten pas bde gshegs bstan pa 'di la rnal 'byor yongs 'gyur ba/_/bar chad mthun pa'i chos ni rnam pa thams cad rgyal rnams tshul bzhin 'di na ston/_/tshigs su bcad pa gsum po 'di [#]dag gis ni gdams ngag gi che ba nyid ston te/_gang gis [#]chos
[\[194b.7\]]kyi sgo'i rgyun la gdams ngag 'thob pa des ni rtag tu sangs rgyas mthong bar 'gyur ro/_/des na gang gis na shin tu dang ba'i shugs kyis sems tshim par byas pa 'di sangs rgyas rnams rtag tu mthong ba de don chen por 'gyur ba mtshungs pa med pa'i chos thos so/_/lhag ma ni don
[\[195a\]]
[\[195a.1\]]go bar zad do/_/rjes su bstan pa rnam pa bzhi ni tshigs su bcad pa gcig gis ston te/_lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyi dbang du mdzad nas/_byang chub sems dpa' rang gi don la [#]yang dag par sbyor ba la bsngags pa mdzad pa dang /_log [#]par sbyor ba la
[\[195a.2\]]snod pa mdzad pa dang /_lhag pa'i sems dang /_lhag pa'i shes rab kyi dbang du mdzad nas gnas pa dang /_rnam par 'byed pa lhur len ba la de dag gi bar du gcod pa dang /_de dag dang mthun pa'i chos rnam pa thams cad ston pa'o/_/gang zhig spangs pa dang bsten [#]pas
[\[195a.3\]]zhes bya ba ni bar du gcod pa dang mthun pa ste go rims bzhin no/_/rnal 'byor zhes bya ba ni zhi gnas dang /_lhag mthong sgom pa'o/_/de ni mthong bar [#]rab dag mi rtog byang chub kyis/_/'jig rten thams cad zil mnan mun pa chen po yang /_/rnam pa kun tu bsal nas nyi ma
[\[195a.4\]]chen po dag_/shar ba bzhin du 'gro ba rnams la lham [#]me'o/_/de ltar rtag tu dge ba bsags pas rab gang zhing /_/thub pa las ni rtag tu gdams ngag che thob pa'i/_/sems dpa' mchog ni sems kyi ting [#]'dzin rab yangs pa/_/thob nas yon tan rgya mtsho'i pha rol
[\[195a.5\]]'gro bar 'gyur/_/tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gi don ni [#]go bar zad do/_/gdams ngag rjes su bstan pa'i skabs rdzogs so/_/[#]sdom ni/_mos pa mang ba [#]nyid dang ni/_/chos tshol ba [#]dang bshad pa dang /_/de bzhin sgrub dang yang dag pa'i/_/gdams ngag rjes su bstan pa yin/_/mjug
[\[195a.6\]]sdud pa'i tshigs su bcad pa ste/_/don go bar zad do//_//[#]thabs dang ldan pa'i las rnam par dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa bzhi ste/_ji ltar nags tshal dang ni lus can ri bo dang /_/chu bo rnams kyi rten ni kun nas sa yin pa/_/de bzhin mkhas pa rnams kyi las
[\[195a.7\]]rnams gsum po yang /_/kun nas sbyin pa la sogs dge ba [#]yin par brjod/_/tshigs su bcad pa 'dis ni kun nas slong ba'i thabs bstan te/_sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dge ba pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_byang chub kyi phyogs dang mthun pa la sogs pa rnam pa thams cad ni las
[\[195b\]]
[\[195b.1\]]gsum gyis kun nas bslang ba'i phyir ro/_/mkhas pa rnams kyi zhes bya ba ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi'o/_/nags tshal la sogs pa smos pa ni nye bar spyad par bya ba dang /_nye bar spyod pa po dang /_brtan [#]pa dang /_mi brtan [#]pa'i dngos po nges par bstan pa'i phyir ro/_shin tu dka'
[\[195b.2\]]ba'i las ni [#]ngo bo sna tshogs pa/_/bskal pa mang pos tshar phyin mngon brtson bdag nyid can/_/rgyal sras rnams ni lus dang ngag sems rang bzhin gyi[#]/_/las rnams dag gis 'di na yid 'byung 'gyur ba med/_/ji ltar bdag la phan 'dod dug dang mtshon dang ni/_/gnam lcags lce dang
[\[195b.3\]]dgra las rang gi lus zlog pa/_/de bzhin rgyal sras theg pa dman pa rnam gnyis las/_/las rnams gsum gyis bdag nyid zlog par byed pa yin/_/tshigs su bcad pa 'di gnyis kyis ni ldang ba'i thabs ston te/_theg pa chen po la skyo ba dang /_theg pa gzhan du lhung ba
[\[195b.4\]]las slong ba'i phyir go rims bzhin no/_/yid 'byung ba ni skyo ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/_/theg pa dman pa dang ldan pa'i las ni theg pa dman par sems yongs su bsngo ba'i phyir dang /_theg pa chen po la dge ba'i rtsa ba gcod pa'i phyir dang /_dge ba ma skyes pa [#]mi skyed [#]cing dge
[\[195b.5\]]ba'i lo tog skyes pa 'joms pa'i phyir dang /_sangs rgyas nyid phun sum tshogs pa thob pa'i gegs su gyur pa'i phyir dug la sogs pa dang chos mthun pa yin no/_/rtag tu rnam par mi rtog las can las min zhing /_/las kyi bya ba rnam pa gsum la mi lta ste/_/des na 'dis ni
[\[195b.6\]]de'i [#]thabs yang dag bzung ba'i phyir/_/las rnams dag pa mtha' yas de yi pha rol 'gro/_/tshigs su bcad pa bzhi pa 'dis ni 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i sgo nas las rnam par dag pa'i thabs ston te/_byed pa po dang /_las dang bya ba rnams mi dmigs pa'i phyir ro/_/mtha'
[\[195b.7\]]yas pa zhes bya ba ni mi zad pa'i phyir ro/_/thabs dang ldan pa'i las kyi skabs [#]rdzogs so//_//pha rol tu phyin pa rab tu dbye ba'i bsdu ba'i sdom ni/_/grangs dang de yi mtshan nyid go rims dang /_/nges pa'i tshig dang goms bya yon tan dang /_/de dag rab dbye bsdu dang mi
[\[196a\]]
[\[196a.1\]]mthun phyogs/_/yon tan phan tshun rnam nges yin zhes bya/_/grangs rnam par dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa drug ste/_re zhig_/longs spyod dang lus phun sum tshogs pa dang /_/'khor rtsom [#]phun sum tshogs pa mngon mtho dang /_/rtag tu nyon mongs dbang nyid mi
[\[196a.2\]]'gro dang /_/bya ba rnams la phyin ci ma log pa'o/_/zhes bya ba ni dang po'o/_/de la pha rol tu phyin pa bzhis ni mngon par mtho ba rnam pa bzhi ste/_sbyin pas ni longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa'o/_/tshul khrims kyis ni lus phun sum tshogs pa'o/_/bzod pas ni 'khor phun sum tshogs
[\[196a.3\]]pa ste/_'di ltar de bstan [#]pas tshe phyi ma la skye bo mang po dga' bar 'gyur ro/_/brtson 'grus kyis ni rtsom [#]pa phun sum tshogs pa ste/_las kyi mtha' thams cad 'grub pa'i phyir ro/_/lnga pas [#]ni nyon mongs pa'i dbang du mi 'gro ba nyid de[#]/_bsam gtan gyis ni nyon mongs pa rnam par
[\[196a.4\]]gnon pa'i phyir ro/_/drug pas ni bya ba rnams la phyin ci ma log pa ste/_bya ba thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes pa'i phyir ro/_/de ltar na mngon par mtho ba dang /_de la yang kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang /_bya ba la phyin ci ma log pa dang /_rtsom pa'i dbang du byas
[\[196a.5\]]nas pha rol tu phyin pa drug rnam par gzhag go/_/sems can don la rab brtson pa/_/gtong dang mi gnod bzod pas byed/_/gnas dang grol ba gzhir [#]bcas pas/_/rang don rnam pa thams cad spyod/_/ces bya ba ni gnyis pa ste/_byang chub sems dpa' sems can gyi [#]don
[\[196a.6\]]rnams la yang dag par rab tu brtson pa ni [#]pha rol tu phyin pa gsum po sbyin pa dang /_tshul khrims dang /_bzod pa dag gis go rims bzhin du gtong ba dang /_mi gnod pa dang /_gnod pa byed pa bzod pas sems can gyi don byed do/_/gsum gyis ni sems gnas pa dang /_rnam
[\[196a.7\]]par grol ba gzhi [#]dang bcas pas rang gi don rnam pa thams cad spyod de[#]/_brtson 'grus la brten nas go rims bzhin du bsam gtan dang /_shes rab dag gis sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa mnyam par [#]'jog pa'i phyir dang /_mnyam par bzhag pa rnam par grol ba'i phyir ro/_/de
[\[196b\]]
[\[196b.1\]]ltar na gzhan gyi [#]don dang rang gi don las brtsams te pha rol tu phyin pa drug go/_/mi phongs pa dang rnam par mi 'tshe dang /_/rnam 'tshe bzod dang bya bas mi skyo dang /_/dga' byed legs par brjod pa de yi phyir/_/gzhan gyi don ni rang gi don yin no/_/zhes bya ba ni gsum pa yin te/_byang
[\[196b.2\]]chub sems dpa'i gzhan gyi don mtha' dag ni sbyin pa la sogs pas go rims bzhin du gzhan dag la yo byad kyis mi phongs pa dang /_rnam par mi 'tshe ba dang /_rnam par 'tshe ba bzod pa dang /_grogs bya ba [#]la skyo ba med pa dang /_rdzu 'phrul la sogs pa'i mthus dga' bar byed pa dang /_
[\[196b.3\]]the tshom gcod pa'i sgo nas legs par brjod pa dag gis 'gyur ro/_/de'i phyir na gzhan gyi [#]don ni byang chub sems dpa' rang gi don du 'gyur te/_gzhan gyi don ni rang gi don yin pa'i phyir dang /_byang chub chen po 'thob pa'i phyir ro/_/de ltar na rang dang gzhan gyi don mtha' dag gi
[\[196b.4\]]skabs kyis [#]pha rol tu phyin pa drug go/_/longs spyod mngon par mi dga' dang /_/rab gus gnyis la mi skyo dang /_/rnal 'byor rnam par mi rtog pa/_/theg chen mtha' dag 'dir zad do/_/zhes bya ba ni bzhi pa ste/_/sbyin pas ni byang chub sems dpa' longs spyod rnams la mi lta ba'i
[\[196b.5\]]phyir mngon par mi dga'o/_/tshul khrims yang dag par blangs pas ni byang chub sems dpa' bslab pa dag la shin tu gus pa nyid do/_/bzod pa dang brtson 'grus kyis ni go rims bzhin du sems can dang sems can ma yin pas byas pa'i sdug bsngal dang /_dge ba la [#]rab tu sbyor ba dang
[\[196b.6\]]gnyis la skyo ba med do/_/bsam gtan dang shes rab dag gis ni zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gis bsdus pa'i rnal 'byor rnam par mi rtog pa [#]ste/_theg pa chen po mtha' dag ni [#]'di tsam du zad do/_/de'i phyir theg pa chen po kun bsdus pa'i dbang du byas nas pha rol tu phyin pa drug go/_/
[\[196b.7\]]yul rnams la ni ma chags lam/_/de thob rnam g.yeng sdom pa'i lam/_/sems can mi gtong [#]'phel ba dang /_/sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i gzhan/_/zhes bya ba ni lnga pa'o/_/de la sbyin pa ni yul rnams la ma [#]chags pa'i lam yin te/_gtong ba la goms pas de la chags
[\[197a\]]
[\[197a.1\]]pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro/_/tshul khrims ni de thob pa'i rnam par g.yeng ba [#]yang dag par sdom pa rnams kyi lam yin te/_dge slong gi sdom pa la gnas pa la yul thob par bya ba'i phyir/_las kyi mtha'i rnam par g.yeng ba thams cad mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro/_/
[\[197a.2\]]bzod pa ni sems can mi gtong ba'i lam ste/_gnod pa byed pa thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyis yid mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro/_/brtson 'grus ni dge ba 'phel ba'i lam ste/_brtson 'grus brtsams pa la de 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/bsam gtan dang shes rab ni
[\[197a.3\]]sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba dag gi [#]lam yin te/_de gnyis kyis nyon mongs pa dang /_shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i phyir ro/_/lam zhes bya ba ni thabs te/_de ltar na lam gyi rnam pa thams cad kyi dbang du byas nas pha rol tu phyin pa drug go/_/bslab gsum dbang du mdzad nas

[\[215a.4\]]sogs pa gcig tu nyes par spyod pa rnams te/_las kyi rnam par smin pa la kun tu rmongs pa'i phyir ro/_/bgrod dka' ba'i lam la kun tu zhugs pa ni/_yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can rnams te/_'khor ba'i lam gtan rgyun mi gcod pa'i phyir ro/_/'ching ba chen po dang
[\[215a.5\]]yang dag par ldan pa ni/_/gzhan mu stegs can thar pa la [#]kun tu zhugs pa rnams te/_lta ba ngan pa sna tshogs kyi 'ching ba dam pos bcings pa'i phyir ro/_/zas chen po dug dang 'dres pa la zhen pa ni/_snyoms par 'jug pa'i bde ba [#]la zhen pa rnams te/_de dag gi snyoms par 'jug pa'i
[\[215a.6\]]bde ba nyon mongs pa can ni/_dper na kha zas zhim po dug dang 'dres pa dang 'dra ste/_de las rab tu nyams par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/lam rab tu stor ba ni mngon pa'i nga rgyal can rnams te/_thar pa'i lam nor ba'i phyir ro/_/lam gol ba la rab tu zhugs pa ni/_ma nges pa theg pa

[\[215b.1\]]pa/_'tshe spongs byang chub mchog gi sa bon dang /_/bde ba skyed [#]dang gdung byed 'dod pa'i rgyu/_/ngo bo nyid sbyin chos la rten [#]pa yi/_/rgyal ba'i sras la byang chub thag mi ring /_/de la 'tshe ba spangs pa nyid kyis ni de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs rnam par 'tshe ba spangs pa'i phyir bral ba'i 'bras bu

[\[215b.4\]]mchog 'khor bar gtogs [#]pa yi/_/sdug bsngal bdag nyid kun dang bdag med pa'ang /_/rnam par shes nas skyo bar mi 'gyur zhing /_/nyes pas rab [#]gnod par yang mi 'gyur ro/_/byang chub sems dpa' 'khor bar gtogs pa thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin yongs su shes

[\[216a.1\]]kyang snying rje'i khyad par gyis skyo bar mi 'gyur ro zhes bya bar rab tu ston to/_/snying rje'i rab tu dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa gnyis te/_snying rje'i bdag nyid can gyi brtse ba 'di/_/rang bzhin dang ni so sor brtags pa dang /_/de sngon goms par byas dang ldan pa dang /_/mi mthun phyogs

[\[219b\]]
[\[219b.1\]]pa med par rab tu dga' bas sbyin pa'i phyir ro/_/zang zing med pa ni gos pa med pa ji lta ba bzhin no/_/dag pa ni gzhi dag pa ji lta ba bzhin no/_/byang chub la gzhol ba ni byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pa'i phyir ro/_/dge ba la gzhol ba ni bde ba bskyed [#]pa ji lta ba bzhin no/_/nye
[\[219b.2\]]bar spyod [#]pa'i khyad par gyi tshigs su bcad pa/_ji ltar bde ba gsum gyis tshim pa'i yid/_/brtse ldan yongs su gtong bas dga' 'gyur bas/_/longs spyod can dag nye bar spyod [#]pa yis/_/de ltar dga' bar 'gyur ba ma yin no/_/de la bde ba gsum ni sbyin pas dga'
[\[219b.3\]]ba dang /_gzhan rjes su 'dzin pas dga' ba dang /_/byang chub kyi tshogs rdzogs pas dga' ba'o/_/lhag ma ni don go bar zad do/_/pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par sgrub pa'i snying rje'i tshigs su bcad pa/_/bkren la brtse dang ma rungs pa la brtse/_/kun 'khrugs la brtse bag med [# ]
[\[219b.4\]]rnams la brtse/_/yul gyi gzhan dbang can la snying rje dang /_/log par mngon par zhen la snying rje ba'o/_/de la bkren pa ni ser sna can rnams so/_/ma rungs pa ni tshul khrims 'chal pa gzhan la gnod pa rnams so/_/kun tu 'khrugs pa ni khro ba can rnams so/_/bag med pa ni le lo can rnams so/_/yul gyi gzhan
[\[219b.5\]]dbang can ni 'dod pa dag la sems rnam par g.yengs pa [#]rnams so/_/log par mngon par zhen pa ni/_shes rab 'chal ba mu stegs can la sogs pa'o/_/pha rol tu phyin pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs la gnas pa 'di dag la/_snying rje ba gang yin pa de ni bkren pa la sogs pa
[\[219b.6\]]la snying rje ba yin te/_de yang de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs rnam par sun 'byin pa'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par sgrub par byed par 'gyur ro/_/de ltar na pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par sgrub pa'i snying rje zhes bya'o/_/snying rje'i rkyen bstan pa'i tshigs su bcad pa/_bde dang sdug
[\[219b.7\]]bsngal de rgyu las/_/byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje ste/_/rgyu dang bshes gnyen rang bzhin las/_/byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje'o/_/de la phyed gong mas ni snying rje'i dmigs pa'i rkyen ston te/_tshor ba rnam pa gsum la dmigs nas sdug bsngal nyid gsum gyis snying rje bar
[\[220a\]]
[\[220a.1\]]byed pa'i phyir ro/_/bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal ba yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba ni bde ba dang sdug bsngal dag gi rgyu yin te/_yang de dag 'dren pa'i phyir ro/_/phyed 'og mas ni go rims bzhin du rgyu dang bshes gnyen dang rang bzhin dag gis snying rje'i rgyu dang bdag po dang
[\[220a.2\]]mtshungs pa de ma thag pa'i rkyen rnams ston to/_/snying rje chen po nyid kyi tshigs su bcad pa/_byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje ni/_/mnyam par shes bya de bsam phyir/_/sgrub phyir 'dod chags bral phyir dang /_/mi dmigs phyir dang dag phyir ro/_/de la mnyam pa ni tshor ba rnam pa gsum
[\[220a.3\]]car [#]gyi gnas skabs su gang ci tshor ba de ni [#]'dir sdug bsngal ba'o zhes bya bar rig pa'i phyir ro/_/de yang bsam pa'i phyir ni sems kyis snying rje ba'i phyir ro/_/sgrub pa'i phyir ni de yongs su skyob pa'i [#]phyir ro/_/'dod chags dang bral ba'i phyir ni de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs rnam par 'tshe ba
[\[220a.4\]]spangs pa'i phyir ro/_/mi dmigs pa'i phyir ni bdag dang gzhan dang snying rjer mi dmigs pa'i phyir ro/_/[#]rnam par dag pa'i phyir ni/_sa brgyad pa la mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pa'i phyir ro/_/rang gi sems kyi [#]byams la sogs/_/bsgom pa chos la mos pa dang /_/bsam
[\[220a.5\]]dang dbang 'byor nyid dang ni/_/rnam par mi rtog [#]gcig phyir mchog_/ces bya ba'i don ni gang [#]du bshad pa'i rjes su 'brangs te khong du chud par bya'o/_/de ltar bcom ldan 'das la dang ba rab skyes shing /_/rdzas dang bkur sti chen pos shin tu rgyun mchod ldan/_/yon tan mang ldan phan
[\[220a.6\]]byed bshes la rtag bsten pa[#]/_/'gro la rjes su brtse ba grub pa kun thob 'gyur/_/'dis ni ji skad bshad pa'i mchod pa dang bstan [#]pa dang tshad med pa rnams kyi go rims dang yon tan mdor bsdus nas ston te/_rdzas dang bkur sti chen pos shin tu rtag tu mchod pa ni rdzas dang bkur sti chen pos
[\[220a.7\]]shin tu rgyun du mchod pa dang ldan pa ste/_/bkur sti ni yang dag pa'i sgrub pa yin par rig par bya'o/_/de ltar na rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang sgrub pa'i mchod pa dang ldan pa yin no/_/yon tan mang po dang ldan pa ni de las gzhan pa dag dang ngo /_/phan par byed pa ni rjes su brtse bar byed pa nyid
[\[220b\]]
[\[220b.1\]]kyis rig par bya'o/_/grub pa kun thob par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba ni rang dang gzhan gyi don [#]grub pa 'thob par 'gyur ba'o/_/mchod pa dang bstan [#]pa dang tshad med pa'i skabs rdzogs so//_//ngo tsha ba rnam par dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa bcu drug ste/_/ngo tsha mi mthun phyogs spangs dang /_/
[\[220b.2\]]rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/_/kha na ma tho med dman yul/_/sems can smin byed brtan [#]pa'i yin/_/'dis ni ngo bo nyid dang /_grogs dang /_dmigs pa dang /_las phun sum tshogs pas byang chub sems dpa'i ngo tsha ba'i mtshan nyid rnam pa bzhi ston te/[# ]yul kha na ma tho ba med cing dman
[\[220b.3\]]pa ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa ste/_de ni kha na ma tho ba med pa yang yin la/_theg pa chen po bas dman pa yang yin pas des kyang byang chub sems dpa' ngo tsha'o/_/ji ltar sems can rnams yongs su smin par byed ce na/_/ngo tsha ba de nyid la gzhan dag rab tu 'god
[\[220b.4\]]pa'i phyir ro/_/pha rol [#]phyin pa drug po yi/_/mi mthun phyogs ni 'phel ba dang /_/gnyen po 'grib pas byang chub sems/_/mi bzad ngo tsha skye bar 'gyur/_/'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'phel ba [#]dang 'grib pas ngo tsha ba yin te/_pha rol tu phyin pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs 'phel ba dang /_
[\[220b.5\]]de'i gnyen po yongs su 'grib pas [#]shin tu ngo tsha ba skye ba'i phyir ro/_/brtan rnams pha rol phyin pa drug_/bsten [#]pa la ni le lo dang /_/nyon mongs rjes su mthun chos la/_/sbyor ba las kyang ngo tshar 'gyur/_/'di ni mi sbyor ba dang sbyor bas ngo tsha ba yin te/_pha rol tu phyin pa sgom pa la
[\[220b.6\]]mi sbyor ba dang /_nyon mongs pa dang mthun pa'i chos dbang po'i sgom bsdams pa la sogs pa la sbyor bas ngo tsha ba skye ba'i phyir ro/_mnyam gzhag ngo bo nyid min chung /_/'bring dang dman pa'i sa pa dang /_/bsam pa dman dang ngar bcas pa'i/_/ngo tsha dman de las gzhan lhag_/'di ni ngo
[\[220b.7\]]tsha ba chung ngu dang chen po ste/_tshigs su bcad pa 'di'i don ni/_sngar bshad pa'i rjes su 'brangs nas khong du chud par bya'o/_/'di man chad tshigs su bcad pa bzhi [#]dang gsum gyis go rims bzhin du ngo tsha ba'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang /_ngo tsha ba'i skyon dang /_yon tan gyi dbye ba ston
[\[221a\]]
[\[221a.1\]]to/_/blo ldan ngo tsha med pa ni/_/tshul bzhin min pas nyon mongs dag_/dang du len cing khong khro dang /_/yal bar 'dor dang nga rgyal gyis/_/sems can rnams dang tshul khrims 'joms/_/zhes bya ba 'dis ni bdag nyid la yang gnod par byed la/_gzhan la
[\[221a.2\]]yang gnod par byed/_gnyi ga la yang gnod par byed ces bstan to/_/tshul bzhin ma yin [(]ba [,]pa [)#]zhes bya ba ni tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pas so/_/yal bar 'dor bas ji ltar sems can rnams 'joms she na/_sems can gyi don la bag med pa'i phyir ro/_/'gyod pas nyams dang
[\[221a.3\]]bcas 'gyur zhing /_/bkur stis dman pa 'thob 'gyur des/_/dad ldan mi min tshogs dang ni/_/ston pas kyang ni btang snyoms mdzad/_/rgyal sras chos dang mthun rnams kyis/_/rnam par smod cing [#]'jig rten las/_/mthong ba'i chos la mi snyan 'thob/_/gzhan du phyir zhing
[\[221a.4\]]mi khom skye/_/zhes bya ba 'dis mi mthong ba'i chos kyi kha na ma tho ba 'phel lo zhes ston te/_go rims bzhin du bdag nyid dang /_/gzhan dang lha dang ston pa dag smod pa'i phyir dang /_tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa mkhas pa dang [#]/_chos nyid kyis rnam par smod [#]pa'i phyir dang /_phyogs
[\[221a.5\]]dang phyogs mtshams su yang sdig pa can gyi mi snyan pa 'byung ba'i phyir ro/_/gzhan du phyir zhing mi khom skye/_/zhes bya ba 'dis ni tshe phyi ma'i kha na ma tho ba 'phel lo zhes bstan te/_mi khom pa rnams su skye ba'i phyir ro[#]/_/des na chos dkar thob pa dang /_ma thob pa las rnam [#]nyams
[\[221a.6\]]'gyur/_/zhes bya ba 'dis ni mthong ba'i chos dang tshe phyi ma'i kha na ma tho ba 'phel lo zhes bstan te[#]/_dge ba'i chos thob pa las yongs su nyams pa dang /_ma thob pa las yongs su nyams pa dang /_go rims bzhin no/_/de phyir sdug bsngal gnas pa dang /_/yid kyang rnal du mi gnas 'gyur/_/
[\[221a.7\]]zhes bya ba 'dis ni de las skyes pa'i sems kyi sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba so sor myong bar 'gyur ro zhes bstan to/_/rgyal sras ngo tsha ldan rnams la/_/nyes pa 'di dag kun mi 'byung /_/zhes bya ba 'di nas bzung ste ngo tsha ba'i yon tan yin par rig par bya ste/_'di ltar nyes pa 'di
[\[221b\]]
[\[221b.1\]]dag kyang mi 'byung bas so/_/mkhas pa rtag tu lha dag dang /_/mi rnams su ni yang dag skye/_/zhes bya ba 'di ni de'i rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu yin no/_/blo ldan ngo tshas myur du ni/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub tshogs rdzogs byed/_/ces bya ba 'di ni bdag po'i 'bras bu'o/_/rgyal ba'i sras
[\[221b.2\]]ni sems can rnams/_/smin byed skyo bar mi 'gyur nyid/_/ces bya ba 'di ni skyes bu byed pa'i 'bras bu yin no/_/de rtag mi mthun phyogs dang ni/_/gnyen po bral dang [#]mi 'bral 'gyur/_/zhes bya ba 'dis ni bral ba dang rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu dag bstan te/_'di lta ste/_mi mthun
[\[221b.3\]]pa'i phyogs dang bral ba nyid dang gnyen po dang ma bral ba nyid do/_/de ltar rgyal sras ngo tsha ldan/_/phan yon de dag 'thob par 'gyur/_/zhes bya bas ni/_ji skad bshad pa'i nyes pa med pa dang yon tan dang ldan pa 'thob bo zhes bstan to/_/byis pa shin tu gos bzang gyon yang ni/_/khrel
[\[221b.4\]]dang bral phyir nyes pas dri ma can/_/rgyal sras ngo tsha shes pa'i gos can ni/_/dgab [#]pa med kyang nyes pa'i dri ma bral/_/'dis ni ngo tsha med pa ni de las [#]gzhan pa'i gos gyon yang nyes pas dri ma can yin pa'i phyir la/_ngo tsha dang ldan pa ni gcer bur 'dug kyang dri ma med pa'i phyir/_ngo tsha ni gos
[\[221b.5\]]khyad par du 'phags pa yin no zhes ston to/_/rgyal ba'i sras ni khrel dang ldan gyur pa/_/nam mkha' bzhin du chos kyis mi gos 'gyur/_/chos kyis [#]zhes bya ba ni 'jig rten pa'i chos rnams [#]so/_/rgyal sras rnams kyi nang du 'dus gyur pa/_/ngo tsha shes pas brgyan pa mdzes pa yin/_/
[\[221b.6\]]tshigs su bcad pa 'dis ni ngo tsha ba nam mkha' dang rgyan dang 'dra ba nyid du ston to/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni ngo tsha bas/_/gdul ba rnams la ma bzhin byams pa nyid/_/bskyab [#]par bya ba'i sems can yal bar bor na ngo tsha ba'i phyir ro/_/ngo tsha ba ni nyes pa thams cad las/_/
[\[221b.7\]]'khor ba kun tu srung [#]bar byed pa'ang yin/_/glang po che dang rta'i tshogs la sogs pa dang 'dra ba'i phyir ro/_/gos la sogs pa'i dpe 'di rnams kyis ngo tsha bas gnas pa na nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po nyid dang /_rgyu ba na 'jig rten gyi [#]chos kyi gnyen po nyid dang chos mthun pa dang /_
[\[222a\]]
[\[222a.1\]]gnas pa dang mthun pa nyid dang /_sems can yongs su smin par byed pa dang mthun pa nyid dang /_nyon mongs pa can ma yin par 'khor ba dang mthun pa nyid ston to/_/kun la dang du [#]len pa dang /_/kun la dang du mi len zhing /_/kun la mi 'jug 'jug pa ni/_/khrel
[\[222a.2\]]ldan khrel bas byas pa'i rtags/_/'dis ni ngo tsha ba dang ldan pa'i rtags [#]ngo tsha bas byas pa rnam pa bzhi ston te/_'di lta ste/_nyes pa thams cad la dang du mi len zhing mi 'jug pa dang /_yon tan thams cad la dang du len zhing 'jug pa'o/_/rang gi sems kyis khrel sgom pa/_chos la mos dang bsam pa dang /_/
[\[222a.3\]]dbang 'byor ba dang mi rtog [#]dang /_/gcig pa nyid kyis gtso bo yin/_/zhes bya ba 'di'i bshad pa ni snga ma bzhin no/_/brtan pa rnam par dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa bdun te/_byang chub sems dpa'i brten [#]pa ni/_/de las gzhan pa thams cad las/_/mtshan nyid dang ni rab dbye dang /_/mi
[\[222a.4\]]'gyur bas ni khyad par 'phags/_/brtson 'grus ting 'dzin shes rab ni/_/snying stobs sran thub brtan [#]bar 'dod/_/gang phyir gsum gyis byang chub sems/_/'jigs pa med par rab tu 'jug//_'dis ni brtan [#]pa'i mtshan nyid rnam grangs dang bcas sgrub pa dang bcas par bshad de/_
[\[222a.5\]]brtson 'grus la sogs pa ni mtshan nyid do/_/snying stobs la sogs pa ni [#]rnam grangs so/_/lhag ma ni sgrub pa'o/_/ji ltar gsum po 'dis 'jigs pa med par rab tu 'jug ce na/_zhum dang g.yo dang rmongs pa yis[#]/_/bya ba rnams la 'jigs pa skye[#]/_/de phyir gnyug ma gsum la ni/_/
[\[222a.6\]]brtan pa'i ming du shes par bya/_/bya ba thams cad la 'jigs pa ni yang na ni zhum pa'i sems kyis skye ste/_de la mi spro ba'i phyir ro/_/yang na ni g.yo ba'i sems kyis te/_sems rnal du mi gnas pa'i phyir ro/_/yang na ni rmongs pas te/_de'i thabs mi shes pa'i phyir ro/_/de dag gi [# ]
[\[222a.7\]]gnyen por [#]ni go rims bzhin du brtson 'grus la sogs pa ste/_de lta bas na brtson 'grus la sogs pa gnyug ma gsum la brtan pa zhes bya bar rig par bya'o/_/gnyug ma zhes bya ba ni so sor brtag pa med par byed pa'o/_/rang bzhin dang ni smon lam dang /_/lta ba med pa nyid dang ni/_/
[\[222b\]]
[\[222b.1\]]sems can log par sgrub pa dang /_/zab cing rgya che thos pa dang /_/gdul bya gdul bar dka' ba dang /_/rgyal sku bsam gyis mi khyab dang /_/dka' ba dag ni sna tshogs dang /_/'khor ba gtong ba med nyid dang /_/de nyid nyon mongs med pa la/_/brtan pa'i brtan [#]pa skye ba ni/_/de las gzhan
[\[222b.2\]]dang mi mtshungs te/_/brtan ldan rnams kyi mchog tu 'dod/_/tshigs su bcad pa gsum po 'dis ni brtan pa'i rab tu dbye ba ston te[#]/_go rims bzhin du rigs dang /_sems bskyed pa dang /_rang gi don dang /_gzhan gyi don dang /_de kho na nyid kyi don dang /_mthu dang /_sems
[\[222b.3\]]can yongs su smin par byed pa dang /_byang chub mchog gi sgo nas so/_/de la mi lta ba nyid ni rang gi don la zhugs pa lus dang srog la mi lta ba nyid las rig par bya'o/_/yang dka' ba spyod pa dang /_bsams bzhin du srid par skye ba dang /_de na kun nas nyon mongs ba med pa'i sgo nas kyang
[\[222b.4\]]rab tu dbye ba yin no/_/phye ma leb dang 'dab chags dang /_/rgya mtsho dag gis ri rab ltar/_/brtan pa grogs ngan sdug bsngal dang /_/zab mo thos pas mi g.yos so/_/'dis ni byang chub sems dpa'i brtan pa'i mi 'gyur ba nyid ston te/_dpe gsum ni [#]gsum gyis mi g.yos pa dang
[\[222b.5\]]go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o/_/mi skyo ba'i rnam par dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa gnyis te/_byang chub mi skyo mnyam med pa/_/gzhi gsum thos pas mi ngoms dang /_/brtson 'grus che dang sdug bsngal la/_/khrel dang brtan la brtan [#]pa ste/_/byang chub che la 'dun pa drag_/_
[\[222b.6\]]blo ldan rnams kyi mi skyo ba/_/sa rnams la ni ma rdzogs dang /_/rdzogs dang shin tu rdzogs par 'dod/_/'di gnyis kyis ni gzhi dang /_rten dang /_ngo bo nyid dang /_rab tu dbye ba'i sgo nas mi skyo ba bstan te/_gzhi gsum ni thos pas mi ngoms pa dang /_yun ring por brtson 'grus rtsom
[\[222b.7\]]pa dang /_'khor ba'i sdug bsngal la'o/_/khrel yod pa dang brtan pa la brten nas de dag gis skyo ba skyes nas ngo tsha zhing mi skyo bar yang byed do/_/byang chub chen po la 'dun pa drag po zhes bya ba ni ngo bo nyid de/_'dun pa log na skyo bar 'gyur bas so/_/ma rdzogs pa ni mos pas spyod pa'i sa
[\[223a\]]
[\[223a.1\]]la'o/_/rdzogs pa ni sa bdun po dag la'o/_/shin tu rdzogs pa ni [#]de yan chad kyi sa la ste 'di ni rab tu dbye ba yin no/_/bstan bcos shes pa nyid kyis [#]tshigs su bcad [#]pa gnyis te/_brtan [#]pa'i bstan bcos shes pa nyid/_/gzhi dang ched du bya ba dang /_/las
[\[223a.2\]]dang mtshan nyid dag dang ni/_/mi zad nyid dang 'bras bu ni/_/yang dag 'grub pas khyad par 'phags/_/ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs sgos bsdus/_/sems can smin par byed pa dang /_/dam chos 'dzin par byed pa'ang yin/_/de la bstan bcos shes pa nyid kyi gzhi [#]ni rig pa'i gnas lnga
[\[223a.3\]]ste/_nang [#]rig pa dang /_gtan tshigs rig pa dang /_sgra rig pa dang /_gso ba rig pa dang /_bzo'i las kyi gnas rig pa'o/_/ched du bya ba ni/_rang dang gzhan gyi don bya ba'o/_/las ni gzhi dang po la bdag nyid sgrub cing gzhan dag la yang de yang dag par ston pa dang /_gnyis pa la de'i
[\[223a.4\]]skyon yongs su shes shing pha rol rgol ba tshar bcad pa dang /_gsum pa la bdag nyid nges pa'i tshig bzang po brjod cing gzhan yid ches par byed pa dang /_bzhi pa la gzhan dag gi nad rab tu zhi bar byed pa dang /_lnga pa la gzhan dag la [#]de bgo bsha' byed pa'o/_/bstan bcos shes pa nyid
[\[223a.5\]]kyi mtshan nyid ni gzhi lnga po 'di dag nyid thos shing 'dzin pa dang /_tshig gis byang ba dang /_yid kyis brtag [#]pa dang /_mthong bas legs par rtogs pa dag yin te/_thos nas go rims bzhin du de 'dzin pa dang /_kha ton byed pa dang /_ci rigs par de dag gi skyon dang yon tan khong du chud
[\[223a.6\]]pa'i sgo nas rab tu dang ba'i yid kyis don sems pa dang /_legs par bshad pa dang nyes par bshad pa dmigs phyed pa'i phyir ro/_/mi zad pa nyid ni phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa na yang mi zad pa'i phyir ro/_/'bras bu yang dag par 'grub pa ni chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad
[\[223a.7\]]du mkhyen pa nyid do/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bstan bcos shes pa nyid de yang ting nge [#]'dzin gyi sgo dag dang /_gzungs kyi sgo dag gis bsdus la [#]sems can yongs su smin par byed pa yang yin te/_ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo dag nas de'i bya ba bsgrub [#]pa'i phyir ro/_/dam pa'i chos 'dzin par byed pa
[\[223b\]]
[\[223b.1\]]yang yin te/_gzungs dag gis de 'dzin pa'i phyir ro/_/'jig rten shes pa nyid kyi tshigs su bcad pa bzhi ste/_brtan rnams 'jig rten shes pa nyid/_/lus dang ngag dang yid dang ni/_/bden pa shes pas mnyam pa med/_/de la gzhan pa dag las 'phags/_/ji ltar lus kyis she na/_bshad
[\[223b.2\]]pa/_brtan rnams rtag tu 'dzum par byed/_/ji ltar ngag gis she na/_bshad pa/_gsong po dag tu smra ba yin/_/de yang ci'i phyir zhe na/_bshad pa/_sems can snod du bya ba'i phyir/_/don gang gi ched du sems can snod du bya zhe na/_bshad pa/_dam chos bsgrub par bya ba'i phyir/_/
[\[223b.3\]]ji ltar bden pa shes pas zhe na/_bshad pa/_gang phyir bden pa gnyis las ni/_/'jig rten rnam dag 'byung bar 'dod/_/gnyis kyis nub 'gyur de yi [#]phyir/_/de shes 'jig rten shes zhes bya/_/bden pa gnyis kyis ni 'jig rten 'khor bar yang dang yang du 'byung ste/_gang dang gang gis
[\[223b.4\]]'byung ba'i phyir ro/_/'gog pa dang lam gyi bden pa gnyis kyis ni nub par 'gyur te/_gang yin pa dang /_gang gis nub par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/de lta bas na de shes pa ni 'jig rten shes pa zhes bya ste/_'jig rten 'byung ba dang nub par 'gyur ba shes pa rab dang ldan pa'i phyir ro/_/de
[\[223b.5\]]dag zhi bya thob bya'i phyir/_/blo ldan bden pa rnams la sbyor/_/gang gis blo ldan bden shes phyir/_/'jig rten shes zhes nges par brjod/_/'dis ni 'jig rten shes pa nyid kyi [#]las bstan te/_/de la zhi bar bya ba ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung gi bden pa dag go/_/thob par bya ba ni 'gog

[\[224a.1\]]bshad pa dang /_/log par yang dag shes pa dang /_/brjod dang bcas pa 'thob pa dag_/'dir ni dgag par bstan pa yin/_/ston pa dang po la ni gtsug lag gi chos spong ba'i gang zag dgag par bstan to/_/gnyis pa la ni tshig 'bru sgra ji bzhin gyi don te dgongs

[\[228a.3\]]'dzin las bsams pa'i don/_/'byor pa nye bar skye bar 'gyur/_/dper na 'khor los sgyur ba'i 'byor pa khyim bdag rin po che las grub pa lta bu'o/_/btang snyoms kyis ni thams cad du/_/'di ni ji ltar 'dod bzhin gnas/_/rjes la thob dang mi rtog pa'i/_/gnas pas

[\[232a.1\]]'gal zhe na/_bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong dag 'du byed de dag thams cad ni sgyu ma lta bu skye zhing 'jig pa/_dus re zhig pa/_yun thung ngur gnas pa'o zhes gsungs pa gang yin pa'i lung dang yang 'gal lo/_/rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi yid la

[\[241b.2\]]byed cing /_/bslab las nyams la smod pa dang /_/phun sum tshogs pa bsngags pa nyid/_/gdams ngag sbyin par byed pa dang /_/bdud rnams sbron par byed pa ste/_/las lnga dag gis rgyal sras rnams/_/sems can rtsa lag 'dra ba yin/_/rtsa lag dag ni rtsa lag rnams la phan pa rnam
[\[241b.3\]]pa lnga byed de/_gsang bar bya ba gsang bar byed/_spyod pa ngan pa la smod par byed/_spyod pa bzang po la bsngags par byed/_bya ba rnams la grogs kyi ngo bor 'gro bar byed/_nyam nga ba'i gnas dag las zlog par byed do/_/byang chub sems dpa'i rnams kyi las lnga po 'di dag kyang
[\[241b.4\]]de dang chos mthun par rig par bya ste/_'os pa ma yin pa dag la zab mo bshad pa [#]gsang ba'i phyir dang /_bslab pa nyams pa dang /_phun sum tshogs pa dag la go rims bzhin du smod pa dang bsngags pa'i phyir dang /_rtogs par bya ba'i ched du 'doms pa'i phyir dang /_bdud

[\[241b.6\]]rnams/_/sems can grogs po 'dra ba yin/_/grogs po'i phan pa dang bde ba la [#]phyin ci mi log pa dang /_bde ba dang phan pa nye bar sgrub pa dang /_mi phyed par 'gyur ba dang /_rtag tu phan pa dang bde ba 'dod pa gang yin pa de ni grogs po yin te/_de bzhin du byang chub sems

[\[242a.6\]]po 'di dag kyang de dang chos mthun par rig par bya'o/_/sems can don la shin tu brtson/_/tshogs rnams rdzogs par byed pa dang /_/tshogs bsags myur du grol bar byed/_/mi mthun phyogs ni spong byed cing /_/'jig rten 'jig rten ma yin pa'i/_/phun sum sna tshogs

[\[243b.1\]]can rnams kyi mi mthun phyogs/_/rnam pa drug ni 'dul bar byed/_/pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs ni rnam pa drug ste/_ser sna dang /_'chal ba'i tshul khrims dang /_khong [#]khro ba dang /_le lo dang /_rnam par g.yeng ba dang /_'chal ba'i shes rab dag dang /_go

[\[244a.1\]]pa rtsa ba drug pa ste/_blo ldan rnam pa thams cad du/_/phun tshogs skye dang mi skyo dang /_/rtag tu sgom par byed pa dang /_/ting [#]'dzin nyams pa med pa dang /_/bya ba grub [#]dang lhun grub pa'i/_/bzod pa 'thob [#]la nges par 'gyur/_/pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi dbang du byas

[\[245b.1\]]pa yongs su tshol ba'o/_/de la dngos po la ming glo bur ba nyid du yongs su tshol ba ni ming yongs su tshol ba yin par rig par bya'o/_/ming la dngos po glo bur ba nyid du yongs su tshol ba ni dngos po yongs su tshol ba yin par rig par bya'o/_/de gnyis 'brel ba la ngo bo nyid dang khyad

[\[246a.1\]]kun brtags pa gang yin pa'o/_/bdag nyid 'dug pa ni rang bzhin gyis dmigs par 'gyur gyi/_'bad pas kun brtags pa ma yin pa gang yin pa'o/_/de rnam par 'jig pa ni 'bral ba ste/_dmigs pa med pa'i ngo bo'o/_/de'i thabs ni mtshan ma'i

[\[259b.7\]]mi byed pa'i phyir ro/_/mi gnas pa nyid ni rtogs pa chung ngu dang /[ (]dan ngon [,]ngan ngon [)]tsam la mi gnas pa'i phyir ro/_/mi g.yo ba [#]nyid ni/_/rnam par mi g.yeng ba'i phyir ro/_/spros [#]pa med pa nyid ni/_rnam par rtog pa'i spros pa thams cad kun tu mi spyod pa'i phyir
[\[260a\]]
[\[260a.1\]]ro/_/sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid rnam par dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa gnyis te/_dam pa'i don ni grub pa ste/_/sa kun las ni nges par byung /_/sems can kun gyi mchog tu gyur/_/sems can thams cad rnam grol mdzad/_/yon tan mi
[\[260a.2\]]zad mnyam med ldan/_/'jig rten dag dang dkyil 'khor na'ang /_/snang la lha dang mi rnams kyis/_/rnam pa kun tu mi mthong ngo /_/'dir ngo bo nyid dang /_rgyu dang /_'bras bu dang /_las dang ldan pa dang /_'jug pa'i don drug gis sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid
[\[260a.3\]]yongs su bstan te/_de la don dam pa grub pa ni/_de bzhin nyid rnam par dag pa ste/_de ni sangs rgyas rnams [#]kyi ngo bo nyid kyi sku'o/_/byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad las nges par byung ba nyid ni rgyu'o/_/sems can thams cad kyi mchog tu gyur pa nyid ni
[\[260a.4\]]'bras bu'o/_/sems can thams cad rnam par grol bar mdzad pa nyid ni las so/_/yon tan mi zad pa dang /_mnyam pa med pa dang ldan pa nyid ni ldan pa'o/_/'jig rten gyi khams sna tshogs su snang ba nyid ni/_sprul pa'i skus so/_/'khor gyi [# ]
[\[260a.5\]]dkyil 'khor rnams na'ang snang ba nyid ni/_longs spyod rdzogs pa'i skus so/_/rnam pa thams cad du mi snang ba nyid ni chos kyi skus te/_'jug pa'i rab tu dbye ba rnam pa gsum yin no/_/[#]theg pa chen po [#]mdo sde'i rgyan byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtogs pa rnam
[\[260a.6\]]par byang bas bshad pa las/_spyod pa dang mthar thug [#]pa'i skabs zhes bya ba ste/_le'u nyi shu rtsa gcig pa'o//_//theg pa chen po [#]mdo sde'i rgyan gyi bshad pa rdzogs so//_//rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya sing+ha dang /_zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de
[\[260a.7\]]dpal brtsegs la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//_//theg chen mdo sde kun gyi rgyan/_/bshad pa 'di'i gzhung tshad ni/_/sha [#]lo ka sum stong dag dang rtsa/_/drug brgya lnga bcu yin par bsgrags//_//[ #]
